  96 // We generally try to create the oops directly when parsing, rather than
  97 // allocating temporary data structures and copying the bytes twice. A
  98 // temporary area is only needed when parsing utf8 entries in the constant
  99 // pool and when parsing line number tables.
 100 
 101 // We add assert in debug mode when class format is not checked.
 102 
 103 #define JAVA_CLASSFILE_MAGIC              0xCAFEBABE
 104 #define JAVA_MIN_SUPPORTED_VERSION        45
 105 #define JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION        65535
 106 
 107 // Used for two backward compatibility reasons:
 108 // - to check for new additions to the class file format in JDK1.5
 109 // - to check for bug fixes in the format checker in JDK1.5
 110 #define JAVA_1_5_VERSION                  49
 111 
 112 // Used for backward compatibility reasons:
 113 // - to check for javac bug fixes that happened after 1.5
 114 // - also used as the max version when running in jdk6
 115 #define JAVA_6_VERSION                    50
 116 
 117 // Used for backward compatibility reasons:
 118 // - to disallow argument and require ACC_STATIC for <clinit> methods
 119 #define JAVA_7_VERSION                    51
 120 
 121 // Extension method support.
 122 #define JAVA_8_VERSION                    52
 123 
 124 #define JAVA_9_VERSION                    53
 125 
 126 #define JAVA_10_VERSION                   54
 127 
 128 #define JAVA_11_VERSION                   55
 129 
 130 #define JAVA_12_VERSION                   56
 131 
 132 #define JAVA_13_VERSION                   57
 133 
 134 #define JAVA_14_VERSION                   58
 135 
 136 #define JAVA_15_VERSION                   59
 137 
 138 #define CONSTANT_CLASS_DESCRIPTORS        59
 139 
 140 void ClassFileParser::set_class_bad_constant_seen(short bad_constant) {
 141   assert((bad_constant == JVM_CONSTANT_Module ||
 142           bad_constant == JVM_CONSTANT_Package) && _major_version >= JAVA_9_VERSION,
 143          "Unexpected bad constant pool entry");
 144   if (_bad_constant_seen == 0) _bad_constant_seen = bad_constant;
 145 }
 146 
 147 void ClassFileParser::parse_constant_pool_entries(const ClassFileStream* const stream,
 148                                                   ConstantPool* cp,
 149                                                   const int length,
 150                                                   TRAPS) {
 151   assert(stream != NULL, "invariant");
 152   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
 153 
 154   // Use a local copy of ClassFileStream. It helps the C++ compiler to optimize
 155   // this function (_current can be allocated in a register, with scalar
 156   // replacement of aggregates). The _current pointer is copied back to
 157   // stream() when this function returns. DON'T call another method within
 158   // this method that uses stream().
 159   const ClassFileStream cfs1 = *stream;
 160   const ClassFileStream* const cfs = &cfs1;
 161 
 162   assert(cfs->allocated_on_stack(), "should be local");
 163   debug_only(const u1* const old_current = stream->current();)
 164 
 165   // Used for batching symbol allocations.
 166   const char* names[SymbolTable::symbol_alloc_batch_size];
 167   int lengths[SymbolTable::symbol_alloc_batch_size];
 168   int indices[SymbolTable::symbol_alloc_batch_size];
 169   unsigned int hashValues[SymbolTable::symbol_alloc_batch_size];
 170   int names_count = 0;
 171 
 172   // parsing  Index 0 is unused
 173   for (int index = 1; index < length; index++) {
 174     // Each of the following case guarantees one more byte in the stream
 175     // for the following tag or the access_flags following constant pool,
 176     // so we don't need bounds-check for reading tag.
 177     const u1 tag = cfs->get_u1_fast();
 178     switch (tag) {
 179       case JVM_CONSTANT_Class: {
 180         cfs->guarantee_more(3, CHECK);  // name_index, tag/access_flags
 181         const u2 name_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
 182         cp->klass_index_at_put(index, name_index);
 183         break;
 184       }
 185       case JVM_CONSTANT_Fieldref: {
 186         cfs->guarantee_more(5, CHECK);  // class_index, name_and_type_index, tag/access_flags
 187         const u2 class_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
 188         const u2 name_and_type_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
 189         cp->field_at_put(index, class_index, name_and_type_index);
 190         break;
 191       }
 192       case JVM_CONSTANT_Methodref: {
 193         cfs->guarantee_more(5, CHECK);  // class_index, name_and_type_index, tag/access_flags
 194         const u2 class_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
 195         const u2 name_and_type_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
 196         cp->method_at_put(index, class_index, name_and_type_index);
 197         break;
 198       }
 199       case JVM_CONSTANT_InterfaceMethodref: {
 200         cfs->guarantee_more(5, CHECK);  // class_index, name_and_type_index, tag/access_flags
 201         const u2 class_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
 202         const u2 name_and_type_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
 203         cp->interface_method_at_put(index, class_index, name_and_type_index);
 204         break;
 205       }
 206       case JVM_CONSTANT_String : {
 207         cfs->guarantee_more(3, CHECK);  // string_index, tag/access_flags
 208         const u2 string_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
 209         cp->string_index_at_put(index, string_index);
 210         break;
 211       }
 212       case JVM_CONSTANT_MethodHandle :
 213       case JVM_CONSTANT_MethodType: {
 214         if (_major_version < Verifier::INVOKEDYNAMIC_MAJOR_VERSION) {
 215           classfile_parse_error(
 216             "Class file version does not support constant tag %u in class file %s",
 217             tag, CHECK);
 218         }
 219         if (tag == JVM_CONSTANT_MethodHandle) {
 220           cfs->guarantee_more(4, CHECK);  // ref_kind, method_index, tag/access_flags
 221           const u1 ref_kind = cfs->get_u1_fast();
 222           const u2 method_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
 223           cp->method_handle_index_at_put(index, ref_kind, method_index);
 224         }
 225         else if (tag == JVM_CONSTANT_MethodType) {
 226           cfs->guarantee_more(3, CHECK);  // signature_index, tag/access_flags
 227           const u2 signature_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
 228           cp->method_type_index_at_put(index, signature_index);
 229         }
 230         else {
 231           ShouldNotReachHere();
 232         }
 233         break;
 234       }
 235       case JVM_CONSTANT_Dynamic : {
 236         if (_major_version < Verifier::DYNAMICCONSTANT_MAJOR_VERSION) {
 237           classfile_parse_error(
 238               "Class file version does not support constant tag %u in class file %s",
 239               tag, CHECK);
 240         }
 241         cfs->guarantee_more(5, CHECK);  // bsm_index, nt, tag/access_flags
 242         const u2 bootstrap_specifier_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
 243         const u2 name_and_type_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
 244         if (_max_bootstrap_specifier_index < (int) bootstrap_specifier_index) {
 245           _max_bootstrap_specifier_index = (int) bootstrap_specifier_index;  // collect for later
 246         }
 247         cp->dynamic_constant_at_put(index, bootstrap_specifier_index, name_and_type_index);
 248         break;
 249       }
 250       case JVM_CONSTANT_InvokeDynamic : {
 251         if (_major_version < Verifier::INVOKEDYNAMIC_MAJOR_VERSION) {
 252           classfile_parse_error(
 253               "Class file version does not support constant tag %u in class file %s",
 254               tag, CHECK);
 255         }
 256         cfs->guarantee_more(5, CHECK);  // bsm_index, nt, tag/access_flags
 257         const u2 bootstrap_specifier_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
 258         const u2 name_and_type_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
 259         if (_max_bootstrap_specifier_index < (int) bootstrap_specifier_index) {
 260           _max_bootstrap_specifier_index = (int) bootstrap_specifier_index;  // collect for later
 261         }
 262         cp->invoke_dynamic_at_put(index, bootstrap_specifier_index, name_and_type_index);
 263         break;
 264       }
 265       case JVM_CONSTANT_Integer: {
 266         cfs->guarantee_more(5, CHECK);  // bytes, tag/access_flags
 267         const u4 bytes = cfs->get_u4_fast();
 268         cp->int_at_put(index, (jint)bytes);
 269         break;
 270       }
 271       case JVM_CONSTANT_Float: {
 272         cfs->guarantee_more(5, CHECK);  // bytes, tag/access_flags
 273         const u4 bytes = cfs->get_u4_fast();
 274         cp->float_at_put(index, *(jfloat*)&bytes);
 275         break;
 276       }
 277       case JVM_CONSTANT_Long: {
 278         // A mangled type might cause you to overrun allocated memory
 279         guarantee_property(index + 1 < length,
 280                            "Invalid constant pool entry %u in class file %s",
 281                            index,
 282                            CHECK);
 283         cfs->guarantee_more(9, CHECK);  // bytes, tag/access_flags
 284         const u8 bytes = cfs->get_u8_fast();
 285         cp->long_at_put(index, bytes);
 286         index++;   // Skip entry following eigth-byte constant, see JVM book p. 98
 287         break;
 288       }
 289       case JVM_CONSTANT_Double: {
 290         // A mangled type might cause you to overrun allocated memory
 291         guarantee_property(index+1 < length,
 292                            "Invalid constant pool entry %u in class file %s",
 293                            index,
 294                            CHECK);
 295         cfs->guarantee_more(9, CHECK);  // bytes, tag/access_flags
 296         const u8 bytes = cfs->get_u8_fast();
 297         cp->double_at_put(index, *(jdouble*)&bytes);
 298         index++;   // Skip entry following eigth-byte constant, see JVM book p. 98
 299         break;
 300       }
 301       case JVM_CONSTANT_NameAndType: {
 302         cfs->guarantee_more(5, CHECK);  // name_index, signature_index, tag/access_flags
 303         const u2 name_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
 304         const u2 signature_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
 305         cp->name_and_type_at_put(index, name_index, signature_index);
 306         break;
 307       }
 308       case JVM_CONSTANT_Utf8 : {
 309         cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK);  // utf8_length
 310         u2  utf8_length = cfs->get_u2_fast();
 311         const u1* utf8_buffer = cfs->current();
 312         assert(utf8_buffer != NULL, "null utf8 buffer");
 313         // Got utf8 string, guarantee utf8_length+1 bytes, set stream position forward.
 314         cfs->guarantee_more(utf8_length+1, CHECK);  // utf8 string, tag/access_flags
 315         cfs->skip_u1_fast(utf8_length);
 316 
 317         // Before storing the symbol, make sure it's legal
 318         if (_need_verify) {
 319           verify_legal_utf8(utf8_buffer, utf8_length, CHECK);
 320         }
 321 
 322         if (has_cp_patch_at(index)) {
 323           Handle patch = clear_cp_patch_at(index);
 324           guarantee_property(java_lang_String::is_instance(patch()),
 325                              "Illegal utf8 patch at %d in class file %s",
 326                              index,
 327                              CHECK);
 328           const char* const str = java_lang_String::as_utf8_string(patch());
 329           // (could use java_lang_String::as_symbol instead, but might as well batch them)
 330           utf8_buffer = (const u1*) str;
 331           utf8_length = (u2) strlen(str);
 332         }
 333 
 334         unsigned int hash;
 335         Symbol* const result = SymbolTable::lookup_only((const char*)utf8_buffer,
 336                                                         utf8_length,
 337                                                         hash);
 338         if (result == NULL) {
 339           names[names_count] = (const char*)utf8_buffer;
 340           lengths[names_count] = utf8_length;
 341           indices[names_count] = index;
 342           hashValues[names_count++] = hash;
 343           if (names_count == SymbolTable::symbol_alloc_batch_size) {
 344             SymbolTable::new_symbols(_loader_data,
 345                                      constantPoolHandle(THREAD, cp),
 346                                      names_count,
 347                                      names,
 348                                      lengths,
 349                                      indices,
 350                                      hashValues);
 351             names_count = 0;
 352           }
 353         } else {
 354           cp->symbol_at_put(index, result);
 355         }
 356         break;
 357       }
 358       case JVM_CONSTANT_Module:
 359       case JVM_CONSTANT_Package: {
 360         // Record that an error occurred in these two cases but keep parsing so
 361         // that ACC_Module can be checked for in the access_flags.  Need to
 362         // throw NoClassDefFoundError in that case.
 363         if (_major_version >= JAVA_9_VERSION) {
 364           cfs->guarantee_more(3, CHECK);
 365           cfs->get_u2_fast();
 366           set_class_bad_constant_seen(tag);
 367           break;
 368         }
 369       }
 370       default: {
 371         classfile_parse_error("Unknown constant tag %u in class file %s",
 372                               tag,
 373                               CHECK);
 374         break;
 375       }
 376     } // end of switch(tag)
 377   } // end of for
 378 
 379   // Allocate the remaining symbols
 380   if (names_count > 0) {
 381     SymbolTable::new_symbols(_loader_data,
 382                              constantPoolHandle(THREAD, cp),
 383                              names_count,
 384                              names,
 385                              lengths,
 386                              indices,
 387                              hashValues);
 388   }
 389 
 390   // Copy _current pointer of local copy back to stream.
 391   assert(stream->current() == old_current, "non-exclusive use of stream");
 392   stream->set_current(cfs1.current());
 393 
 394 }
 395 
 396 static inline bool valid_cp_range(int index, int length) {
 397   return (index > 0 && index < length);
 398 }
 399 
 400 static inline Symbol* check_symbol_at(const ConstantPool* cp, int index) {
 401   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
 402   if (valid_cp_range(index, cp->length()) && cp->tag_at(index).is_utf8()) {
 403     return cp->symbol_at(index);
 404   }
 405   return NULL;
 406 }
 407 
 408 #ifdef ASSERT
 409 PRAGMA_DIAG_PUSH
 410 PRAGMA_FORMAT_NONLITERAL_IGNORED
 411 void ClassFileParser::report_assert_property_failure(const char* msg, TRAPS) const {
 412   ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
 413   fatal(msg, _class_name->as_C_string());
 414 }
 415 
 416 void ClassFileParser::report_assert_property_failure(const char* msg,
 417                                                      int index,
 418                                                      TRAPS) const {
 419   ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
 420   fatal(msg, index, _class_name->as_C_string());
 421 }
 422 PRAGMA_DIAG_POP
 423 #endif
 424 
 425 void ClassFileParser::parse_constant_pool(const ClassFileStream* const stream,
 426                                          ConstantPool* const cp,
 427                                          const int length,
 428                                          TRAPS) {
 429   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
 430   assert(stream != NULL, "invariant");
 431 
 432   // parsing constant pool entries
 433   parse_constant_pool_entries(stream, cp, length, CHECK);
 434   if (class_bad_constant_seen() != 0) {
 435     // a bad CP entry has been detected previously so stop parsing and just return.
 436     return;
 437   }
 438 
 439   int index = 1;  // declared outside of loops for portability
 440   int num_klasses = 0;
 441 
 442   // first verification pass - validate cross references
 443   // and fixup class and string constants
 444   for (index = 1; index < length; index++) {          // Index 0 is unused
 445     const jbyte tag = cp->tag_at(index).value();
 446     switch (tag) {
 447       case JVM_CONSTANT_Class: {
 448         ShouldNotReachHere();     // Only JVM_CONSTANT_ClassIndex should be present
 449         break;
 450       }
 451       case JVM_CONSTANT_Fieldref:
 452         // fall through
 453       case JVM_CONSTANT_Methodref:
 454         // fall through
 455       case JVM_CONSTANT_InterfaceMethodref: {
 456         if (!_need_verify) break;
 457         const int klass_ref_index = cp->klass_ref_index_at(index);
 458         const int name_and_type_ref_index = cp->name_and_type_ref_index_at(index);
 459         check_property(valid_klass_reference_at(klass_ref_index),
 460                        "Invalid constant pool index %u in class file %s",
 461                        klass_ref_index, CHECK);
 462         check_property(valid_cp_range(name_and_type_ref_index, length) &&
 463           cp->tag_at(name_and_type_ref_index).is_name_and_type(),
 464           "Invalid constant pool index %u in class file %s",
 465           name_and_type_ref_index, CHECK);
 466         break;
 467       }
 468       case JVM_CONSTANT_String: {
 469         ShouldNotReachHere();     // Only JVM_CONSTANT_StringIndex should be present
 470         break;
 471       }
 472       case JVM_CONSTANT_Integer:
 473         break;
 474       case JVM_CONSTANT_Float:
 475         break;
 476       case JVM_CONSTANT_Long:
 477       case JVM_CONSTANT_Double: {
 478         index++;
 479         check_property(
 480           (index < length && cp->tag_at(index).is_invalid()),
 481           "Improper constant pool long/double index %u in class file %s",
 482           index, CHECK);
 483         break;
 484       }
 485       case JVM_CONSTANT_NameAndType: {
 486         if (!_need_verify) break;
 487         const int name_ref_index = cp->name_ref_index_at(index);
 488         const int signature_ref_index = cp->signature_ref_index_at(index);
 489         check_property(valid_symbol_at(name_ref_index),
 490           "Invalid constant pool index %u in class file %s",
 491           name_ref_index, CHECK);
 492         check_property(valid_symbol_at(signature_ref_index),
 493           "Invalid constant pool index %u in class file %s",
 494           signature_ref_index, CHECK);
 495         break;
 496       }
 497       case JVM_CONSTANT_Utf8:
 498         break;
 499       case JVM_CONSTANT_UnresolvedClass:         // fall-through
 500       case JVM_CONSTANT_UnresolvedClassInError: {
 501         ShouldNotReachHere();     // Only JVM_CONSTANT_ClassIndex should be present
 502         break;
 503       }
 504       case JVM_CONSTANT_ClassIndex: {
 505         const int class_index = cp->klass_index_at(index);
 506         check_property(valid_symbol_at(class_index),
 507           "Invalid constant pool index %u in class file %s",
 508           class_index, CHECK);
 509 
 510         Symbol* const name = cp->symbol_at(class_index);
 511         const unsigned int name_len = name->utf8_length();
 512         if (name->is_Q_signature()) {
 513           cp->unresolved_qdescriptor_at_put(index, class_index, num_klasses++);
 514         } else {
 515           cp->unresolved_klass_at_put(index, class_index, num_klasses++);
 516         }
 517         break;
 518       }
 519       case JVM_CONSTANT_StringIndex: {
 520         const int string_index = cp->string_index_at(index);
 521         check_property(valid_symbol_at(string_index),
 522           "Invalid constant pool index %u in class file %s",
 523           string_index, CHECK);
 524         Symbol* const sym = cp->symbol_at(string_index);
 525         cp->unresolved_string_at_put(index, sym);
 526         break;
 527       }
 528       case JVM_CONSTANT_MethodHandle: {
 529         const int ref_index = cp->method_handle_index_at(index);
 530         check_property(valid_cp_range(ref_index, length),
 531           "Invalid constant pool index %u in class file %s",
 532           ref_index, CHECK);
 533         const constantTag tag = cp->tag_at(ref_index);
 534         const int ref_kind = cp->method_handle_ref_kind_at(index);
 535 
 536         switch (ref_kind) {
 537           case JVM_REF_getField:
 538           case JVM_REF_getStatic:
 539           case JVM_REF_putField:
 540           case JVM_REF_putStatic: {
 541             check_property(
 542               tag.is_field(),
 543               "Invalid constant pool index %u in class file %s (not a field)",
 544               ref_index, CHECK);
 545             break;
 546           }
 547           case JVM_REF_invokeVirtual:
 548           case JVM_REF_newInvokeSpecial: {
 549             check_property(
 550               tag.is_method(),
 551               "Invalid constant pool index %u in class file %s (not a method)",
 552               ref_index, CHECK);
 553             break;
 554           }
 555           case JVM_REF_invokeStatic:
 556           case JVM_REF_invokeSpecial: {
 557             check_property(
 558               tag.is_method() ||
 559               ((_major_version >= JAVA_8_VERSION) && tag.is_interface_method()),
 560               "Invalid constant pool index %u in class file %s (not a method)",
 561               ref_index, CHECK);
 562             break;
 563           }
 564           case JVM_REF_invokeInterface: {
 565             check_property(
 566               tag.is_interface_method(),
 567               "Invalid constant pool index %u in class file %s (not an interface method)",
 568               ref_index, CHECK);
 569             break;
 570           }
 571           default: {
 572             classfile_parse_error(
 573               "Bad method handle kind at constant pool index %u in class file %s",
 574               index, CHECK);
 575           }
 576         } // switch(refkind)
 577         // Keep the ref_index unchanged.  It will be indirected at link-time.
 578         break;
 579       } // case MethodHandle
 580       case JVM_CONSTANT_MethodType: {
 581         const int ref_index = cp->method_type_index_at(index);
 582         check_property(valid_symbol_at(ref_index),
 583           "Invalid constant pool index %u in class file %s",
 584           ref_index, CHECK);
 585         break;
 586       }
 587       case JVM_CONSTANT_Dynamic: {
 588         const int name_and_type_ref_index =
 589           cp->bootstrap_name_and_type_ref_index_at(index);
 590 
 591         check_property(valid_cp_range(name_and_type_ref_index, length) &&
 592           cp->tag_at(name_and_type_ref_index).is_name_and_type(),
 593           "Invalid constant pool index %u in class file %s",
 594           name_and_type_ref_index, CHECK);
 595         // bootstrap specifier index must be checked later,
 596         // when BootstrapMethods attr is available
 597 
 598         // Mark the constant pool as having a CONSTANT_Dynamic_info structure
 599         cp->set_has_dynamic_constant();
 600         break;
 601       }
 602       case JVM_CONSTANT_InvokeDynamic: {
 603         const int name_and_type_ref_index =
 604           cp->bootstrap_name_and_type_ref_index_at(index);
 605 
 606         check_property(valid_cp_range(name_and_type_ref_index, length) &&
 607           cp->tag_at(name_and_type_ref_index).is_name_and_type(),
 608           "Invalid constant pool index %u in class file %s",
 609           name_and_type_ref_index, CHECK);
 610         // bootstrap specifier index must be checked later,
 611         // when BootstrapMethods attr is available
 612         break;
 613       }
 614       default: {
 615         fatal("bad constant pool tag value %u", cp->tag_at(index).value());
 616         ShouldNotReachHere();
 617         break;
 618       }
 619     } // switch(tag)
 620   } // end of for
 621 
 622   _first_patched_klass_resolved_index = num_klasses;
 623   cp->allocate_resolved_klasses(_loader_data, num_klasses + _max_num_patched_klasses, CHECK);
 624 
 625   if (_cp_patches != NULL) {
 626     // need to treat this_class specially...
 627 
 628     // Add dummy utf8 entries in the space reserved for names of patched classes. We'll use "*"
 629     // for now. These will be replaced with actual names of the patched classes in patch_class().
 630     Symbol* s = vmSymbols::star_name();
 631     for (int n=_orig_cp_size; n<cp->length(); n++) {
 632       cp->symbol_at_put(n, s);
 633     }
 634 
 635     int this_class_index;
 636     {
 637       stream->guarantee_more(8, CHECK);  // flags, this_class, super_class, infs_len
 638       const u1* const mark = stream->current();
 639       stream->skip_u2_fast(1); // skip flags
 640       this_class_index = stream->get_u2_fast();
 641       stream->set_current(mark);  // revert to mark
 642     }
 643 
 644     for (index = 1; index < length; index++) {          // Index 0 is unused
 645       if (has_cp_patch_at(index)) {
 646         guarantee_property(index != this_class_index,
 647           "Illegal constant pool patch to self at %d in class file %s",
 648           index, CHECK);
 649         patch_constant_pool(cp, index, cp_patch_at(index), CHECK);
 650       }
 651     }
 652   }
 653 
 654   if (!_need_verify) {
 655     return;
 656   }
 657 
 658   // second verification pass - checks the strings are of the right format.
 659   // but not yet to the other entries
 660   for (index = 1; index < length; index++) {
 661     const jbyte tag = cp->tag_at(index).value();
 662     switch (tag) {
 663       case JVM_CONSTANT_UnresolvedClass: {
 664         const Symbol* const class_name = cp->klass_name_at(index);
 665         // check the name, even if _cp_patches will overwrite it
 666         verify_legal_class_name(class_name, CHECK);
 667         break;
 668       }
 669       case JVM_CONSTANT_NameAndType: {
 670         if (_need_verify) {
 671           const int sig_index = cp->signature_ref_index_at(index);
 672           const int name_index = cp->name_ref_index_at(index);
 673           const Symbol* const name = cp->symbol_at(name_index);
 674           const Symbol* const sig = cp->symbol_at(sig_index);
 675           guarantee_property(sig->utf8_length() != 0,
 676             "Illegal zero length constant pool entry at %d in class %s",
 677             sig_index, CHECK);
 678           guarantee_property(name->utf8_length() != 0,
 679             "Illegal zero length constant pool entry at %d in class %s",
 680             name_index, CHECK);
 681 
 682           if (Signature::is_method(sig)) {
 683             // Format check method name and signature
 684             verify_legal_method_name(name, CHECK);
 685             verify_legal_method_signature(name, sig, CHECK);
 686           } else {
 687             // Format check field name and signature
 688             verify_legal_field_name(name, CHECK);
 689             verify_legal_field_signature(name, sig, CHECK);
 690           }
 691         }
 692         break;
 693       }
 694       case JVM_CONSTANT_Dynamic: {
 695         const int name_and_type_ref_index =
 696           cp->name_and_type_ref_index_at(index);
 697         // already verified to be utf8
 698         const int name_ref_index =
 699           cp->name_ref_index_at(name_and_type_ref_index);
 700         // already verified to be utf8
 701         const int signature_ref_index =
 702           cp->signature_ref_index_at(name_and_type_ref_index);
 703         const Symbol* const name = cp->symbol_at(name_ref_index);
 704         const Symbol* const signature = cp->symbol_at(signature_ref_index);
 705         if (_need_verify) {
 706           // CONSTANT_Dynamic's name and signature are verified above, when iterating NameAndType_info.
 707           // Need only to be sure signature is the right type.
 708           if (Signature::is_method(signature)) {
 709             throwIllegalSignature("CONSTANT_Dynamic", name, signature, CHECK);
 710           }
 711         }
 712         break;
 713       }
 714       case JVM_CONSTANT_InvokeDynamic:
 715       case JVM_CONSTANT_Fieldref:
 716       case JVM_CONSTANT_Methodref:
 717       case JVM_CONSTANT_InterfaceMethodref: {
 718         const int name_and_type_ref_index =
 719           cp->name_and_type_ref_index_at(index);
 720         // already verified to be utf8
 721         const int name_ref_index =
 722           cp->name_ref_index_at(name_and_type_ref_index);
 723         // already verified to be utf8
 724         const int signature_ref_index =
 725           cp->signature_ref_index_at(name_and_type_ref_index);
 726         const Symbol* const name = cp->symbol_at(name_ref_index);
 727         const Symbol* const signature = cp->symbol_at(signature_ref_index);
 728         if (tag == JVM_CONSTANT_Fieldref) {
 729           if (_need_verify) {
 730             // Field name and signature are verified above, when iterating NameAndType_info.
 731             // Need only to be sure signature is non-zero length and the right type.
 732             if (Signature::is_method(signature)) {
 733               throwIllegalSignature("Field", name, signature, CHECK);
 734             }
 735           }
 736         } else {
 737           if (_need_verify) {
 738             // Method name and signature are verified above, when iterating NameAndType_info.
 739             // Need only to be sure signature is non-zero length and the right type.
 740             if (!Signature::is_method(signature)) {
 741               throwIllegalSignature("Method", name, signature, CHECK);
 742             }
 743           }
 744           // 4509014: If a class method name begins with '<', it must be "<init>"
 745           const unsigned int name_len = name->utf8_length();
 746           if (tag == JVM_CONSTANT_Methodref &&
 747               name_len != 0 &&
 748               name->char_at(0) == JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL &&
 749               name != vmSymbols::object_initializer_name()) {
 750             classfile_parse_error(
 751               "Bad method name at constant pool index %u in class file %s",
 752               name_ref_index, CHECK);
 753           }
 754         }
 755         break;
 756       }
 757       case JVM_CONSTANT_MethodHandle: {
 758         const int ref_index = cp->method_handle_index_at(index);
 759         const int ref_kind = cp->method_handle_ref_kind_at(index);
 760         switch (ref_kind) {
 761           case JVM_REF_invokeVirtual:
 762           case JVM_REF_invokeStatic:
 763           case JVM_REF_invokeSpecial:
 764           case JVM_REF_newInvokeSpecial: {
 765             const int name_and_type_ref_index =
 766               cp->name_and_type_ref_index_at(ref_index);
 767             const int name_ref_index =
 768               cp->name_ref_index_at(name_and_type_ref_index);
 769             const Symbol* const name = cp->symbol_at(name_ref_index);
 770             if (name != vmSymbols::object_initializer_name()) {
 771               if (ref_kind == JVM_REF_newInvokeSpecial) {
 772                 classfile_parse_error(
 773                   "Bad constructor name at constant pool index %u in class file %s",
 774                     name_ref_index, CHECK);
 775               }
 776             } else {
 777               // The allowed invocation mode of <init> depends on its signature.
 778               // This test corresponds to verify_invoke_instructions in the verifier.
 779               const int signature_ref_index =
 780                 cp->signature_ref_index_at(name_and_type_ref_index);
 781               const Symbol* const signature = cp->symbol_at(signature_ref_index);
 782               if (signature->is_void_method_signature()
 783                   && ref_kind == JVM_REF_newInvokeSpecial) {
 784                 // OK, could be a constructor call
 785               } else if (!signature->is_void_method_signature()
 786                          && ref_kind == JVM_REF_invokeStatic) {
 787                 // also OK, could be a static factory call
 788               } else {
 789                 classfile_parse_error(
 790                   "Bad method name at constant pool index %u in class file %s",
 791                   name_ref_index, CHECK);
 792               }
 793             }
 794             break;
 795           }
 796           // Other ref_kinds are already fully checked in previous pass.
 797         } // switch(ref_kind)
 798         break;
 799       }
 800       case JVM_CONSTANT_MethodType: {
 801         const Symbol* const no_name = vmSymbols::type_name(); // place holder
 802         const Symbol* const signature = cp->method_type_signature_at(index);
 803         verify_legal_method_signature(no_name, signature, CHECK);
 804         break;
 805       }
 806       case JVM_CONSTANT_Utf8: {
 807         assert(cp->symbol_at(index)->refcount() != 0, "count corrupted");
 808       }
 809     }  // switch(tag)
 810   }  // end of for
 811 }
 812 
 813 Handle ClassFileParser::clear_cp_patch_at(int index) {
 814   Handle patch = cp_patch_at(index);
 815   _cp_patches->at_put(index, Handle());
 816   assert(!has_cp_patch_at(index), "");
 817   return patch;
 818 }
 819 
 820 void ClassFileParser::patch_class(ConstantPool* cp, int class_index, Klass* k, Symbol* name) {
 821   int name_index = _orig_cp_size + _num_patched_klasses;
 822   int resolved_klass_index = _first_patched_klass_resolved_index + _num_patched_klasses;
 823 
 824   cp->klass_at_put(class_index, name_index, resolved_klass_index, k, name);
 825   _num_patched_klasses ++;
 826 }
 827 
 828 void ClassFileParser::patch_constant_pool(ConstantPool* cp,
 829                                           int index,
 830                                           Handle patch,
 831                                           TRAPS) {
 832   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
 833 
 834   BasicType patch_type = T_VOID;
 835 
 836   switch (cp->tag_at(index).value()) {
 837 
 838     case JVM_CONSTANT_UnresolvedClass: {
 839       // Patching a class means pre-resolving it.
 840       // The name in the constant pool is ignored.
 841       if (java_lang_Class::is_instance(patch())) {
 842         guarantee_property(!java_lang_Class::is_primitive(patch()),
 843                            "Illegal class patch at %d in class file %s",
 844                            index, CHECK);
 845         Klass* k = java_lang_Class::as_Klass(patch());
 846         patch_class(cp, index, k, k->name());
 847       } else {
 848         guarantee_property(java_lang_String::is_instance(patch()),
 849                            "Illegal class patch at %d in class file %s",
 850                            index, CHECK);
 851         Symbol* const name = java_lang_String::as_symbol(patch());
 852         patch_class(cp, index, NULL, name);
 853       }
 854       break;
 855     }
 856 
 857     case JVM_CONSTANT_String: {
 858       // skip this patch and don't clear it.  Needs the oop array for resolved
 859       // references to be created first.
 860       return;
 861     }
 862     case JVM_CONSTANT_Integer: patch_type = T_INT;    goto patch_prim;
 863     case JVM_CONSTANT_Float:   patch_type = T_FLOAT;  goto patch_prim;
 864     case JVM_CONSTANT_Long:    patch_type = T_LONG;   goto patch_prim;
 865     case JVM_CONSTANT_Double:  patch_type = T_DOUBLE; goto patch_prim;
 866     patch_prim:
 867     {
 868       jvalue value;
 869       BasicType value_type = java_lang_boxing_object::get_value(patch(), &value);
 870       guarantee_property(value_type == patch_type,
 871                          "Illegal primitive patch at %d in class file %s",
 872                          index, CHECK);
 873       switch (value_type) {
 874         case T_INT:    cp->int_at_put(index,   value.i); break;
 875         case T_FLOAT:  cp->float_at_put(index, value.f); break;
 876         case T_LONG:   cp->long_at_put(index,  value.j); break;
 877         case T_DOUBLE: cp->double_at_put(index, value.d); break;
 878         default:       assert(false, "");
 879       }
 880     } // end patch_prim label
 881     break;
 882 
 883     default: {
 884       // %%% TODO: put method handles into CONSTANT_InterfaceMethodref, etc.
 885       guarantee_property(!has_cp_patch_at(index),
 886                          "Illegal unexpected patch at %d in class file %s",
 887                          index, CHECK);
 888       return;
 889     }
 890   } // end of switch(tag)
 891 
 892   // On fall-through, mark the patch as used.
 893   clear_cp_patch_at(index);
 894 }
 895 class NameSigHash: public ResourceObj {
 896  public:
 897   const Symbol*       _name;       // name
 898   const Symbol*       _sig;        // signature
 899   NameSigHash*  _next;             // Next entry in hash table
 900 };
 901 
 902 static const int HASH_ROW_SIZE = 256;
 903 
 904 static unsigned int hash(const Symbol* name, const Symbol* sig) {
 905   unsigned int raw_hash = 0;
 906   raw_hash += ((unsigned int)(uintptr_t)name) >> (LogHeapWordSize + 2);
 907   raw_hash += ((unsigned int)(uintptr_t)sig) >> LogHeapWordSize;
 908 
 909   return (raw_hash + (unsigned int)(uintptr_t)name) % HASH_ROW_SIZE;
 910 }
 911 
 912 
 913 static void initialize_hashtable(NameSigHash** table) {
 914   memset((void*)table, 0, sizeof(NameSigHash*) * HASH_ROW_SIZE);
 915 }
 916 // Return false if the name/sig combination is found in table.
 917 // Return true if no duplicate is found. And name/sig is added as a new entry in table.
 918 // The old format checker uses heap sort to find duplicates.
 919 // NOTE: caller should guarantee that GC doesn't happen during the life cycle
 920 // of table since we don't expect Symbol*'s to move.
 921 static bool put_after_lookup(const Symbol* name, const Symbol* sig, NameSigHash** table) {
 922   assert(name != NULL, "name in constant pool is NULL");
 923 
 924   // First lookup for duplicates
 925   int index = hash(name, sig);
 926   NameSigHash* entry = table[index];
 927   while (entry != NULL) {
 928     if (entry->_name == name && entry->_sig == sig) {
 929       return false;
 930     }
 931     entry = entry->_next;
 932   }
 933 
 934   // No duplicate is found, allocate a new entry and fill it.
 935   entry = new NameSigHash();
 936   entry->_name = name;
 937   entry->_sig = sig;
 938 
 939   // Insert into hash table
 940   entry->_next = table[index];
 941   table[index] = entry;
 942 
 943   return true;
 944 }
 945 
 946 // Side-effects: populates the _local_interfaces field
 947 void ClassFileParser::parse_interfaces(const ClassFileStream* stream,
 948                                        int itfs_len,
 949                                        ConstantPool* cp,
 950                                        bool is_inline_type,
 951                                        bool* const has_nonstatic_concrete_methods,
 952                                        // FIXME: lots of these functions
 953                                        // declare their parameters as const,
 954                                        // which adds only noise to the code.
 955                                        // Remove the spurious const modifiers.
 956                                        // Many are of the form "const int x"
 957                                        // or "T* const x".
 958                                        bool* const is_declared_atomic,
 959                                        TRAPS) {
 960   assert(stream != NULL, "invariant");
 961   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
 962   assert(has_nonstatic_concrete_methods != NULL, "invariant");
 963 
 964   if (itfs_len == 0) {
 965     _local_interfaces = Universe::the_empty_instance_klass_array();
 966   } else {
 967     assert(itfs_len > 0, "only called for len>0");
 968     _local_interfaces = MetadataFactory::new_array<InstanceKlass*>(_loader_data, itfs_len, NULL, CHECK);
 969 
 970     int index;
 971     for (index = 0; index < itfs_len; index++) {
 972       const u2 interface_index = stream->get_u2(CHECK);
 973       Klass* interf;
 974       check_property(
 975         valid_klass_reference_at(interface_index),
 976         "Interface name has bad constant pool index %u in class file %s",
 977         interface_index, CHECK);
 978       if (cp->tag_at(interface_index).is_klass()) {
 979         interf = cp->resolved_klass_at(interface_index);
 980       } else {
 981         Symbol* const unresolved_klass  = cp->klass_name_at(interface_index);
 982 
 983         // Don't need to check legal name because it's checked when parsing constant pool.
 984         // But need to make sure it's not an array type.
 985         guarantee_property(unresolved_klass->char_at(0) != JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY,
 986                            "Bad interface name in class file %s", CHECK);
 987 
 988         // Call resolve_super so classcircularity is checked
 989         interf = SystemDictionary::resolve_super_or_fail(
 990                                                   _class_name,
 991                                                   unresolved_klass,
 992                                                   Handle(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader()),
 993                                                   _protection_domain,
 994                                                   false,
 995                                                   CHECK);
 996       }
 997 
 998       if (!interf->is_interface()) {
 999         THROW_MSG(vmSymbols::java_lang_IncompatibleClassChangeError(),
1000                   err_msg("class %s can not implement %s, because it is not an interface (%s)",
1001                           _class_name->as_klass_external_name(),
1002                           interf->external_name(),
1003                           interf->class_in_module_of_loader()));
1004       }
1005 
1006       InstanceKlass* ik = InstanceKlass::cast(interf);
1007       if (is_inline_type && ik->invalid_inline_super()) {
1008         ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
1009         Exceptions::fthrow(
1010           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
1011           vmSymbols::java_lang_IncompatibleClassChangeError(),
1012           "Inline type %s attempts to implement interface java.lang.IdentityObject",
1013           _class_name->as_klass_external_name());
1014         return;
1015       }
1016       if (ik->invalid_inline_super()) {
1017         set_invalid_inline_super();
1018       }
1019       if (ik->has_nonstatic_concrete_methods()) {
1020         *has_nonstatic_concrete_methods = true;
1021       }
1022       if (ik->is_declared_atomic()) {
1023         *is_declared_atomic = true;
1024       }
1025       _local_interfaces->at_put(index, ik);
1026     }
1027 
1028     if (!_need_verify || itfs_len <= 1) {
1029       return;
1030     }
1031 
1032     // Check if there's any duplicates in interfaces
1033     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
1034     NameSigHash** interface_names = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(THREAD,
1035                                                                  NameSigHash*,
1036                                                                  HASH_ROW_SIZE);
1037     initialize_hashtable(interface_names);
1038     bool dup = false;
1039     const Symbol* name = NULL;
1040     {
1041       debug_only(NoSafepointVerifier nsv;)
1042       for (index = 0; index < itfs_len; index++) {
1043         const InstanceKlass* const k = _local_interfaces->at(index);
1044         name = k->name();
1045         // If no duplicates, add (name, NULL) in hashtable interface_names.
1046         if (!put_after_lookup(name, NULL, interface_names)) {
1047           dup = true;
1048           break;
1049         }
1050       }
1051     }
1052     if (dup) {
1053       classfile_parse_error("Duplicate interface name \"%s\" in class file %s",
1054                              name->as_C_string(), CHECK);
1055     }
1056   }
1057 }
1058 
1059 void ClassFileParser::verify_constantvalue(const ConstantPool* const cp,
1060                                            int constantvalue_index,
1061                                            int signature_index,
1062                                            TRAPS) const {
1063   // Make sure the constant pool entry is of a type appropriate to this field
1064   guarantee_property(
1065     (constantvalue_index > 0 &&
1066       constantvalue_index < cp->length()),
1067     "Bad initial value index %u in ConstantValue attribute in class file %s",
1068     constantvalue_index, CHECK);
1069 
1070   const constantTag value_type = cp->tag_at(constantvalue_index);
1071   switch(cp->basic_type_for_signature_at(signature_index)) {
1072     case T_LONG: {
1073       guarantee_property(value_type.is_long(),
1074                          "Inconsistent constant value type in class file %s",
1075                          CHECK);
1076       break;
1077     }
1078     case T_FLOAT: {
1079       guarantee_property(value_type.is_float(),
1080                          "Inconsistent constant value type in class file %s",
1081                          CHECK);
1082       break;
1083     }
1084     case T_DOUBLE: {
1085       guarantee_property(value_type.is_double(),
1086                          "Inconsistent constant value type in class file %s",
1087                          CHECK);
1088       break;
1089     }
1090     case T_BYTE:
1091     case T_CHAR:
1092     case T_SHORT:
1093     case T_BOOLEAN:
1094     case T_INT: {
1095       guarantee_property(value_type.is_int(),
1096                          "Inconsistent constant value type in class file %s",
1097                          CHECK);
1098       break;
1099     }
1100     case T_OBJECT: {
1101       guarantee_property((cp->symbol_at(signature_index)->equals("Ljava/lang/String;")
1102                          && value_type.is_string()),
1103                          "Bad string initial value in class file %s",
1104                          CHECK);
1105       break;
1106     }
1107     default: {
1108       classfile_parse_error("Unable to set initial value %u in class file %s",
1109                              constantvalue_index,
1110                              CHECK);
1111     }
1112   }
1113 }
1114 
1115 class AnnotationCollector : public ResourceObj{
1116 public:
1117   enum Location { _in_field, _in_method, _in_class };
1118   enum ID {
1119     _unknown = 0,
1120     _method_CallerSensitive,
1121     _method_ForceInline,
1122     _method_DontInline,
1123     _method_InjectedProfile,
1124     _method_LambdaForm_Compiled,
1125     _method_Hidden,
1126     _method_HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate,
1127     _jdk_internal_vm_annotation_Contended,
1128     _field_Stable,
1129     _jdk_internal_vm_annotation_ReservedStackAccess,
1130     _annotation_LIMIT
1131   };
1132   const Location _location;
1133   int _annotations_present;
1134   u2 _contended_group;
1135 
1136   AnnotationCollector(Location location)
1137     : _location(location), _annotations_present(0)
1138   {
1139     assert((int)_annotation_LIMIT <= (int)sizeof(_annotations_present) * BitsPerByte, "");
1140   }
1141   // If this annotation name has an ID, report it (or _none).
1142   ID annotation_index(const ClassLoaderData* loader_data, const Symbol* name);
1143   // Set the annotation name:
1144   void set_annotation(ID id) {
1145     assert((int)id >= 0 && (int)id < (int)_annotation_LIMIT, "oob");
1146     _annotations_present |= nth_bit((int)id);
1147   }
1148 
1149   void remove_annotation(ID id) {
1150     assert((int)id >= 0 && (int)id < (int)_annotation_LIMIT, "oob");
1151     _annotations_present &= ~nth_bit((int)id);
1152   }
1153 
1154   // Report if the annotation is present.
1155   bool has_any_annotations() const { return _annotations_present != 0; }
1156   bool has_annotation(ID id) const { return (nth_bit((int)id) & _annotations_present) != 0; }
1157 
1158   void set_contended_group(u2 group) { _contended_group = group; }
1159   u2 contended_group() const { return _contended_group; }
1160 
1161   bool is_contended() const { return has_annotation(_jdk_internal_vm_annotation_Contended); }
1162 
1163   void set_stable(bool stable) { set_annotation(_field_Stable); }
1164   bool is_stable() const { return has_annotation(_field_Stable); }
1165 };
1166 
1167 // This class also doubles as a holder for metadata cleanup.
1168 class ClassFileParser::FieldAnnotationCollector : public AnnotationCollector {
1169 private:
1170   ClassLoaderData* _loader_data;
1171   AnnotationArray* _field_annotations;
1172   AnnotationArray* _field_type_annotations;
1173 public:
1174   FieldAnnotationCollector(ClassLoaderData* loader_data) :
1175     AnnotationCollector(_in_field),
1176     _loader_data(loader_data),
1177     _field_annotations(NULL),
1178     _field_type_annotations(NULL) {}
1179   ~FieldAnnotationCollector();
1180   void apply_to(FieldInfo* f);
1181   AnnotationArray* field_annotations()      { return _field_annotations; }
1182   AnnotationArray* field_type_annotations() { return _field_type_annotations; }
1183 
1184   void set_field_annotations(AnnotationArray* a)      { _field_annotations = a; }
1185   void set_field_type_annotations(AnnotationArray* a) { _field_type_annotations = a; }
1186 };

1199 
1200 
1201 static int skip_annotation_value(const u1*, int, int); // fwd decl
1202 
1203 // Safely increment index by val if does not pass limit
1204 #define SAFE_ADD(index, limit, val) \
1205 if (index >= limit - val) return limit; \
1206 index += val;
1207 
1208 // Skip an annotation.  Return >=limit if there is any problem.
1209 static int skip_annotation(const u1* buffer, int limit, int index) {
1210   assert(buffer != NULL, "invariant");
1211   // annotation := atype:u2 do(nmem:u2) {member:u2 value}
1212   // value := switch (tag:u1) { ... }
1213   SAFE_ADD(index, limit, 4); // skip atype and read nmem
1214   int nmem = Bytes::get_Java_u2((address)buffer + index - 2);
1215   while (--nmem >= 0 && index < limit) {
1216     SAFE_ADD(index, limit, 2); // skip member
1217     index = skip_annotation_value(buffer, limit, index);
1218   }
1219   return index;
1220 }
1221 
1222 // Skip an annotation value.  Return >=limit if there is any problem.
1223 static int skip_annotation_value(const u1* buffer, int limit, int index) {
1224   assert(buffer != NULL, "invariant");
1225 
1226   // value := switch (tag:u1) {
1227   //   case B, C, I, S, Z, D, F, J, c: con:u2;
1228   //   case e: e_class:u2 e_name:u2;
1229   //   case s: s_con:u2;
1230   //   case [: do(nval:u2) {value};
1231   //   case @: annotation;
1232   //   case s: s_con:u2;
1233   // }
1234   SAFE_ADD(index, limit, 1); // read tag
1235   const u1 tag = buffer[index - 1];
1236   switch (tag) {
1237     case 'B':
1238     case 'C':
1239     case 'I':
1240     case 'S':
1241     case 'Z':
1242     case 'D':
1243     case 'F':
1244     case 'J':
1245     case 'c':
1246     case 's':
1247       SAFE_ADD(index, limit, 2);  // skip con or s_con
1248       break;
1249     case 'e':
1250       SAFE_ADD(index, limit, 4);  // skip e_class, e_name
1251       break;
1252     case '[':
1253     {
1254       SAFE_ADD(index, limit, 2); // read nval
1255       int nval = Bytes::get_Java_u2((address)buffer + index - 2);
1256       while (--nval >= 0 && index < limit) {
1257         index = skip_annotation_value(buffer, limit, index);
1258       }
1259     }
1260     break;
1261     case '@':
1262       index = skip_annotation(buffer, limit, index);
1263       break;
1264     default:
1265       return limit;  //  bad tag byte
1266   }
1267   return index;
1268 }
1269 
1270 // Sift through annotations, looking for those significant to the VM:
1271 static void parse_annotations(const ConstantPool* const cp,
1272                               const u1* buffer, int limit,
1273                               AnnotationCollector* coll,
1274                               ClassLoaderData* loader_data,
1275                               TRAPS) {
1276 
1277   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
1278   assert(buffer != NULL, "invariant");
1279   assert(coll != NULL, "invariant");
1280   assert(loader_data != NULL, "invariant");
1281 
1282   // annotations := do(nann:u2) {annotation}
1283   int index = 2; // read nann
1284   if (index >= limit)  return;
1285   int nann = Bytes::get_Java_u2((address)buffer + index - 2);
1286   enum {  // initial annotation layout
1287     atype_off = 0,      // utf8 such as 'Ljava/lang/annotation/Retention;'
1288     count_off = 2,      // u2   such as 1 (one value)
1289     member_off = 4,     // utf8 such as 'value'
1290     tag_off = 6,        // u1   such as 'c' (type) or 'e' (enum)
1291     e_tag_val = 'e',
1292     e_type_off = 7,   // utf8 such as 'Ljava/lang/annotation/RetentionPolicy;'
1293     e_con_off = 9,    // utf8 payload, such as 'SOURCE', 'CLASS', 'RUNTIME'
1294     e_size = 11,     // end of 'e' annotation
1295     c_tag_val = 'c',    // payload is type
1296     c_con_off = 7,    // utf8 payload, such as 'I'
1297     c_size = 9,       // end of 'c' annotation
1298     s_tag_val = 's',    // payload is String
1299     s_con_off = 7,    // utf8 payload, such as 'Ljava/lang/String;'
1300     s_size = 9,
1301     min_size = 6        // smallest possible size (zero members)
1302   };
1303   // Cannot add min_size to index in case of overflow MAX_INT
1304   while ((--nann) >= 0 && (index - 2 <= limit - min_size)) {
1305     int index0 = index;
1306     index = skip_annotation(buffer, limit, index);
1307     const u1* const abase = buffer + index0;
1308     const int atype = Bytes::get_Java_u2((address)abase + atype_off);
1309     const int count = Bytes::get_Java_u2((address)abase + count_off);
1310     const Symbol* const aname = check_symbol_at(cp, atype);
1311     if (aname == NULL)  break;  // invalid annotation name
1312     const Symbol* member = NULL;
1313     if (count >= 1) {
1314       const int member_index = Bytes::get_Java_u2((address)abase + member_off);
1315       member = check_symbol_at(cp, member_index);
1316       if (member == NULL)  break;  // invalid member name
1317     }
1318 
1319     // Here is where parsing particular annotations will take place.
1320     AnnotationCollector::ID id = coll->annotation_index(loader_data, aname);
1321     if (AnnotationCollector::_unknown == id)  continue;
1322     coll->set_annotation(id);
1323 
1324     if (AnnotationCollector::_jdk_internal_vm_annotation_Contended == id) {
1325       // @Contended can optionally specify the contention group.
1326       //
1327       // Contended group defines the equivalence class over the fields:
1328       // the fields within the same contended group are not treated distinct.
1329       // The only exception is default group, which does not incur the
1330       // equivalence. Naturally, contention group for classes is meaningless.
1331       //
1332       // While the contention group is specified as String, annotation
1333       // values are already interned, and we might as well use the constant
1334       // pool index as the group tag.
1335       //
1336       u2 group_index = 0; // default contended group
1337       if (count == 1
1338         && s_size == (index - index0)  // match size
1339         && s_tag_val == *(abase + tag_off)
1340         && member == vmSymbols::value_name()) {
1341         group_index = Bytes::get_Java_u2((address)abase + s_con_off);
1342         if (cp->symbol_at(group_index)->utf8_length() == 0) {
1343           group_index = 0; // default contended group
1344         }
1345       }
1346       coll->set_contended_group(group_index);
1347     }
1348   }
1349 }
1350 
1351 
1352 // Parse attributes for a field.
1353 void ClassFileParser::parse_field_attributes(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
1354                                              u2 attributes_count,
1355                                              bool is_static, u2 signature_index,
1356                                              u2* const constantvalue_index_addr,
1357                                              bool* const is_synthetic_addr,
1358                                              u2* const generic_signature_index_addr,
1359                                              ClassFileParser::FieldAnnotationCollector* parsed_annotations,
1360                                              TRAPS) {
1361   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
1362   assert(constantvalue_index_addr != NULL, "invariant");
1363   assert(is_synthetic_addr != NULL, "invariant");
1364   assert(generic_signature_index_addr != NULL, "invariant");
1365   assert(parsed_annotations != NULL, "invariant");
1366   assert(attributes_count > 0, "attributes_count should be greater than 0");
1367 
1368   u2 constantvalue_index = 0;
1369   u2 generic_signature_index = 0;
1370   bool is_synthetic = false;
1371   const u1* runtime_visible_annotations = NULL;
1372   int runtime_visible_annotations_length = 0;
1373   const u1* runtime_invisible_annotations = NULL;
1374   int runtime_invisible_annotations_length = 0;
1375   const u1* runtime_visible_type_annotations = NULL;
1376   int runtime_visible_type_annotations_length = 0;
1377   const u1* runtime_invisible_type_annotations = NULL;
1378   int runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length = 0;
1379   bool runtime_invisible_annotations_exists = false;
1380   bool runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists = false;
1381   const ConstantPool* const cp = _cp;
1382 
1383   while (attributes_count--) {
1384     cfs->guarantee_more(6, CHECK);  // attribute_name_index, attribute_length
1385     const u2 attribute_name_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
1386     const u4 attribute_length = cfs->get_u4_fast();
1387     check_property(valid_symbol_at(attribute_name_index),
1388                    "Invalid field attribute index %u in class file %s",
1389                    attribute_name_index,
1390                    CHECK);
1391 
1392     const Symbol* const attribute_name = cp->symbol_at(attribute_name_index);
1393     if (is_static && attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_constant_value()) {
1394       // ignore if non-static
1395       if (constantvalue_index != 0) {
1396         classfile_parse_error("Duplicate ConstantValue attribute in class file %s", CHECK);
1397       }
1398       check_property(
1399         attribute_length == 2,
1400         "Invalid ConstantValue field attribute length %u in class file %s",
1401         attribute_length, CHECK);
1402 
1403       constantvalue_index = cfs->get_u2(CHECK);
1404       if (_need_verify) {
1405         verify_constantvalue(cp, constantvalue_index, signature_index, CHECK);
1406       }
1407     } else if (attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_synthetic()) {
1408       if (attribute_length != 0) {
1409         classfile_parse_error(
1410           "Invalid Synthetic field attribute length %u in class file %s",
1411           attribute_length, CHECK);
1412       }
1413       is_synthetic = true;
1414     } else if (attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_deprecated()) { // 4276120
1415       if (attribute_length != 0) {
1416         classfile_parse_error(
1417           "Invalid Deprecated field attribute length %u in class file %s",
1418           attribute_length, CHECK);
1419       }
1420     } else if (_major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
1421       if (attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_signature()) {
1422         if (generic_signature_index != 0) {
1423           classfile_parse_error(
1424             "Multiple Signature attributes for field in class file %s", CHECK);
1425         }
1426         if (attribute_length != 2) {
1427           classfile_parse_error(
1428             "Wrong size %u for field's Signature attribute in class file %s",
1429             attribute_length, CHECK);
1430         }
1431         generic_signature_index = parse_generic_signature_attribute(cfs, CHECK);
1432       } else if (attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_annotations()) {
1433         if (runtime_visible_annotations != NULL) {
1434           classfile_parse_error(
1435             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleAnnotations attributes for field in class file %s", CHECK);
1436         }
1437         runtime_visible_annotations_length = attribute_length;
1438         runtime_visible_annotations = cfs->current();
1439         assert(runtime_visible_annotations != NULL, "null visible annotations");
1440         cfs->guarantee_more(runtime_visible_annotations_length, CHECK);
1441         parse_annotations(cp,
1442                           runtime_visible_annotations,
1443                           runtime_visible_annotations_length,
1444                           parsed_annotations,
1445                           _loader_data,
1446                           CHECK);
1447         cfs->skip_u1_fast(runtime_visible_annotations_length);
1448       } else if (attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_annotations()) {
1449         if (runtime_invisible_annotations_exists) {
1450           classfile_parse_error(
1451             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleAnnotations attributes for field in class file %s", CHECK);
1452         }
1453         runtime_invisible_annotations_exists = true;
1454         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
1455           runtime_invisible_annotations_length = attribute_length;
1456           runtime_invisible_annotations = cfs->current();
1457           assert(runtime_invisible_annotations != NULL, "null invisible annotations");
1458         }
1459         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
1460       } else if (attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_type_annotations()) {
1461         if (runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL) {
1462           classfile_parse_error(
1463             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleTypeAnnotations attributes for field in class file %s", CHECK);
1464         }
1465         runtime_visible_type_annotations_length = attribute_length;
1466         runtime_visible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
1467         assert(runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL, "null visible type annotations");
1468         cfs->skip_u1(runtime_visible_type_annotations_length, CHECK);
1469       } else if (attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_type_annotations()) {
1470         if (runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists) {
1471           classfile_parse_error(
1472             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleTypeAnnotations attributes for field in class file %s", CHECK);
1473         } else {
1474           runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists = true;
1475         }
1476         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
1477           runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length = attribute_length;
1478           runtime_invisible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
1479           assert(runtime_invisible_type_annotations != NULL, "null invisible type annotations");
1480         }
1481         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
1482       } else {
1483         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);  // Skip unknown attributes
1484       }
1485     } else {
1486       cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);  // Skip unknown attributes
1487     }
1488   }
1489 
1490   *constantvalue_index_addr = constantvalue_index;
1491   *is_synthetic_addr = is_synthetic;
1492   *generic_signature_index_addr = generic_signature_index;
1493   AnnotationArray* a = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_annotations,
1494                                             runtime_visible_annotations_length,
1495                                             runtime_invisible_annotations,
1496                                             runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
1497                                             CHECK);
1498   parsed_annotations->set_field_annotations(a);
1499   a = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_type_annotations,
1500                            runtime_visible_type_annotations_length,
1501                            runtime_invisible_type_annotations,
1502                            runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length,
1503                            CHECK);
1504   parsed_annotations->set_field_type_annotations(a);
1505   return;
1506 }
1507 
1508 
1509 // Field allocation types. Used for computing field offsets.
1510 
1511 enum FieldAllocationType {
1512   STATIC_OOP,           // Oops
1513   STATIC_BYTE,          // Boolean, Byte, char
1514   STATIC_SHORT,         // shorts
1515   STATIC_WORD,          // ints
1516   STATIC_DOUBLE,        // aligned long or double
1517   STATIC_FLATTENABLE,   // flattenable field
1518   NONSTATIC_OOP,
1519   NONSTATIC_BYTE,
1520   NONSTATIC_SHORT,
1521   NONSTATIC_WORD,
1522   NONSTATIC_DOUBLE,
1523   NONSTATIC_FLATTENABLE,
1524   MAX_FIELD_ALLOCATION_TYPE,
1525   BAD_ALLOCATION_TYPE = -1
1526 };
1527 
1528 static FieldAllocationType _basic_type_to_atype[2 * (T_CONFLICT + 1)] = {
1529   BAD_ALLOCATION_TYPE, // 0
1530   BAD_ALLOCATION_TYPE, // 1
1531   BAD_ALLOCATION_TYPE, // 2
1532   BAD_ALLOCATION_TYPE, // 3
1533   NONSTATIC_BYTE ,     // T_BOOLEAN     =  4,
1534   NONSTATIC_SHORT,     // T_CHAR        =  5,
1535   NONSTATIC_WORD,      // T_FLOAT       =  6,
1536   NONSTATIC_DOUBLE,    // T_DOUBLE      =  7,
1537   NONSTATIC_BYTE,      // T_BYTE        =  8,
1538   NONSTATIC_SHORT,     // T_SHORT       =  9,
1539   NONSTATIC_WORD,      // T_INT         = 10,
1540   NONSTATIC_DOUBLE,    // T_LONG        = 11,
1541   NONSTATIC_OOP,       // T_OBJECT      = 12,
1542   NONSTATIC_OOP,       // T_ARRAY       = 13,
1543   NONSTATIC_OOP,       // T_VALUETYPE   = 14,
1544   BAD_ALLOCATION_TYPE, // T_VOID        = 15,
1545   BAD_ALLOCATION_TYPE, // T_ADDRESS     = 16,
1546   BAD_ALLOCATION_TYPE, // T_NARROWOOP   = 17,
1547   BAD_ALLOCATION_TYPE, // T_METADATA    = 18,
1548   BAD_ALLOCATION_TYPE, // T_NARROWKLASS = 19,
1549   BAD_ALLOCATION_TYPE, // T_CONFLICT    = 20,
1550   BAD_ALLOCATION_TYPE, // 0
1551   BAD_ALLOCATION_TYPE, // 1
1552   BAD_ALLOCATION_TYPE, // 2
1553   BAD_ALLOCATION_TYPE, // 3
1554   STATIC_BYTE ,        // T_BOOLEAN     =  4,
1555   STATIC_SHORT,        // T_CHAR        =  5,
1556   STATIC_WORD,         // T_FLOAT       =  6,
1557   STATIC_DOUBLE,       // T_DOUBLE      =  7,
1558   STATIC_BYTE,         // T_BYTE        =  8,
1559   STATIC_SHORT,        // T_SHORT       =  9,
1560   STATIC_WORD,         // T_INT         = 10,
1561   STATIC_DOUBLE,       // T_LONG        = 11,
1562   STATIC_OOP,          // T_OBJECT      = 12,
1563   STATIC_OOP,          // T_ARRAY       = 13,
1564   STATIC_OOP,          // T_VALUETYPE   = 14,
1565   BAD_ALLOCATION_TYPE, // T_VOID        = 15,
1566   BAD_ALLOCATION_TYPE, // T_ADDRESS     = 16,
1567   BAD_ALLOCATION_TYPE, // T_NARROWOOP   = 17,
1568   BAD_ALLOCATION_TYPE, // T_METADATA    = 18,
1569   BAD_ALLOCATION_TYPE, // T_NARROWKLASS = 19,
1570   BAD_ALLOCATION_TYPE, // T_CONFLICT    = 20
1571 };
1572 
1573 static FieldAllocationType basic_type_to_atype(bool is_static, BasicType type, bool is_flattenable) {
1574   assert(type >= T_BOOLEAN && type < T_VOID, "only allowable values");
1575   FieldAllocationType result = _basic_type_to_atype[type + (is_static ? (T_CONFLICT + 1) : 0)];
1576   assert(result != BAD_ALLOCATION_TYPE, "bad type");
1577   if (is_flattenable) {
1578     result = is_static ? STATIC_FLATTENABLE : NONSTATIC_FLATTENABLE;
1579   }
1580   return result;
1581 }
1582 
1583 class ClassFileParser::FieldAllocationCount : public ResourceObj {
1584  public:
1585   u2 count[MAX_FIELD_ALLOCATION_TYPE];
1586 
1587   FieldAllocationCount() {
1588     for (int i = 0; i < MAX_FIELD_ALLOCATION_TYPE; i++) {
1589       count[i] = 0;
1590     }
1591   }
1592 
1593   FieldAllocationType update(bool is_static, BasicType type, bool is_flattenable) {
1594     FieldAllocationType atype = basic_type_to_atype(is_static, type, is_flattenable);
1595     if (atype != BAD_ALLOCATION_TYPE) {
1596       // Make sure there is no overflow with injected fields.
1597       assert(count[atype] < 0xFFFF, "More than 65535 fields");
1598       count[atype]++;
1599     }
1600     return atype;
1601   }
1602 };
1603 
1604 // Side-effects: populates the _fields, _fields_annotations,
1605 // _fields_type_annotations fields
1606 void ClassFileParser::parse_fields(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
1607                                    bool is_interface,
1608                                    bool is_value_type,
1609                                    FieldAllocationCount* const fac,
1610                                    ConstantPool* cp,
1611                                    const int cp_size,
1612                                    u2* const java_fields_count_ptr,
1613                                    TRAPS) {
1614 
1615   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
1616   assert(fac != NULL, "invariant");
1617   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
1618   assert(java_fields_count_ptr != NULL, "invariant");
1619 
1620   assert(NULL == _fields, "invariant");
1621   assert(NULL == _fields_annotations, "invariant");
1622   assert(NULL == _fields_type_annotations, "invariant");
1623 
1624   cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK);  // length
1625   const u2 length = cfs->get_u2_fast();
1626   *java_fields_count_ptr = length;
1627 
1628   int num_injected = 0;
1629   const InjectedField* const injected = JavaClasses::get_injected(_class_name,
1630                                                                   &num_injected);
1631 
1632   // two more slots are required for inline classes:
1633   // one for the static field with a reference to the pre-allocated default value
1634   // one for the field the JVM injects when detecting an empty inline class
1635   const int total_fields = length + num_injected + (is_value_type ? 2 : 0);
1636 
1637   // The field array starts with tuples of shorts
1638   // [access, name index, sig index, initial value index, byte offset].
1639   // A generic signature slot only exists for field with generic
1640   // signature attribute. And the access flag is set with
1641   // JVM_ACC_FIELD_HAS_GENERIC_SIGNATURE for that field. The generic
1642   // signature slots are at the end of the field array and after all
1643   // other fields data.
1644   //
1645   //   f1: [access, name index, sig index, initial value index, low_offset, high_offset]
1646   //   f2: [access, name index, sig index, initial value index, low_offset, high_offset]
1647   //       ...
1648   //   fn: [access, name index, sig index, initial value index, low_offset, high_offset]
1649   //       [generic signature index]
1650   //       [generic signature index]
1651   //       ...
1652   //
1653   // Allocate a temporary resource array for field data. For each field,
1654   // a slot is reserved in the temporary array for the generic signature
1655   // index. After parsing all fields, the data are copied to a permanent
1656   // array and any unused slots will be discarded.
1657   ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
1658   u2* const fa = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(THREAD,
1659                                               u2,
1660                                               total_fields * (FieldInfo::field_slots + 1));
1661 
1662   // The generic signature slots start after all other fields' data.
1663   int generic_signature_slot = total_fields * FieldInfo::field_slots;
1664   int num_generic_signature = 0;
1665   int instance_fields_count = 0;
1666   for (int n = 0; n < length; n++) {
1667     // access_flags, name_index, descriptor_index, attributes_count
1668     cfs->guarantee_more(8, CHECK);
1669 
1670     jint recognized_modifiers = JVM_RECOGNIZED_FIELD_MODIFIERS;
1671 
1672     const jint flags = cfs->get_u2_fast() & recognized_modifiers;
1673     verify_legal_field_modifiers(flags, is_interface, is_value_type, CHECK);
1674     AccessFlags access_flags;
1675     access_flags.set_flags(flags);
1676 
1677     const u2 name_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
1678     check_property(valid_symbol_at(name_index),
1679       "Invalid constant pool index %u for field name in class file %s",
1680       name_index, CHECK);
1681     const Symbol* const name = cp->symbol_at(name_index);
1682     verify_legal_field_name(name, CHECK);
1683 
1684     const u2 signature_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
1685     check_property(valid_symbol_at(signature_index),
1686       "Invalid constant pool index %u for field signature in class file %s",
1687       signature_index, CHECK);
1688     const Symbol* const sig = cp->symbol_at(signature_index);
1689     verify_legal_field_signature(name, sig, CHECK);
1690     assert(!access_flags.is_flattenable(), "ACC_FLATTENABLE should have been filtered out");
1691     if (sig->is_Q_signature()) {
1692       // assert(_major_version >= CONSTANT_CLASS_DESCRIPTORS, "Q-descriptors are only supported in recent classfiles");
1693       access_flags.set_is_flattenable();
1694     }
1695     if (access_flags.is_flattenable()) {
1696       // Array flattenability cannot be specified.  Arrays of value classes are
1697       // are always flattenable.  Arrays of other classes are not flattenable.
1698       if (sig->utf8_length() > 1 && sig->char_at(0) == '[') {
1699         classfile_parse_error(
1700             "Field \"%s\" with signature \"%s\" in class file %s is invalid."
1701             " ACC_FLATTENABLE cannot be specified for an array",
1702             name->as_C_string(), sig->as_klass_external_name(), CHECK);
1703       }
1704       _has_flattenable_fields = true;
1705     }
1706     if (!access_flags.is_static()) instance_fields_count++;
1707 
1708     u2 constantvalue_index = 0;
1709     bool is_synthetic = false;
1710     u2 generic_signature_index = 0;
1711     const bool is_static = access_flags.is_static();
1712     FieldAnnotationCollector parsed_annotations(_loader_data);
1713 
1714     const u2 attributes_count = cfs->get_u2_fast();
1715     if (attributes_count > 0) {
1716       parse_field_attributes(cfs,
1717                              attributes_count,
1718                              is_static,
1719                              signature_index,
1720                              &constantvalue_index,
1721                              &is_synthetic,
1722                              &generic_signature_index,
1723                              &parsed_annotations,
1724                              CHECK);
1725 
1726       if (parsed_annotations.field_annotations() != NULL) {
1727         if (_fields_annotations == NULL) {
1728           _fields_annotations = MetadataFactory::new_array<AnnotationArray*>(
1729                                              _loader_data, length, NULL,
1730                                              CHECK);
1731         }
1732         _fields_annotations->at_put(n, parsed_annotations.field_annotations());
1733         parsed_annotations.set_field_annotations(NULL);
1734       }
1735       if (parsed_annotations.field_type_annotations() != NULL) {
1736         if (_fields_type_annotations == NULL) {
1737           _fields_type_annotations =
1738             MetadataFactory::new_array<AnnotationArray*>(_loader_data,
1739                                                          length,
1740                                                          NULL,
1741                                                          CHECK);
1742         }
1743         _fields_type_annotations->at_put(n, parsed_annotations.field_type_annotations());
1744         parsed_annotations.set_field_type_annotations(NULL);
1745       }
1746 
1747       if (is_synthetic) {
1748         access_flags.set_is_synthetic();
1749       }
1750       if (generic_signature_index != 0) {
1751         access_flags.set_field_has_generic_signature();
1752         fa[generic_signature_slot] = generic_signature_index;
1753         generic_signature_slot ++;
1754         num_generic_signature ++;
1755       }
1756     }
1757 
1758     FieldInfo* const field = FieldInfo::from_field_array(fa, n);
1759     field->initialize(access_flags.as_short(),
1760                       name_index,
1761                       signature_index,
1762                       constantvalue_index);
1763     const BasicType type = cp->basic_type_for_signature_at(signature_index);
1764 
1765     // Remember how many oops we encountered and compute allocation type
1766     const FieldAllocationType atype = fac->update(is_static, type, access_flags.is_flattenable());
1767     field->set_allocation_type(atype);
1768 
1769     // After field is initialized with type, we can augment it with aux info
1770     if (parsed_annotations.has_any_annotations()) {
1771       parsed_annotations.apply_to(field);
1772       if (field->is_contended()) {
1773         _has_contended_fields = true;
1774       }
1775     }
1776   }
1777 
1778   int index = length;
1779   if (num_injected != 0) {
1780     for (int n = 0; n < num_injected; n++) {
1781       // Check for duplicates
1782       if (injected[n].may_be_java) {
1783         const Symbol* const name      = injected[n].name();
1784         const Symbol* const signature = injected[n].signature();
1785         bool duplicate = false;
1786         for (int i = 0; i < length; i++) {
1787           const FieldInfo* const f = FieldInfo::from_field_array(fa, i);
1788           if (name      == cp->symbol_at(f->name_index()) &&
1789               signature == cp->symbol_at(f->signature_index())) {
1790             // Symbol is desclared in Java so skip this one
1791             duplicate = true;
1792             break;
1793           }
1794         }
1795         if (duplicate) {
1796           // These will be removed from the field array at the end
1797           continue;
1798         }
1799       }
1800 
1801       // Injected field
1802       FieldInfo* const field = FieldInfo::from_field_array(fa, index);
1803       field->initialize(JVM_ACC_FIELD_INTERNAL,
1804                         injected[n].name_index,
1805                         injected[n].signature_index,
1806                         0);
1807 
1808       const BasicType type = Signature::basic_type(injected[n].signature());
1809 
1810       // Remember how many oops we encountered and compute allocation type
1811       const FieldAllocationType atype = fac->update(false, type, false);
1812       field->set_allocation_type(atype);
1813       index++;
1814     }
1815   }
1816 
1817   if (is_value_type) {
1818     FieldInfo* const field = FieldInfo::from_field_array(fa, index);
1819     field->initialize(JVM_ACC_FIELD_INTERNAL | JVM_ACC_STATIC,
1820                       vmSymbols::default_value_name_enum,
1821                       vmSymbols::object_signature_enum,
1822                       0);
1823     const BasicType type = Signature::basic_type(vmSymbols::object_signature());
1824     const FieldAllocationType atype = fac->update(true, type, false);
1825     field->set_allocation_type(atype);
1826     index++;
1827   }
1828 
1829   if (is_value_type && instance_fields_count == 0) {
1830     _is_empty_value = true;
1831     FieldInfo* const field = FieldInfo::from_field_array(fa, index);
1832     field->initialize(JVM_ACC_FIELD_INTERNAL,
1833         vmSymbols::empty_marker_name_enum,
1834         vmSymbols::byte_signature_enum,
1835         0);
1836     const BasicType type = Signature::basic_type(vmSymbols::byte_signature());
1837     const FieldAllocationType atype = fac->update(false, type, false);
1838     field->set_allocation_type(atype);
1839     index++;
1840   }
1841 
1842   assert(NULL == _fields, "invariant");
1843 
1844   _fields =
1845     MetadataFactory::new_array<u2>(_loader_data,
1846                                    index * FieldInfo::field_slots + num_generic_signature,
1847                                    CHECK);
1848   // Sometimes injected fields already exist in the Java source so
1849   // the fields array could be too long.  In that case the
1850   // fields array is trimed. Also unused slots that were reserved
1851   // for generic signature indexes are discarded.
1852   {
1853     int i = 0;
