1854     for (; i < index * FieldInfo::field_slots; i++) {
1855       _fields->at_put(i, fa[i]);
1856     }
1857     for (int j = total_fields * FieldInfo::field_slots;
1858          j < generic_signature_slot; j++) {
1859       _fields->at_put(i++, fa[j]);
1860     }
1861     assert(_fields->length() == i, "");
1862   }
1863 
1864   if (_need_verify && length > 1) {
1865     // Check duplicated fields
1866     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
1867     NameSigHash** names_and_sigs = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(
1868       THREAD, NameSigHash*, HASH_ROW_SIZE);
1869     initialize_hashtable(names_and_sigs);
1870     bool dup = false;
1871     const Symbol* name = NULL;
1872     const Symbol* sig = NULL;
1873     {
1874       debug_only(NoSafepointVerifier nsv;)
1875       for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
1876         name = fs.name();
1877         sig = fs.signature();
1878         // If no duplicates, add name/signature in hashtable names_and_sigs.
1879         if (!put_after_lookup(name, sig, names_and_sigs)) {
1880           dup = true;
1881           break;
1882         }
1883       }
1884     }
1885     if (dup) {
1886       classfile_parse_error("Duplicate field name \"%s\" with signature \"%s\" in class file %s",
1887                              name->as_C_string(), sig->as_klass_external_name(), CHECK);
1888     }
1889   }
1890 }
1891 
1892 
1893 const ClassFileParser::unsafe_u2* ClassFileParser::parse_exception_table(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
1894                                                                          u4 code_length,
1895                                                                          u4 exception_table_length,
1896                                                                          TRAPS) {
1897   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
1898 
1899   const unsafe_u2* const exception_table_start = cfs->current();
1900   assert(exception_table_start != NULL, "null exception table");
1901 
1902   cfs->guarantee_more(8 * exception_table_length, CHECK_NULL); // start_pc,
1903                                                                // end_pc,
1904                                                                // handler_pc,
1905                                                                // catch_type_index
1906 
1907   // Will check legal target after parsing code array in verifier.
1908   if (_need_verify) {
1909     for (unsigned int i = 0; i < exception_table_length; i++) {
1910       const u2 start_pc = cfs->get_u2_fast();
1911       const u2 end_pc = cfs->get_u2_fast();
1912       const u2 handler_pc = cfs->get_u2_fast();
1913       const u2 catch_type_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
1914       guarantee_property((start_pc < end_pc) && (end_pc <= code_length),
1915                          "Illegal exception table range in class file %s",
1916                          CHECK_NULL);
1917       guarantee_property(handler_pc < code_length,
1918                          "Illegal exception table handler in class file %s",
1919                          CHECK_NULL);
1920       if (catch_type_index != 0) {
1921         guarantee_property(valid_klass_reference_at(catch_type_index),
1922                            "Catch type in exception table has bad constant type in class file %s", CHECK_NULL);
1923       }
1924     }
1925   } else {
1926     cfs->skip_u2_fast(exception_table_length * 4);
1927   }
1928   return exception_table_start;
1929 }
1930 
1931 void ClassFileParser::parse_linenumber_table(u4 code_attribute_length,
1932                                              u4 code_length,
1933                                              CompressedLineNumberWriteStream**const write_stream,
1934                                              TRAPS) {
1935 
1936   const ClassFileStream* const cfs = _stream;
1937   unsigned int num_entries = cfs->get_u2(CHECK);
1938 
1939   // Each entry is a u2 start_pc, and a u2 line_number
1940   const unsigned int length_in_bytes = num_entries * (sizeof(u2) * 2);
1941 
1942   // Verify line number attribute and table length
1943   check_property(
1944     code_attribute_length == sizeof(u2) + length_in_bytes,
1945     "LineNumberTable attribute has wrong length in class file %s", CHECK);
1946 
1947   cfs->guarantee_more(length_in_bytes, CHECK);
1948 
1949   if ((*write_stream) == NULL) {
1950     if (length_in_bytes > fixed_buffer_size) {
1951       (*write_stream) = new CompressedLineNumberWriteStream(length_in_bytes);
1952     } else {
1953       (*write_stream) = new CompressedLineNumberWriteStream(
1954         _linenumbertable_buffer, fixed_buffer_size);
1955     }
1956   }
1957 
1958   while (num_entries-- > 0) {
1959     const u2 bci  = cfs->get_u2_fast(); // start_pc
1960     const u2 line = cfs->get_u2_fast(); // line_number
1961     guarantee_property(bci < code_length,
1962         "Invalid pc in LineNumberTable in class file %s", CHECK);
1963     (*write_stream)->write_pair(bci, line);
1964   }
1965 }
1966 
1967 
1968 class LVT_Hash : public AllStatic {
1969  public:
1970 
1971   static bool equals(LocalVariableTableElement const& e0, LocalVariableTableElement const& e1) {
1972   /*
1973    * 3-tuple start_bci/length/slot has to be unique key,
1974    * so the following comparison seems to be redundant:
1975    *       && elem->name_cp_index == entry->_elem->name_cp_index
1976    */
1977     return (e0.start_bci     == e1.start_bci &&
1978             e0.length        == e1.length &&
1979             e0.name_cp_index == e1.name_cp_index &&
1980             e0.slot          == e1.slot);
1981   }
1982 
1983   static unsigned int hash(LocalVariableTableElement const& e0) {
1984     unsigned int raw_hash = e0.start_bci;
1985 
1986     raw_hash = e0.length        + raw_hash * 37;
1987     raw_hash = e0.name_cp_index + raw_hash * 37;
1988     raw_hash = e0.slot          + raw_hash * 37;
1989 
1990     return raw_hash;
1991   }
1992 };
1993 
1994 
1995 // Class file LocalVariableTable elements.
1996 class Classfile_LVT_Element {
1997  public:
1998   u2 start_bci;
1999   u2 length;
2000   u2 name_cp_index;
2001   u2 descriptor_cp_index;
2002   u2 slot;
2003 };
2004 
2005 static void copy_lvt_element(const Classfile_LVT_Element* const src,
2006                              LocalVariableTableElement* const lvt) {
2007   lvt->start_bci           = Bytes::get_Java_u2((u1*) &src->start_bci);
2008   lvt->length              = Bytes::get_Java_u2((u1*) &src->length);
2009   lvt->name_cp_index       = Bytes::get_Java_u2((u1*) &src->name_cp_index);
2010   lvt->descriptor_cp_index = Bytes::get_Java_u2((u1*) &src->descriptor_cp_index);
2011   lvt->signature_cp_index  = 0;
2012   lvt->slot                = Bytes::get_Java_u2((u1*) &src->slot);
2013 }
2014 
2015 // Function is used to parse both attributes:
2016 // LocalVariableTable (LVT) and LocalVariableTypeTable (LVTT)
2017 const ClassFileParser::unsafe_u2* ClassFileParser::parse_localvariable_table(const ClassFileStream* cfs,
2018                                                                              u4 code_length,
2019                                                                              u2 max_locals,
2020                                                                              u4 code_attribute_length,
2021                                                                              u2* const localvariable_table_length,
2022                                                                              bool isLVTT,
2023                                                                              TRAPS) {
2024   const char* const tbl_name = (isLVTT) ? "LocalVariableTypeTable" : "LocalVariableTable";
2025   *localvariable_table_length = cfs->get_u2(CHECK_NULL);
2026   const unsigned int size =
2027     (*localvariable_table_length) * sizeof(Classfile_LVT_Element) / sizeof(u2);
2028 
2029   const ConstantPool* const cp = _cp;
2030 
2031   // Verify local variable table attribute has right length
2032   if (_need_verify) {
2033     guarantee_property(code_attribute_length == (sizeof(*localvariable_table_length) + size * sizeof(u2)),
2034                        "%s has wrong length in class file %s", tbl_name, CHECK_NULL);
2035   }
2036 
2037   const unsafe_u2* const localvariable_table_start = cfs->current();
2038   assert(localvariable_table_start != NULL, "null local variable table");
2039   if (!_need_verify) {
2040     cfs->skip_u2_fast(size);
2041   } else {
2042     cfs->guarantee_more(size * 2, CHECK_NULL);
2043     for(int i = 0; i < (*localvariable_table_length); i++) {
2044       const u2 start_pc = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2045       const u2 length = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2046       const u2 name_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2047       const u2 descriptor_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2048       const u2 index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2049       // Assign to a u4 to avoid overflow
2050       const u4 end_pc = (u4)start_pc + (u4)length;
2051 
2052       if (start_pc >= code_length) {
2053         classfile_parse_error(
2054           "Invalid start_pc %u in %s in class file %s",
2055           start_pc, tbl_name, CHECK_NULL);
2056       }
2057       if (end_pc > code_length) {
2058         classfile_parse_error(
2059           "Invalid length %u in %s in class file %s",
2060           length, tbl_name, CHECK_NULL);
2061       }
2062       const int cp_size = cp->length();
2063       guarantee_property(valid_symbol_at(name_index),
2064         "Name index %u in %s has bad constant type in class file %s",
2065         name_index, tbl_name, CHECK_NULL);
2066       guarantee_property(valid_symbol_at(descriptor_index),
2067         "Signature index %u in %s has bad constant type in class file %s",
2068         descriptor_index, tbl_name, CHECK_NULL);
2069 
2070       const Symbol* const name = cp->symbol_at(name_index);
2071       const Symbol* const sig = cp->symbol_at(descriptor_index);
2072       verify_legal_field_name(name, CHECK_NULL);
2073       u2 extra_slot = 0;
2074       if (!isLVTT) {
2075         verify_legal_field_signature(name, sig, CHECK_NULL);
2076 
2077         // 4894874: check special cases for double and long local variables
2078         if (sig == vmSymbols::type_signature(T_DOUBLE) ||
2079             sig == vmSymbols::type_signature(T_LONG)) {
2080           extra_slot = 1;
2081         }
2082       }
2083       guarantee_property((index + extra_slot) < max_locals,
2084                           "Invalid index %u in %s in class file %s",
2085                           index, tbl_name, CHECK_NULL);
2086     }
2087   }
2088   return localvariable_table_start;
2089 }
2090 
2091 static const u1* parse_stackmap_table(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
2092                                       u4 code_attribute_length,
2093                                       bool need_verify,
2094                                       TRAPS) {
2095   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
2096 
2097   if (0 == code_attribute_length) {
2098     return NULL;
2099   }
2100 
2101   const u1* const stackmap_table_start = cfs->current();
2102   assert(stackmap_table_start != NULL, "null stackmap table");
2103 
2104   // check code_attribute_length first
2105   cfs->skip_u1(code_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2106 
2107   if (!need_verify && !DumpSharedSpaces) {
2108     return NULL;
2109   }
2110   return stackmap_table_start;
2111 }
2112 
2113 const ClassFileParser::unsafe_u2* ClassFileParser::parse_checked_exceptions(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
2114                                                                             u2* const checked_exceptions_length,
2115                                                                             u4 method_attribute_length,
2116                                                                             TRAPS) {
2117   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
2118   assert(checked_exceptions_length != NULL, "invariant");
2119 
2120   cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK_NULL);  // checked_exceptions_length
2121   *checked_exceptions_length = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2122   const unsigned int size =
2123     (*checked_exceptions_length) * sizeof(CheckedExceptionElement) / sizeof(u2);
2124   const unsafe_u2* const checked_exceptions_start = cfs->current();
2125   assert(checked_exceptions_start != NULL, "null checked exceptions");
2126   if (!_need_verify) {
2127     cfs->skip_u2_fast(size);
2128   } else {
2129     // Verify each value in the checked exception table
2130     u2 checked_exception;
2131     const u2 len = *checked_exceptions_length;
2132     cfs->guarantee_more(2 * len, CHECK_NULL);
2133     for (int i = 0; i < len; i++) {
2134       checked_exception = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2135       check_property(
2136         valid_klass_reference_at(checked_exception),
2137         "Exception name has bad type at constant pool %u in class file %s",
2138         checked_exception, CHECK_NULL);
2139     }
2140   }
2141   // check exceptions attribute length
2142   if (_need_verify) {
2143     guarantee_property(method_attribute_length == (sizeof(*checked_exceptions_length) +
2144                                                    sizeof(u2) * size),
2145                       "Exceptions attribute has wrong length in class file %s", CHECK_NULL);
2146   }
2147   return checked_exceptions_start;
2148 }
2149 
2150 void ClassFileParser::throwIllegalSignature(const char* type,
2151                                             const Symbol* name,
2152                                             const Symbol* sig,
2153                                             TRAPS) const {
2154   assert(name != NULL, "invariant");
2155   assert(sig != NULL, "invariant");
2156 
2157   const char* class_note = "";
2158   if (is_value_type() && name == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name()) {
2159     class_note = " (an inline class)";
2160   }
2161 
2162   ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
2163   Exceptions::fthrow(THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
2164       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
2165       "%s \"%s\" in class %s%s has illegal signature \"%s\"", type,
2166       name->as_C_string(), _class_name->as_C_string(), class_note, sig->as_C_string());
2167 }
2168 
2169 AnnotationCollector::ID
2170 AnnotationCollector::annotation_index(const ClassLoaderData* loader_data,
2171                                       const Symbol* name) {
2172   const vmSymbols::SID sid = vmSymbols::find_sid(name);
2173   // Privileged code can use all annotations.  Other code silently drops some.
2174   const bool privileged = loader_data->is_the_null_class_loader_data() ||
2175                           loader_data->is_platform_class_loader_data() ||
2176                           loader_data->is_unsafe_anonymous();
2177   switch (sid) {
2178     case vmSymbols::VM_SYMBOL_ENUM_NAME(reflect_CallerSensitive_signature): {
2179       if (_location != _in_method)  break;  // only allow for methods
2180       if (!privileged)              break;  // only allow in privileged code
2181       return _method_CallerSensitive;
2182     }
2183     case vmSymbols::VM_SYMBOL_ENUM_NAME(jdk_internal_vm_annotation_ForceInline_signature): {
2184       if (_location != _in_method)  break;  // only allow for methods
2185       if (!privileged)              break;  // only allow in privileged code
2186       return _method_ForceInline;
2187     }
2188     case vmSymbols::VM_SYMBOL_ENUM_NAME(jdk_internal_vm_annotation_DontInline_signature): {
2189       if (_location != _in_method)  break;  // only allow for methods
2190       if (!privileged)              break;  // only allow in privileged code
2191       return _method_DontInline;
2192     }
2193     case vmSymbols::VM_SYMBOL_ENUM_NAME(java_lang_invoke_InjectedProfile_signature): {
2194       if (_location != _in_method)  break;  // only allow for methods
2195       if (!privileged)              break;  // only allow in privileged code
2196       return _method_InjectedProfile;
2197     }
2198     case vmSymbols::VM_SYMBOL_ENUM_NAME(java_lang_invoke_LambdaForm_Compiled_signature): {
2199       if (_location != _in_method)  break;  // only allow for methods
2200       if (!privileged)              break;  // only allow in privileged code
2201       return _method_LambdaForm_Compiled;
2202     }
2203     case vmSymbols::VM_SYMBOL_ENUM_NAME(jdk_internal_vm_annotation_Hidden_signature): {
2204       if (_location != _in_method)  break;  // only allow for methods
2205       if (!privileged)              break;  // only allow in privileged code
2206       return _method_Hidden;
2207     }
2208     case vmSymbols::VM_SYMBOL_ENUM_NAME(jdk_internal_HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate_signature): {
2209       if (_location != _in_method)  break;  // only allow for methods
2210       if (!privileged)              break;  // only allow in privileged code
2211       return _method_HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate;
2212     }
2213     case vmSymbols::VM_SYMBOL_ENUM_NAME(jdk_internal_vm_annotation_Stable_signature): {
2214       if (_location != _in_field)   break;  // only allow for fields
2215       if (!privileged)              break;  // only allow in privileged code
2216       return _field_Stable;
2217     }
2218     case vmSymbols::VM_SYMBOL_ENUM_NAME(jdk_internal_vm_annotation_Contended_signature): {
2219       if (_location != _in_field && _location != _in_class) {
2220         break;  // only allow for fields and classes
2221       }
2222       if (!EnableContended || (RestrictContended && !privileged)) {
2223         break;  // honor privileges
2224       }
2225       return _jdk_internal_vm_annotation_Contended;
2226     }
2227     case vmSymbols::VM_SYMBOL_ENUM_NAME(jdk_internal_vm_annotation_ReservedStackAccess_signature): {
2228       if (_location != _in_method)  break;  // only allow for methods
2229       if (RestrictReservedStack && !privileged) break; // honor privileges
2230       return _jdk_internal_vm_annotation_ReservedStackAccess;
2231     }
2232     default: {
2233       break;
2234     }
2235   }
2236   return AnnotationCollector::_unknown;
2237 }
2238 
2239 void ClassFileParser::FieldAnnotationCollector::apply_to(FieldInfo* f) {
2240   if (is_contended())
2241     f->set_contended_group(contended_group());
2242   if (is_stable())
2243     f->set_stable(true);
2244 }
2245 
2246 ClassFileParser::FieldAnnotationCollector::~FieldAnnotationCollector() {
2247   // If there's an error deallocate metadata for field annotations
2248   MetadataFactory::free_array<u1>(_loader_data, _field_annotations);
2249   MetadataFactory::free_array<u1>(_loader_data, _field_type_annotations);
2250 }
2251 
2252 void MethodAnnotationCollector::apply_to(const methodHandle& m) {
2253   if (has_annotation(_method_CallerSensitive))
2254     m->set_caller_sensitive(true);
2255   if (has_annotation(_method_ForceInline))
2256     m->set_force_inline(true);
2257   if (has_annotation(_method_DontInline))
2258     m->set_dont_inline(true);
2259   if (has_annotation(_method_InjectedProfile))
2260     m->set_has_injected_profile(true);
2261   if (has_annotation(_method_LambdaForm_Compiled) && m->intrinsic_id() == vmIntrinsics::_none)
2262     m->set_intrinsic_id(vmIntrinsics::_compiledLambdaForm);
2263   if (has_annotation(_method_Hidden))
2264     m->set_hidden(true);
2265   if (has_annotation(_method_HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate) && !m->is_synthetic())
2266     m->set_intrinsic_candidate(true);
2267   if (has_annotation(_jdk_internal_vm_annotation_ReservedStackAccess))
2268     m->set_has_reserved_stack_access(true);
2269 }
2270 
2271 void ClassFileParser::ClassAnnotationCollector::apply_to(InstanceKlass* ik) {
2272   assert(ik != NULL, "invariant");
2273   ik->set_is_contended(is_contended());
2274 }
2275 
2276 #define MAX_ARGS_SIZE 255
2277 #define MAX_CODE_SIZE 65535
2278 #define INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER 256
2279 
2280 /* Copy class file LVT's/LVTT's into the HotSpot internal LVT.
2281  *
2282  * Rules for LVT's and LVTT's are:
2283  *   - There can be any number of LVT's and LVTT's.
2284  *   - If there are n LVT's, it is the same as if there was just
2285  *     one LVT containing all the entries from the n LVT's.
2286  *   - There may be no more than one LVT entry per local variable.
2287  *     Two LVT entries are 'equal' if these fields are the same:
2288  *        start_pc, length, name, slot
2289  *   - There may be no more than one LVTT entry per each LVT entry.
2290  *     Each LVTT entry has to match some LVT entry.
2291  *   - HotSpot internal LVT keeps natural ordering of class file LVT entries.
2292  */
2293 void ClassFileParser::copy_localvariable_table(const ConstMethod* cm,
2294                                                int lvt_cnt,
2295                                                u2* const localvariable_table_length,
2296                                                const unsafe_u2** const localvariable_table_start,
2297                                                int lvtt_cnt,
2298                                                u2* const localvariable_type_table_length,
2299                                                const unsafe_u2** const localvariable_type_table_start,
2300                                                TRAPS) {
2301 
2302   ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
2303 
2304   typedef ResourceHashtable<LocalVariableTableElement, LocalVariableTableElement*,
2305                             &LVT_Hash::hash, &LVT_Hash::equals> LVT_HashTable;
2306 
2307   LVT_HashTable* const table = new LVT_HashTable();
2308 
2309   // To fill LocalVariableTable in
2310   const Classfile_LVT_Element* cf_lvt;
2311   LocalVariableTableElement* lvt = cm->localvariable_table_start();
2312 
2313   for (int tbl_no = 0; tbl_no < lvt_cnt; tbl_no++) {
2314     cf_lvt = (Classfile_LVT_Element *) localvariable_table_start[tbl_no];
2315     for (int idx = 0; idx < localvariable_table_length[tbl_no]; idx++, lvt++) {
2316       copy_lvt_element(&cf_lvt[idx], lvt);
2317       // If no duplicates, add LVT elem in hashtable.
2318       if (table->put(*lvt, lvt) == false
2319           && _need_verify
2320           && _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
2321         classfile_parse_error("Duplicated LocalVariableTable attribute "
2322                               "entry for '%s' in class file %s",
2323                                _cp->symbol_at(lvt->name_cp_index)->as_utf8(),
2324                                CHECK);
2325       }
2326     }
2327   }
2328 
2329   // To merge LocalVariableTable and LocalVariableTypeTable
2330   const Classfile_LVT_Element* cf_lvtt;
2331   LocalVariableTableElement lvtt_elem;
2332 
2333   for (int tbl_no = 0; tbl_no < lvtt_cnt; tbl_no++) {
2334     cf_lvtt = (Classfile_LVT_Element *) localvariable_type_table_start[tbl_no];
2335     for (int idx = 0; idx < localvariable_type_table_length[tbl_no]; idx++) {
2336       copy_lvt_element(&cf_lvtt[idx], &lvtt_elem);
2337       LocalVariableTableElement** entry = table->get(lvtt_elem);
2338       if (entry == NULL) {
2339         if (_need_verify) {
2340           classfile_parse_error("LVTT entry for '%s' in class file %s "
2341                                 "does not match any LVT entry",
2342                                  _cp->symbol_at(lvtt_elem.name_cp_index)->as_utf8(),
2343                                  CHECK);
2344         }
2345       } else if ((*entry)->signature_cp_index != 0 && _need_verify) {
2346         classfile_parse_error("Duplicated LocalVariableTypeTable attribute "
2347                               "entry for '%s' in class file %s",
2348                                _cp->symbol_at(lvtt_elem.name_cp_index)->as_utf8(),
2349                                CHECK);
2350       } else {
2351         // to add generic signatures into LocalVariableTable
2352         (*entry)->signature_cp_index = lvtt_elem.descriptor_cp_index;
2353       }
2354     }
2355   }
2356 }
2357 
2358 
2359 void ClassFileParser::copy_method_annotations(ConstMethod* cm,
2360                                        const u1* runtime_visible_annotations,
2361                                        int runtime_visible_annotations_length,
2362                                        const u1* runtime_invisible_annotations,
2363                                        int runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
2364                                        const u1* runtime_visible_parameter_annotations,
2365                                        int runtime_visible_parameter_annotations_length,
2366                                        const u1* runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations,
2367                                        int runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations_length,
2368                                        const u1* runtime_visible_type_annotations,
2369                                        int runtime_visible_type_annotations_length,
2370                                        const u1* runtime_invisible_type_annotations,
2371                                        int runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length,
2372                                        const u1* annotation_default,
2373                                        int annotation_default_length,
2374                                        TRAPS) {
2375 
2376   AnnotationArray* a;
2377 
2378   if (runtime_visible_annotations_length +
2379       runtime_invisible_annotations_length > 0) {
2380      a = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_annotations,
2381                               runtime_visible_annotations_length,
2382                               runtime_invisible_annotations,
2383                               runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
2384                               CHECK);
2385      cm->set_method_annotations(a);
2386   }
2387 
2388   if (runtime_visible_parameter_annotations_length +
2389       runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations_length > 0) {
2390     a = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_parameter_annotations,
2391                              runtime_visible_parameter_annotations_length,
2392                              runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations,
2393                              runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations_length,
2394                              CHECK);
2395     cm->set_parameter_annotations(a);
2396   }
2397 
2398   if (annotation_default_length > 0) {
2399     a = assemble_annotations(annotation_default,
2400                              annotation_default_length,
2401                              NULL,
2402                              0,
2403                              CHECK);
2404     cm->set_default_annotations(a);
2405   }
2406 
2407   if (runtime_visible_type_annotations_length +
2408       runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length > 0) {
2409     a = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_type_annotations,
2410                              runtime_visible_type_annotations_length,
2411                              runtime_invisible_type_annotations,
2412                              runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length,
2413                              CHECK);
2414     cm->set_type_annotations(a);
2415   }
2416 }
2417 
2418 
2419 // Note: the parse_method below is big and clunky because all parsing of the code and exceptions
2420 // attribute is inlined. This is cumbersome to avoid since we inline most of the parts in the
2421 // Method* to save footprint, so we only know the size of the resulting Method* when the
2422 // entire method attribute is parsed.
2423 //
2424 // The promoted_flags parameter is used to pass relevant access_flags
2425 // from the method back up to the containing klass. These flag values
2426 // are added to klass's access_flags.
2427 
2428 Method* ClassFileParser::parse_method(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
2429                                       bool is_interface,
2430                                       bool is_value_type,
2431                                       const ConstantPool* cp,
2432                                       AccessFlags* const promoted_flags,
2433                                       TRAPS) {
2434   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
2435   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
2436   assert(promoted_flags != NULL, "invariant");
2437 
2438   ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
2439   // Parse fixed parts:
2440   // access_flags, name_index, descriptor_index, attributes_count
2441   cfs->guarantee_more(8, CHECK_NULL);
2442 
2443   int flags = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2444   const u2 name_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2445   const int cp_size = cp->length();
2446   check_property(
2447     valid_symbol_at(name_index),
2448     "Illegal constant pool index %u for method name in class file %s",
2449     name_index, CHECK_NULL);
2450   const Symbol* const name = cp->symbol_at(name_index);
2451   verify_legal_method_name(name, CHECK_NULL);
2452 
2453   const u2 signature_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2454   guarantee_property(
2455     valid_symbol_at(signature_index),
2456     "Illegal constant pool index %u for method signature in class file %s",
2457     signature_index, CHECK_NULL);
2458   const Symbol* const signature = cp->symbol_at(signature_index);
2459 
2460   if (name == vmSymbols::class_initializer_name()) {
2461     // We ignore the other access flags for a valid class initializer.
2462     // (JVM Spec 2nd ed., chapter 4.6)
2463     if (_major_version < 51) { // backward compatibility
2464       flags = JVM_ACC_STATIC;
2465     } else if ((flags & JVM_ACC_STATIC) == JVM_ACC_STATIC) {
2466       flags &= JVM_ACC_STATIC | JVM_ACC_STRICT;
2467     } else {
2468       classfile_parse_error("Method <clinit> is not static in class file %s", CHECK_NULL);
2469     }
2470   } else {
2471     verify_legal_method_modifiers(flags, is_interface, is_value_type, name, CHECK_NULL);
2472   }
2473 
2474   if (name == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name()) {
2475     if (is_interface) {
2476       classfile_parse_error("Interface cannot have a method named <init>, class file %s", CHECK_NULL);
2477     } else if (!is_value_type && signature->is_void_method_signature()) {
2478       // OK, a constructor
2479     } else if (is_value_type && !signature->is_void_method_signature()) {
2480       // also OK, a static factory, as long as the return value is good
2481       bool ok = false;
2482       SignatureStream ss((Symbol*) signature, true);
2483       while (!ss.at_return_type())  ss.next();
2484       if (ss.is_reference()) {
2485         Symbol* ret = ss.as_symbol();
2486         const Symbol* required = class_name();
2487         if (is_unsafe_anonymous()) {
2488           // The original class name in the UAC byte stream gets changed.  So
2489           // using the original name in the return type is no longer valid.
2490           required = vmSymbols::java_lang_Object();
2491         }
2492         ok = (ret == required);
2493       }
2494       if (!ok) {
2495         throwIllegalSignature("Method", name, signature, CHECK_0);
2496       }
2497     } else {
2498       // not OK, so throw the same error as in verify_legal_method_signature.
2499       throwIllegalSignature("Method", name, signature, CHECK_0);
2500     }
2501     // A declared <init> method must always be either a non-static
2502     // object constructor, with a void return, or else it must be a
2503     // static factory method, with a non-void return.  No other
2504     // definition of <init> is possible.
2505     //
2506     // The verifier (in verify_invoke_instructions) will inspect the
2507     // signature of any attempt to invoke <init>, and ensures that it
2508     // returns non-void if and only if it is being invoked by
2509     // invokestatic, and void if and only if it is being invoked by
2510     // invokespecial.
2511     //
2512     // When a symbolic reference to <init> is resolved for a
2513     // particular invocation mode (special or static), the mode is
2514     // matched to the JVM_ACC_STATIC modifier of the <init> method.
2515     // Thus, it is impossible to statically invoke a constructor, and
2516     // impossible to "new + invokespecial" a static factory, either
2517     // through bytecode or through reflection.
2518   }
2519 
2520   int args_size = -1;  // only used when _need_verify is true
2521   if (_need_verify) {
2522     args_size = ((flags & JVM_ACC_STATIC) ? 0 : 1) +
2523                  verify_legal_method_signature(name, signature, CHECK_NULL);
2524     if (args_size > MAX_ARGS_SIZE) {
2525       classfile_parse_error("Too many arguments in method signature in class file %s", CHECK_NULL);
2526     }
2527   }
2528 
2529   AccessFlags access_flags(flags & JVM_RECOGNIZED_METHOD_MODIFIERS);
2530 
2531   // Default values for code and exceptions attribute elements
2532   u2 max_stack = 0;
2533   u2 max_locals = 0;
2534   u4 code_length = 0;
2535   const u1* code_start = 0;
2536   u2 exception_table_length = 0;
2537   const unsafe_u2* exception_table_start = NULL; // (potentially unaligned) pointer to array of u2 elements
2538   Array<int>* exception_handlers = Universe::the_empty_int_array();
2539   u2 checked_exceptions_length = 0;
2540   const unsafe_u2* checked_exceptions_start = NULL; // (potentially unaligned) pointer to array of u2 elements
2541   CompressedLineNumberWriteStream* linenumber_table = NULL;
2542   int linenumber_table_length = 0;
2543   int total_lvt_length = 0;
2544   u2 lvt_cnt = 0;
2545   u2 lvtt_cnt = 0;
2546   bool lvt_allocated = false;
2547   u2 max_lvt_cnt = INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER;
2548   u2 max_lvtt_cnt = INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER;
2549   u2* localvariable_table_length = NULL;
2550   const unsafe_u2** localvariable_table_start = NULL; // (potentially unaligned) pointer to array of LVT attributes
2551   u2* localvariable_type_table_length = NULL;
2552   const unsafe_u2** localvariable_type_table_start = NULL; // (potentially unaligned) pointer to LVTT attributes
2553   int method_parameters_length = -1;
2554   const u1* method_parameters_data = NULL;
2555   bool method_parameters_seen = false;
2556   bool parsed_code_attribute = false;
2557   bool parsed_checked_exceptions_attribute = false;
2558   bool parsed_stackmap_attribute = false;
2559   // stackmap attribute - JDK1.5
2560   const u1* stackmap_data = NULL;
2561   int stackmap_data_length = 0;
2562   u2 generic_signature_index = 0;
2563   MethodAnnotationCollector parsed_annotations;
2564   const u1* runtime_visible_annotations = NULL;
2565   int runtime_visible_annotations_length = 0;
2566   const u1* runtime_invisible_annotations = NULL;
2567   int runtime_invisible_annotations_length = 0;
2568   const u1* runtime_visible_parameter_annotations = NULL;
2569   int runtime_visible_parameter_annotations_length = 0;
2570   const u1* runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations = NULL;
2571   int runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations_length = 0;
2572   const u1* runtime_visible_type_annotations = NULL;
2573   int runtime_visible_type_annotations_length = 0;
2574   const u1* runtime_invisible_type_annotations = NULL;
2575   int runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length = 0;
2576   bool runtime_invisible_annotations_exists = false;
2577   bool runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists = false;
2578   bool runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations_exists = false;
2579   const u1* annotation_default = NULL;
2580   int annotation_default_length = 0;
2581 
2582   // Parse code and exceptions attribute
2583   u2 method_attributes_count = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2584   while (method_attributes_count--) {
2585     cfs->guarantee_more(6, CHECK_NULL);  // method_attribute_name_index, method_attribute_length
2586     const u2 method_attribute_name_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2587     const u4 method_attribute_length = cfs->get_u4_fast();
2588     check_property(
2589       valid_symbol_at(method_attribute_name_index),
2590       "Invalid method attribute name index %u in class file %s",
2591       method_attribute_name_index, CHECK_NULL);
2592 
2593     const Symbol* const method_attribute_name = cp->symbol_at(method_attribute_name_index);
2594     if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_code()) {
2595       // Parse Code attribute
2596       if (_need_verify) {
2597         guarantee_property(
2598             !access_flags.is_native() && !access_flags.is_abstract(),
2599                         "Code attribute in native or abstract methods in class file %s",
2600                          CHECK_NULL);
2601       }
2602       if (parsed_code_attribute) {
2603         classfile_parse_error("Multiple Code attributes in class file %s",
2604                               CHECK_NULL);
2605       }
2606       parsed_code_attribute = true;
2607 
2608       // Stack size, locals size, and code size
2609       cfs->guarantee_more(8, CHECK_NULL);
2610       max_stack = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2611       max_locals = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2612       code_length = cfs->get_u4_fast();
2613       if (_need_verify) {
2614         guarantee_property(args_size <= max_locals,
2615                            "Arguments can't fit into locals in class file %s",
2616                            CHECK_NULL);
2617         guarantee_property(code_length > 0 && code_length <= MAX_CODE_SIZE,
2618                            "Invalid method Code length %u in class file %s",
2619                            code_length, CHECK_NULL);
2620       }
2621       // Code pointer
2622       code_start = cfs->current();
2623       assert(code_start != NULL, "null code start");
2624       cfs->guarantee_more(code_length, CHECK_NULL);
2625       cfs->skip_u1_fast(code_length);
2626 
2627       // Exception handler table
2628       cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK_NULL);  // exception_table_length
2629       exception_table_length = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2630       if (exception_table_length > 0) {
2631         exception_table_start = parse_exception_table(cfs,
2632                                                       code_length,
2633                                                       exception_table_length,
2634                                                       CHECK_NULL);
2635       }
2636 
2637       // Parse additional attributes in code attribute
2638       cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK_NULL);  // code_attributes_count
2639       u2 code_attributes_count = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2640 
2641       unsigned int calculated_attribute_length = 0;
2642 
2643       calculated_attribute_length =
2644           sizeof(max_stack) + sizeof(max_locals) + sizeof(code_length);
2645       calculated_attribute_length +=
2646         code_length +
2647         sizeof(exception_table_length) +
2648         sizeof(code_attributes_count) +
2649         exception_table_length *
2650             ( sizeof(u2) +   // start_pc
2651               sizeof(u2) +   // end_pc
2652               sizeof(u2) +   // handler_pc
2653               sizeof(u2) );  // catch_type_index
2654 
2655       while (code_attributes_count--) {
2656         cfs->guarantee_more(6, CHECK_NULL);  // code_attribute_name_index, code_attribute_length
2657         const u2 code_attribute_name_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2658         const u4 code_attribute_length = cfs->get_u4_fast();
2659         calculated_attribute_length += code_attribute_length +
2660                                        sizeof(code_attribute_name_index) +
2661                                        sizeof(code_attribute_length);
2662         check_property(valid_symbol_at(code_attribute_name_index),
2663                        "Invalid code attribute name index %u in class file %s",
2664                        code_attribute_name_index,
2665                        CHECK_NULL);
2666         if (LoadLineNumberTables &&
2667             cp->symbol_at(code_attribute_name_index) == vmSymbols::tag_line_number_table()) {
2668           // Parse and compress line number table
2669           parse_linenumber_table(code_attribute_length,
2670                                  code_length,
2671                                  &linenumber_table,
2672                                  CHECK_NULL);
2673 
2674         } else if (LoadLocalVariableTables &&
2675                    cp->symbol_at(code_attribute_name_index) == vmSymbols::tag_local_variable_table()) {
2676           // Parse local variable table
2677           if (!lvt_allocated) {
2678             localvariable_table_length = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(
2679               THREAD, u2,  INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER);
2680             localvariable_table_start = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(
2681               THREAD, const unsafe_u2*, INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER);
2682             localvariable_type_table_length = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(
2683               THREAD, u2,  INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER);
2684             localvariable_type_table_start = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(
2685               THREAD, const unsafe_u2*, INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER);
2686             lvt_allocated = true;
2687           }
2688           if (lvt_cnt == max_lvt_cnt) {
2689             max_lvt_cnt <<= 1;
2690             localvariable_table_length = REALLOC_RESOURCE_ARRAY(u2, localvariable_table_length, lvt_cnt, max_lvt_cnt);
2691             localvariable_table_start  = REALLOC_RESOURCE_ARRAY(const unsafe_u2*, localvariable_table_start, lvt_cnt, max_lvt_cnt);
2692           }
2693           localvariable_table_start[lvt_cnt] =
2694             parse_localvariable_table(cfs,
2695                                       code_length,
2696                                       max_locals,
2697                                       code_attribute_length,
2698                                       &localvariable_table_length[lvt_cnt],
2699                                       false,    // is not LVTT
2700                                       CHECK_NULL);
2701           total_lvt_length += localvariable_table_length[lvt_cnt];
2702           lvt_cnt++;
2703         } else if (LoadLocalVariableTypeTables &&
2704                    _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION &&
2705                    cp->symbol_at(code_attribute_name_index) == vmSymbols::tag_local_variable_type_table()) {
2706           if (!lvt_allocated) {
2707             localvariable_table_length = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(
2708               THREAD, u2,  INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER);
2709             localvariable_table_start = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(
2710               THREAD, const unsafe_u2*, INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER);
2711             localvariable_type_table_length = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(
2712               THREAD, u2,  INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER);
2713             localvariable_type_table_start = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(
2714               THREAD, const unsafe_u2*, INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER);
2715             lvt_allocated = true;
2716           }
2717           // Parse local variable type table
2718           if (lvtt_cnt == max_lvtt_cnt) {
2719             max_lvtt_cnt <<= 1;
2720             localvariable_type_table_length = REALLOC_RESOURCE_ARRAY(u2, localvariable_type_table_length, lvtt_cnt, max_lvtt_cnt);
2721             localvariable_type_table_start  = REALLOC_RESOURCE_ARRAY(const unsafe_u2*, localvariable_type_table_start, lvtt_cnt, max_lvtt_cnt);
2722           }
2723           localvariable_type_table_start[lvtt_cnt] =
2724             parse_localvariable_table(cfs,
2725                                       code_length,
2726                                       max_locals,
2727                                       code_attribute_length,
2728                                       &localvariable_type_table_length[lvtt_cnt],
2729                                       true,     // is LVTT
2730                                       CHECK_NULL);
2731           lvtt_cnt++;
2732         } else if (_major_version >= Verifier::STACKMAP_ATTRIBUTE_MAJOR_VERSION &&
2733                    cp->symbol_at(code_attribute_name_index) == vmSymbols::tag_stack_map_table()) {
2734           // Stack map is only needed by the new verifier in JDK1.5.
2735           if (parsed_stackmap_attribute) {
2736             classfile_parse_error("Multiple StackMapTable attributes in class file %s", CHECK_NULL);
2737           }
2738           stackmap_data = parse_stackmap_table(cfs, code_attribute_length, _need_verify, CHECK_NULL);
2739           stackmap_data_length = code_attribute_length;
2740           parsed_stackmap_attribute = true;
2741         } else {
2742           // Skip unknown attributes
2743           cfs->skip_u1(code_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2744         }
2745       }
2746       // check method attribute length
2747       if (_need_verify) {
2748         guarantee_property(method_attribute_length == calculated_attribute_length,
2749                            "Code segment has wrong length in class file %s",
2750                            CHECK_NULL);
2751       }
2752     } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_exceptions()) {
2753       // Parse Exceptions attribute
2754       if (parsed_checked_exceptions_attribute) {
2755         classfile_parse_error("Multiple Exceptions attributes in class file %s",
2756                               CHECK_NULL);
2757       }
2758       parsed_checked_exceptions_attribute = true;
2759       checked_exceptions_start =
2760             parse_checked_exceptions(cfs,
2761                                      &checked_exceptions_length,
2762                                      method_attribute_length,
2763                                      CHECK_NULL);
2764     } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_method_parameters()) {
2765       // reject multiple method parameters
2766       if (method_parameters_seen) {
2767         classfile_parse_error("Multiple MethodParameters attributes in class file %s",
2768                               CHECK_NULL);
2769       }
2770       method_parameters_seen = true;
2771       method_parameters_length = cfs->get_u1_fast();
2772       const u2 real_length = (method_parameters_length * 4u) + 1u;
2773       if (method_attribute_length != real_length) {
2774         classfile_parse_error(
2775           "Invalid MethodParameters method attribute length %u in class file",
2776           method_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2777       }
2778       method_parameters_data = cfs->current();
2779       cfs->skip_u2_fast(method_parameters_length);
2780       cfs->skip_u2_fast(method_parameters_length);
2781       // ignore this attribute if it cannot be reflected
2782       if (!SystemDictionary::Parameter_klass_loaded())
2783         method_parameters_length = -1;
2784     } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_synthetic()) {
2785       if (method_attribute_length != 0) {
2786         classfile_parse_error(
2787           "Invalid Synthetic method attribute length %u in class file %s",
2788           method_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2789       }
2790       // Should we check that there hasn't already been a synthetic attribute?
2791       access_flags.set_is_synthetic();
2792     } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_deprecated()) { // 4276120
2793       if (method_attribute_length != 0) {
2794         classfile_parse_error(
2795           "Invalid Deprecated method attribute length %u in class file %s",
2796           method_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2797       }
2798     } else if (_major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
2799       if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_signature()) {
2800         if (generic_signature_index != 0) {
2801           classfile_parse_error(
2802             "Multiple Signature attributes for method in class file %s",
2803             CHECK_NULL);
2804         }
2805         if (method_attribute_length != 2) {
2806           classfile_parse_error(
2807             "Invalid Signature attribute length %u in class file %s",
2808             method_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2809         }
2810         generic_signature_index = parse_generic_signature_attribute(cfs, CHECK_NULL);
2811       } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_annotations()) {
2812         if (runtime_visible_annotations != NULL) {
2813           classfile_parse_error(
2814             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleAnnotations attributes for method in class file %s",
2815             CHECK_NULL);
2816         }
2817         runtime_visible_annotations_length = method_attribute_length;
2818         runtime_visible_annotations = cfs->current();
2819         assert(runtime_visible_annotations != NULL, "null visible annotations");
2820         cfs->guarantee_more(runtime_visible_annotations_length, CHECK_NULL);
2821         parse_annotations(cp,
2822                           runtime_visible_annotations,
2823                           runtime_visible_annotations_length,
2824                           &parsed_annotations,
2825                           _loader_data,
2826                           CHECK_NULL);
2827         cfs->skip_u1_fast(runtime_visible_annotations_length);
2828       } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_annotations()) {
2829         if (runtime_invisible_annotations_exists) {
2830           classfile_parse_error(
2831             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleAnnotations attributes for method in class file %s",
2832             CHECK_NULL);
2833         }
2834         runtime_invisible_annotations_exists = true;
2835         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
2836           runtime_invisible_annotations_length = method_attribute_length;
2837           runtime_invisible_annotations = cfs->current();
2838           assert(runtime_invisible_annotations != NULL, "null invisible annotations");
2839         }
2840         cfs->skip_u1(method_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2841       } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_parameter_annotations()) {
2842         if (runtime_visible_parameter_annotations != NULL) {
2843           classfile_parse_error(
2844             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleParameterAnnotations attributes for method in class file %s",
2845             CHECK_NULL);
2846         }
2847         runtime_visible_parameter_annotations_length = method_attribute_length;
2848         runtime_visible_parameter_annotations = cfs->current();
2849         assert(runtime_visible_parameter_annotations != NULL, "null visible parameter annotations");
2850         cfs->skip_u1(runtime_visible_parameter_annotations_length, CHECK_NULL);
2851       } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations()) {
2852         if (runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations_exists) {
2853           classfile_parse_error(
2854             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleParameterAnnotations attributes for method in class file %s",
2855             CHECK_NULL);
2856         }
2857         runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations_exists = true;
2858         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
2859           runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations_length = method_attribute_length;
2860           runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations = cfs->current();
2861           assert(runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations != NULL,
2862             "null invisible parameter annotations");
2863         }
2864         cfs->skip_u1(method_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2865       } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_annotation_default()) {
2866         if (annotation_default != NULL) {
2867           classfile_parse_error(
2868             "Multiple AnnotationDefault attributes for method in class file %s",
2869             CHECK_NULL);
2870         }
2871         annotation_default_length = method_attribute_length;
2872         annotation_default = cfs->current();
2873         assert(annotation_default != NULL, "null annotation default");
2874         cfs->skip_u1(annotation_default_length, CHECK_NULL);
2875       } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_type_annotations()) {
2876         if (runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL) {
2877           classfile_parse_error(
2878             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleTypeAnnotations attributes for method in class file %s",
2879             CHECK_NULL);
2880         }
2881         runtime_visible_type_annotations_length = method_attribute_length;
2882         runtime_visible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
2883         assert(runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL, "null visible type annotations");
2884         // No need for the VM to parse Type annotations
2885         cfs->skip_u1(runtime_visible_type_annotations_length, CHECK_NULL);
2886       } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_type_annotations()) {
2887         if (runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists) {
2888           classfile_parse_error(
2889             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleTypeAnnotations attributes for method in class file %s",
2890             CHECK_NULL);
2891         } else {
2892           runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists = true;
2893         }
2894         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
2895           runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length = method_attribute_length;
2896           runtime_invisible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
2897           assert(runtime_invisible_type_annotations != NULL, "null invisible type annotations");
2898         }
2899         cfs->skip_u1(method_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2900       } else {
2901         // Skip unknown attributes
2902         cfs->skip_u1(method_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2903       }
2904     } else {
2905       // Skip unknown attributes
2906       cfs->skip_u1(method_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2907     }
2908   }
2909 
2910   if (linenumber_table != NULL) {
2911     linenumber_table->write_terminator();
2912     linenumber_table_length = linenumber_table->position();
2913   }
2914 
2915   // Make sure there's at least one Code attribute in non-native/non-abstract method
2916   if (_need_verify) {
2917     guarantee_property(access_flags.is_native() ||
2918                        access_flags.is_abstract() ||
2919                        parsed_code_attribute,
2920                        "Absent Code attribute in method that is not native or abstract in class file %s",
2921                        CHECK_NULL);
2922   }
2923 
2924   // All sizing information for a Method* is finally available, now create it
2925   InlineTableSizes sizes(
2926       total_lvt_length,
2927       linenumber_table_length,
2928       exception_table_length,
2929       checked_exceptions_length,
2930       method_parameters_length,
2931       generic_signature_index,
2932       runtime_visible_annotations_length +
2933            runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
2934       runtime_visible_parameter_annotations_length +
2935            runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations_length,
2936       runtime_visible_type_annotations_length +
2937            runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length,
2938       annotation_default_length,
2939       0);
2940 
2941   Method* const m = Method::allocate(_loader_data,
2942                                      code_length,
2943                                      access_flags,
2944                                      &sizes,
2945                                      ConstMethod::NORMAL,
2946                                      CHECK_NULL);
2947 
2948   ClassLoadingService::add_class_method_size(m->size()*wordSize);
2949 
2950   // Fill in information from fixed part (access_flags already set)
2951   m->set_constants(_cp);
2952   m->set_name_index(name_index);
2953   m->set_signature_index(signature_index);
2954   m->compute_from_signature(cp->symbol_at(signature_index));
2955   assert(args_size < 0 || args_size == m->size_of_parameters(), "");
2956 
2957   // Fill in code attribute information
2958   m->set_max_stack(max_stack);
2959   m->set_max_locals(max_locals);
2960   if (stackmap_data != NULL) {
2961     m->constMethod()->copy_stackmap_data(_loader_data,
2962                                          (u1*)stackmap_data,
2963                                          stackmap_data_length,
2964                                          CHECK_NULL);
2965   }
2966 
2967   // Copy byte codes
2968   m->set_code((u1*)code_start);
2969 
2970   // Copy line number table
2971   if (linenumber_table != NULL) {
2972     memcpy(m->compressed_linenumber_table(),
2973            linenumber_table->buffer(),
2974            linenumber_table_length);
2975   }
2976 
2977   // Copy exception table
2978   if (exception_table_length > 0) {
2979     Copy::conjoint_swap_if_needed<Endian::JAVA>(exception_table_start,
2980                                                 m->exception_table_start(),
2981                                                 exception_table_length * sizeof(ExceptionTableElement),
2982                                                 sizeof(u2));
2983   }
2984 
2985   // Copy method parameters
2986   if (method_parameters_length > 0) {
2987     MethodParametersElement* elem = m->constMethod()->method_parameters_start();
2988     for (int i = 0; i < method_parameters_length; i++) {
2989       elem[i].name_cp_index = Bytes::get_Java_u2((address)method_parameters_data);
2990       method_parameters_data += 2;
2991       elem[i].flags = Bytes::get_Java_u2((address)method_parameters_data);
2992       method_parameters_data += 2;
2993     }
2994   }
2995 
2996   // Copy checked exceptions
2997   if (checked_exceptions_length > 0) {
2998     Copy::conjoint_swap_if_needed<Endian::JAVA>(checked_exceptions_start,
2999                                                 m->checked_exceptions_start(),
3000                                                 checked_exceptions_length * sizeof(CheckedExceptionElement),
3001                                                 sizeof(u2));
3002   }
3003 
3004   // Copy class file LVT's/LVTT's into the HotSpot internal LVT.
3005   if (total_lvt_length > 0) {
3006     promoted_flags->set_has_localvariable_table();
3007     copy_localvariable_table(m->constMethod(),
3008                              lvt_cnt,
3009                              localvariable_table_length,
3010                              localvariable_table_start,
3011                              lvtt_cnt,
3012                              localvariable_type_table_length,
3013                              localvariable_type_table_start,
3014                              CHECK_NULL);
3015   }
3016 
3017   if (parsed_annotations.has_any_annotations())
3018     parsed_annotations.apply_to(methodHandle(THREAD, m));
3019 
3020   // Copy annotations
3021   copy_method_annotations(m->constMethod(),
3022                           runtime_visible_annotations,
3023                           runtime_visible_annotations_length,
3024                           runtime_invisible_annotations,
3025                           runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
3026                           runtime_visible_parameter_annotations,
3027                           runtime_visible_parameter_annotations_length,
3028                           runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations,
3029                           runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations_length,
3030                           runtime_visible_type_annotations,
3031                           runtime_visible_type_annotations_length,
3032                           runtime_invisible_type_annotations,
3033                           runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length,
3034                           annotation_default,
3035                           annotation_default_length,
3036                           CHECK_NULL);
3037 
3038   if (name == vmSymbols::finalize_method_name() &&
3039       signature == vmSymbols::void_method_signature()) {
3040     if (m->is_empty_method()) {
3041       _has_empty_finalizer = true;
3042     } else {
3043       _has_finalizer = true;
3044     }
3045   }
3046   if (name == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name() &&
3047       signature == vmSymbols::void_method_signature() &&
3048       m->is_vanilla_constructor()) {
3049     _has_vanilla_constructor = true;
3050   }
3051 
3052   NOT_PRODUCT(m->verify());
3053   return m;
3054 }
3055 
3056 
3057 // The promoted_flags parameter is used to pass relevant access_flags
3058 // from the methods back up to the containing klass. These flag values
3059 // are added to klass's access_flags.
3060 // Side-effects: populates the _methods field in the parser
3061 void ClassFileParser::parse_methods(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3062                                     bool is_interface,
3063                                     bool is_value_type,
3064                                     AccessFlags* promoted_flags,
3065                                     bool* has_final_method,
3066                                     bool* declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods,
3067                                     TRAPS) {
3068   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
3069   assert(promoted_flags != NULL, "invariant");
3070   assert(has_final_method != NULL, "invariant");
3071   assert(declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods != NULL, "invariant");
3072 
3073   assert(NULL == _methods, "invariant");
3074 
3075   cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK);  // length
3076   const u2 length = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3077   if (length == 0) {
3078     _methods = Universe::the_empty_method_array();
3079   } else {
3080     _methods = MetadataFactory::new_array<Method*>(_loader_data,
3081                                                    length,
3082                                                    NULL,
3083                                                    CHECK);
3084 
3085     for (int index = 0; index < length; index++) {
3086       Method* method = parse_method(cfs,
3087                                     is_interface,
3088                                     is_value_type,
3089                                     _cp,
3090                                     promoted_flags,
3091                                     CHECK);
3092 
3093       if (method->is_final()) {
3094         *has_final_method = true;
3095       }
3096       // declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods: declares concrete instance methods, any access flags
3097       // used for interface initialization, and default method inheritance analysis
3098       if (is_interface && !(*declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods)
3099         && !method->is_abstract() && !method->is_static()) {
3100         *declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods = true;
3101       }
3102       _methods->at_put(index, method);
3103     }
3104 
3105     if (_need_verify && length > 1) {
3106       // Check duplicated methods
3107       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
3108       NameSigHash** names_and_sigs = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(
3109         THREAD, NameSigHash*, HASH_ROW_SIZE);
3110       initialize_hashtable(names_and_sigs);
3111       bool dup = false;
3112       const Symbol* name = NULL;
3113       const Symbol* sig = NULL;
3114       {
3115         debug_only(NoSafepointVerifier nsv;)
3116         for (int i = 0; i < length; i++) {
3117           const Method* const m = _methods->at(i);
3118           name = m->name();
3119           sig = m->signature();
3120           // If no duplicates, add name/signature in hashtable names_and_sigs.
3121           if (!put_after_lookup(name, sig, names_and_sigs)) {
3122             dup = true;
3123             break;
3124           }
3125         }
3126       }
3127       if (dup) {
3128         classfile_parse_error("Duplicate method name \"%s\" with signature \"%s\" in class file %s",
3129                                name->as_C_string(), sig->as_klass_external_name(), CHECK);
3130       }
3131     }
3132   }
3133 }
3134 
3135 static const intArray* sort_methods(Array<Method*>* methods) {
3136   const int length = methods->length();
3137   // If JVMTI original method ordering or sharing is enabled we have to
3138   // remember the original class file ordering.
3139   // We temporarily use the vtable_index field in the Method* to store the
3140   // class file index, so we can read in after calling qsort.
3141   // Put the method ordering in the shared archive.
3142   if (JvmtiExport::can_maintain_original_method_order() || Arguments::is_dumping_archive()) {
3143     for (int index = 0; index < length; index++) {
3144       Method* const m = methods->at(index);
3145       assert(!m->valid_vtable_index(), "vtable index should not be set");
3146       m->set_vtable_index(index);
3147     }
3148   }
3149   // Sort method array by ascending method name (for faster lookups & vtable construction)
3150   // Note that the ordering is not alphabetical, see Symbol::fast_compare
3151   Method::sort_methods(methods);
3152 
3153   intArray* method_ordering = NULL;
3154   // If JVMTI original method ordering or sharing is enabled construct int
3155   // array remembering the original ordering
3156   if (JvmtiExport::can_maintain_original_method_order() || Arguments::is_dumping_archive()) {
3157     method_ordering = new intArray(length, length, -1);
3158     for (int index = 0; index < length; index++) {
3159       Method* const m = methods->at(index);
3160       const int old_index = m->vtable_index();
3161       assert(old_index >= 0 && old_index < length, "invalid method index");
3162       method_ordering->at_put(index, old_index);
3163       m->set_vtable_index(Method::invalid_vtable_index);
3164     }
3165   }
3166   return method_ordering;
3167 }
3168 
3169 // Parse generic_signature attribute for methods and fields
3170 u2 ClassFileParser::parse_generic_signature_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3171                                                       TRAPS) {
3172   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
3173 
3174   cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK_0);  // generic_signature_index
3175   const u2 generic_signature_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3176   check_property(
3177     valid_symbol_at(generic_signature_index),
3178     "Invalid Signature attribute at constant pool index %u in class file %s",
3179     generic_signature_index, CHECK_0);
3180   return generic_signature_index;
3181 }
3182 
3183 void ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_sourcefile_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3184                                                            TRAPS) {
3185 
3186   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
3187 
3188   cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK);  // sourcefile_index
3189   const u2 sourcefile_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3190   check_property(
3191     valid_symbol_at(sourcefile_index),
3192     "Invalid SourceFile attribute at constant pool index %u in class file %s",
3193     sourcefile_index, CHECK);
3194   set_class_sourcefile_index(sourcefile_index);
3195 }
3196 
3197 void ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_source_debug_extension_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3198                                                                        int length,
3199                                                                        TRAPS) {
3200   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
3201 
3202   const u1* const sde_buffer = cfs->current();
3203   assert(sde_buffer != NULL, "null sde buffer");
3204 
3205   // Don't bother storing it if there is no way to retrieve it
3206   if (JvmtiExport::can_get_source_debug_extension()) {
3207     assert((length+1) > length, "Overflow checking");
3208     u1* const sde = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(THREAD, u1, length+1);
3209     for (int i = 0; i < length; i++) {
3210       sde[i] = sde_buffer[i];
3211     }
3212     sde[length] = '\0';
3213     set_class_sde_buffer((const char*)sde, length);
3214   }
3215   // Got utf8 string, set stream position forward
3216   cfs->skip_u1(length, CHECK);
3217 }
3218 
3219 
3220 // Inner classes can be static, private or protected (classic VM does this)
3221 #define RECOGNIZED_INNER_CLASS_MODIFIERS ( JVM_RECOGNIZED_CLASS_MODIFIERS | \
3222                                            JVM_ACC_PRIVATE |                \
3223                                            JVM_ACC_PROTECTED |              \
3224                                            JVM_ACC_STATIC                   \
3225                                          )
3226 
3227 // Return number of classes in the inner classes attribute table
3228 u2 ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_inner_classes_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3229                                                             const u1* const inner_classes_attribute_start,
3230                                                             bool parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute,
3231                                                             u2 enclosing_method_class_index,
3232                                                             u2 enclosing_method_method_index,
3233                                                             TRAPS) {
3234   const u1* const current_mark = cfs->current();
3235   u2 length = 0;
3236   if (inner_classes_attribute_start != NULL) {
3237     cfs->set_current(inner_classes_attribute_start);
3238     cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK_0);  // length
3239     length = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3240   }
3241 
3242   // 4-tuples of shorts of inner classes data and 2 shorts of enclosing
3243   // method data:
3244   //   [inner_class_info_index,
3245   //    outer_class_info_index,
3246   //    inner_name_index,
3247   //    inner_class_access_flags,
3248   //    ...
3249   //    enclosing_method_class_index,
3250   //    enclosing_method_method_index]
3251   const int size = length * 4 + (parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute ? 2 : 0);
3252   Array<u2>* const inner_classes = MetadataFactory::new_array<u2>(_loader_data, size, CHECK_0);
3253   _inner_classes = inner_classes;
3254 
3255   int index = 0;
3256   cfs->guarantee_more(8 * length, CHECK_0);  // 4-tuples of u2
3257   for (int n = 0; n < length; n++) {
3258     // Inner class index
3259     const u2 inner_class_info_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3260     check_property(
3261       valid_klass_reference_at(inner_class_info_index),
3262       "inner_class_info_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3263       inner_class_info_index, CHECK_0);
3264     // Outer class index
3265     const u2 outer_class_info_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3266     check_property(
3267       outer_class_info_index == 0 ||
3268         valid_klass_reference_at(outer_class_info_index),
3269       "outer_class_info_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3270       outer_class_info_index, CHECK_0);
3271     // Inner class name
3272     const u2 inner_name_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3273     check_property(
3274       inner_name_index == 0 || valid_symbol_at(inner_name_index),
3275       "inner_name_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3276       inner_name_index, CHECK_0);
3277     if (_need_verify) {
3278       guarantee_property(inner_class_info_index != outer_class_info_index,
3279                          "Class is both outer and inner class in class file %s", CHECK_0);
3280     }
3281 
3282     jint recognized_modifiers = RECOGNIZED_INNER_CLASS_MODIFIERS;
3283     // JVM_ACC_MODULE is defined in JDK-9 and later.
3284     if (_major_version >= JAVA_9_VERSION) {
3285       recognized_modifiers |= JVM_ACC_MODULE;
3286     }
3287     // JVM_ACC_VALUE is defined for class file version 55 and later
3288     if (supports_value_types()) {
3289       recognized_modifiers |= JVM_ACC_VALUE;
3290     }
3291 
3292     // Access flags
3293     jint flags = cfs->get_u2_fast() & recognized_modifiers;
3294 
3295     if ((flags & JVM_ACC_INTERFACE) && _major_version < JAVA_6_VERSION) {
3296       // Set abstract bit for old class files for backward compatibility
3297       flags |= JVM_ACC_ABSTRACT;
3298     }
3299     verify_legal_class_modifiers(flags, CHECK_0);
3300     AccessFlags inner_access_flags(flags);
3301 
3302     inner_classes->at_put(index++, inner_class_info_index);
3303     inner_classes->at_put(index++, outer_class_info_index);
3304     inner_classes->at_put(index++, inner_name_index);
3305     inner_classes->at_put(index++, inner_access_flags.as_short());
3306   }
3307 
3308   // 4347400: make sure there's no duplicate entry in the classes array
3309   if (_need_verify && _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
3310     for(int i = 0; i < length * 4; i += 4) {
3311       for(int j = i + 4; j < length * 4; j += 4) {
3312         guarantee_property((inner_classes->at(i)   != inner_classes->at(j) ||
3313                             inner_classes->at(i+1) != inner_classes->at(j+1) ||
3314                             inner_classes->at(i+2) != inner_classes->at(j+2) ||
3315                             inner_classes->at(i+3) != inner_classes->at(j+3)),
3316                             "Duplicate entry in InnerClasses in class file %s",
3317                             CHECK_0);
3318       }
3319     }
3320   }
3321 
3322   // Set EnclosingMethod class and method indexes.
3323   if (parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute) {
3324     inner_classes->at_put(index++, enclosing_method_class_index);
3325     inner_classes->at_put(index++, enclosing_method_method_index);
3326   }
3327   assert(index == size, "wrong size");
3328 
3329   // Restore buffer's current position.
3330   cfs->set_current(current_mark);
3331 
3332   return length;
3333 }
3334 
3335 u2 ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_nest_members_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3336                                                            const u1* const nest_members_attribute_start,
3337                                                            TRAPS) {
3338   const u1* const current_mark = cfs->current();
3339   u2 length = 0;
3340   if (nest_members_attribute_start != NULL) {
3341     cfs->set_current(nest_members_attribute_start);
3342     cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK_0);  // length
3343     length = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3344   }
3345   const int size = length;
3346   Array<u2>* const nest_members = MetadataFactory::new_array<u2>(_loader_data, size, CHECK_0);
3347   _nest_members = nest_members;
3348 
3349   int index = 0;
3350   cfs->guarantee_more(2 * length, CHECK_0);
3351   for (int n = 0; n < length; n++) {
3352     const u2 class_info_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3353     check_property(
3354       valid_klass_reference_at(class_info_index),
3355       "Nest member class_info_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3356       class_info_index, CHECK_0);
3357     nest_members->at_put(index++, class_info_index);
3358   }
3359   assert(index == size, "wrong size");
3360 
3361   // Restore buffer's current position.
3362   cfs->set_current(current_mark);
3363 
3364   return length;
3365 }
3366 
3367 //  Record {
3368 //    u2 attribute_name_index;
3369 //    u4 attribute_length;
3370 //    u2 components_count;
3371 //    component_info components[components_count];
3372 //  }
3373 //  component_info {
3374 //    u2 name_index;
3375 //    u2 descriptor_index
3376 //    u2 attributes_count;
3377 //    attribute_info_attributes[attributes_count];
3378 //  }
3379 u2 ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_record_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3380                                                      const ConstantPool* cp,
3381                                                      const u1* const record_attribute_start,
3382                                                      TRAPS) {
3383   const u1* const current_mark = cfs->current();
3384   int components_count = 0;
3385   unsigned int calculate_attr_size = 0;
3386   if (record_attribute_start != NULL) {
3387     cfs->set_current(record_attribute_start);
3388     cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK_0);  // num of components
3389     components_count = (int)cfs->get_u2_fast();
3390     calculate_attr_size = 2;
3391   }
3392 
3393   Array<RecordComponent*>* const record_components =
3394     MetadataFactory::new_array<RecordComponent*>(_loader_data, components_count, NULL, CHECK_0);
3395   _record_components = record_components;
3396 
3397   for (int x = 0; x < components_count; x++) {
3398     cfs->guarantee_more(6, CHECK_0); // name_index, descriptor_index, attributes_count
3399 
3400     const u2 name_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3401     check_property(valid_symbol_at(name_index),
3402       "Invalid constant pool index %u for name in Record attribute in class file %s",
3403       name_index, CHECK_0);
3404     const Symbol* const name = cp->symbol_at(name_index);
3405     verify_legal_field_name(name, CHECK_0);
3406 
3407     const u2 descriptor_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3408     check_property(valid_symbol_at(descriptor_index),
3409       "Invalid constant pool index %u for descriptor in Record attribute in class file %s",
3410       descriptor_index, CHECK_0);
3411     const Symbol* const descr = cp->symbol_at(descriptor_index);
3412     verify_legal_field_signature(name, descr, CHECK_0);
3413 
3414     const u2 attributes_count = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3415     calculate_attr_size += 6;
3416     u2 generic_sig_index = 0;
3417     const u1* runtime_visible_annotations = NULL;
3418     int runtime_visible_annotations_length = 0;
3419     const u1* runtime_invisible_annotations = NULL;
3420     int runtime_invisible_annotations_length = 0;
3421     bool runtime_invisible_annotations_exists = false;
3422     const u1* runtime_visible_type_annotations = NULL;
3423     int runtime_visible_type_annotations_length = 0;
3424     const u1* runtime_invisible_type_annotations = NULL;
3425     int runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length = 0;
3426     bool runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists = false;
3427 
3428     // Expected attributes for record components are Signature, Runtime(In)VisibleAnnotations,
3429     // and Runtime(In)VisibleTypeAnnotations.  Other attributes are ignored.
3430     for (int y = 0; y < attributes_count; y++) {
3431       cfs->guarantee_more(6, CHECK_0);  // attribute_name_index, attribute_length
3432       const u2 attribute_name_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3433       const u4 attribute_length = cfs->get_u4_fast();
3434       calculate_attr_size += 6;
3435       check_property(
3436         valid_symbol_at(attribute_name_index),
3437         "Invalid Record attribute name index %u in class file %s",
3438         attribute_name_index, CHECK_0);
3439 
3440       const Symbol* const attribute_name = cp->symbol_at(attribute_name_index);
3441       if (attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_signature()) {
3442         if (generic_sig_index != 0) {
3443           classfile_parse_error(
3444             "Multiple Signature attributes for Record component in class file %s",
3445             CHECK_0);
3446         }
3447         if (attribute_length != 2) {
3448           classfile_parse_error(
3449             "Invalid Signature attribute length %u in Record component in class file %s",
3450             attribute_length, CHECK_0);
3451         }
3452         generic_sig_index = parse_generic_signature_attribute(cfs, CHECK_0);
3453 
3454       } else if (attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_annotations()) {
3455         if (runtime_visible_annotations != NULL) {
3456           classfile_parse_error(
3457             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleAnnotations attributes for Record component in class file %s", CHECK_0);
3458         }
3459         runtime_visible_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3460         runtime_visible_annotations = cfs->current();
3461 
3462         assert(runtime_visible_annotations != NULL, "null record component visible annotation");
3463         cfs->guarantee_more(runtime_visible_annotations_length, CHECK_0);
3464         cfs->skip_u1_fast(runtime_visible_annotations_length);
3465 
3466       } else if (attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_annotations()) {
3467         if (runtime_invisible_annotations_exists) {
3468           classfile_parse_error(
3469             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleAnnotations attributes for Record component in class file %s", CHECK_0);
3470         }
3471         runtime_invisible_annotations_exists = true;
3472         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
3473           runtime_invisible_annotations_length = attribute_length;
