3474           runtime_invisible_annotations = cfs->current();
3475           assert(runtime_invisible_annotations != NULL, "null record component invisible annotation");
3476         }
3477         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK_0);
3478 
3479       } else if (attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_type_annotations()) {
3480         if (runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL) {
3481           classfile_parse_error(
3482             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleTypeAnnotations attributes for Record component in class file %s", CHECK_0);
3483         }
3484         runtime_visible_type_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3485         runtime_visible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
3486 
3487         assert(runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL, "null record component visible type annotation");
3488         cfs->guarantee_more(runtime_visible_type_annotations_length, CHECK_0);
3489         cfs->skip_u1_fast(runtime_visible_type_annotations_length);
3490 
3491       } else if (attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_type_annotations()) {
3492         if (runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists) {
3493           classfile_parse_error(
3494             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleTypeAnnotations attributes for Record component in class file %s", CHECK_0);
3495         }
3496         runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists = true;
3497         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
3498           runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3499           runtime_invisible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
3500           assert(runtime_invisible_type_annotations != NULL, "null record component invisible type annotation");
3501         }
3502         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK_0);
3503 
3504       } else {
3505         // Skip unknown attributes
3506         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK_0);
3507       }
3508       calculate_attr_size += attribute_length;
3509     } // End of attributes For loop
3510 
3511     AnnotationArray* annotations = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_annotations,
3512                                                         runtime_visible_annotations_length,
3513                                                         runtime_invisible_annotations,
3514                                                         runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
3515                                                         CHECK_0);
3516     AnnotationArray* type_annotations = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_type_annotations,
3517                                                              runtime_visible_type_annotations_length,
3518                                                              runtime_invisible_type_annotations,
3519                                                              runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length,
3520                                                              CHECK_0);
3521 
3522     RecordComponent* record_component =
3523       RecordComponent::allocate(_loader_data, name_index, descriptor_index,
3524                                 attributes_count, generic_sig_index,
3525                                 annotations, type_annotations, CHECK_0);
3526     record_components->at_put(x, record_component);
3527   }  // End of component processing loop
3528 
3529   // Restore buffer's current position.
3530   cfs->set_current(current_mark);
3531   return calculate_attr_size;
3532 }
3533 
3534 void ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_synthetic_attribute(TRAPS) {
3535   set_class_synthetic_flag(true);
3536 }
3537 
3538 void ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_signature_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs, TRAPS) {
3539   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
3540 
3541   const u2 signature_index = cfs->get_u2(CHECK);
3542   check_property(
3543     valid_symbol_at(signature_index),
3544     "Invalid constant pool index %u in Signature attribute in class file %s",
3545     signature_index, CHECK);
3546   set_class_generic_signature_index(signature_index);
3547 }
3548 
3549 void ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_bootstrap_methods_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3550                                                                   ConstantPool* cp,
3551                                                                   u4 attribute_byte_length,
3552                                                                   TRAPS) {
3553   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
3554   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
3555 
3556   const u1* const current_start = cfs->current();
3557 
3558   guarantee_property(attribute_byte_length >= sizeof(u2),
3559                      "Invalid BootstrapMethods attribute length %u in class file %s",
3560                      attribute_byte_length,
3561                      CHECK);
3562 
3563   cfs->guarantee_more(attribute_byte_length, CHECK);
3564 
3565   const int attribute_array_length = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3566 
3567   guarantee_property(_max_bootstrap_specifier_index < attribute_array_length,
3568                      "Short length on BootstrapMethods in class file %s",
3569                      CHECK);
3570 
3571 
3572   // The attribute contains a counted array of counted tuples of shorts,
3573   // represending bootstrap specifiers:
3574   //    length*{bootstrap_method_index, argument_count*{argument_index}}
3575   const int operand_count = (attribute_byte_length - sizeof(u2)) / sizeof(u2);
3576   // operand_count = number of shorts in attr, except for leading length
3577 
3578   // The attribute is copied into a short[] array.
3579   // The array begins with a series of short[2] pairs, one for each tuple.
3580   const int index_size = (attribute_array_length * 2);
3581 
3582   Array<u2>* const operands =
3583     MetadataFactory::new_array<u2>(_loader_data, index_size + operand_count, CHECK);
3584 
3585   // Eagerly assign operands so they will be deallocated with the constant
3586   // pool if there is an error.
3587   cp->set_operands(operands);
3588 
3589   int operand_fill_index = index_size;
3590   const int cp_size = cp->length();
3591 
3592   for (int n = 0; n < attribute_array_length; n++) {
3593     // Store a 32-bit offset into the header of the operand array.
3594     ConstantPool::operand_offset_at_put(operands, n, operand_fill_index);
3595 
3596     // Read a bootstrap specifier.
3597     cfs->guarantee_more(sizeof(u2) * 2, CHECK);  // bsm, argc
3598     const u2 bootstrap_method_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3599     const u2 argument_count = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3600     check_property(
3601       valid_cp_range(bootstrap_method_index, cp_size) &&
3602       cp->tag_at(bootstrap_method_index).is_method_handle(),
3603       "bootstrap_method_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3604       bootstrap_method_index,
3605       CHECK);
3606 
3607     guarantee_property((operand_fill_index + 1 + argument_count) < operands->length(),
3608       "Invalid BootstrapMethods num_bootstrap_methods or num_bootstrap_arguments value in class file %s",
3609       CHECK);
3610 
3611     operands->at_put(operand_fill_index++, bootstrap_method_index);
3612     operands->at_put(operand_fill_index++, argument_count);
3613 
3614     cfs->guarantee_more(sizeof(u2) * argument_count, CHECK);  // argv[argc]
3615     for (int j = 0; j < argument_count; j++) {
3616       const u2 argument_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3617       check_property(
3618         valid_cp_range(argument_index, cp_size) &&
3619         cp->tag_at(argument_index).is_loadable_constant(),
3620         "argument_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3621         argument_index,
3622         CHECK);
3623       operands->at_put(operand_fill_index++, argument_index);
3624     }
3625   }
3626   guarantee_property(current_start + attribute_byte_length == cfs->current(),
3627                      "Bad length on BootstrapMethods in class file %s",
3628                      CHECK);
3629 }
3630 
3631 bool ClassFileParser::supports_records() {
3632   return _major_version == JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION &&
3633     _minor_version == JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION &&
3634     Arguments::enable_preview();
3635 }
3636 
3637 void ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_attributes(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3638                                                  ConstantPool* cp,
3639                  ClassFileParser::ClassAnnotationCollector* parsed_annotations,
3640                                                  TRAPS) {
3641   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
3642   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
3643   assert(parsed_annotations != NULL, "invariant");
3644 
3645   // Set inner classes attribute to default sentinel
3646   _inner_classes = Universe::the_empty_short_array();
3647   // Set nest members attribute to default sentinel
3648   _nest_members = Universe::the_empty_short_array();
3649   cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK);  // attributes_count
3650   u2 attributes_count = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3651   bool parsed_sourcefile_attribute = false;
3652   bool parsed_innerclasses_attribute = false;
3653   bool parsed_nest_members_attribute = false;
3654   bool parsed_nest_host_attribute = false;
3655   bool parsed_record_attribute = false;
3656   bool parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute = false;
3657   bool parsed_bootstrap_methods_attribute = false;
3658   const u1* runtime_visible_annotations = NULL;
3659   int runtime_visible_annotations_length = 0;
3660   const u1* runtime_invisible_annotations = NULL;
3661   int runtime_invisible_annotations_length = 0;
3662   const u1* runtime_visible_type_annotations = NULL;
3663   int runtime_visible_type_annotations_length = 0;
3664   const u1* runtime_invisible_type_annotations = NULL;
3665   int runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length = 0;
3666   bool runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists = false;
3667   bool runtime_invisible_annotations_exists = false;
3668   bool parsed_source_debug_ext_annotations_exist = false;
3669   const u1* inner_classes_attribute_start = NULL;
3670   u4  inner_classes_attribute_length = 0;
3671   const u1* value_types_attribute_start = NULL;
3672   u4 value_types_attribute_length = 0;
3673   u2  enclosing_method_class_index = 0;
3674   u2  enclosing_method_method_index = 0;
3675   const u1* nest_members_attribute_start = NULL;
3676   u4  nest_members_attribute_length = 0;
3677   const u1* record_attribute_start = NULL;
3678   u4  record_attribute_length = 0;
3679 
3680   // Iterate over attributes
3681   while (attributes_count--) {
3682     cfs->guarantee_more(6, CHECK);  // attribute_name_index, attribute_length
3683     const u2 attribute_name_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3684     const u4 attribute_length = cfs->get_u4_fast();
3685     check_property(
3686       valid_symbol_at(attribute_name_index),
3687       "Attribute name has bad constant pool index %u in class file %s",
3688       attribute_name_index, CHECK);
3689     const Symbol* const tag = cp->symbol_at(attribute_name_index);
3690     if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_source_file()) {
3691       // Check for SourceFile tag
3692       if (_need_verify) {
3693         guarantee_property(attribute_length == 2, "Wrong SourceFile attribute length in class file %s", CHECK);
3694       }
3695       if (parsed_sourcefile_attribute) {
3696         classfile_parse_error("Multiple SourceFile attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3697       } else {
3698         parsed_sourcefile_attribute = true;
3699       }
3700       parse_classfile_sourcefile_attribute(cfs, CHECK);
3701     } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_source_debug_extension()) {
3702       // Check for SourceDebugExtension tag
3703       if (parsed_source_debug_ext_annotations_exist) {
3704           classfile_parse_error(
3705             "Multiple SourceDebugExtension attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3706       }
3707       parsed_source_debug_ext_annotations_exist = true;
3708       parse_classfile_source_debug_extension_attribute(cfs, (int)attribute_length, CHECK);
3709     } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_inner_classes()) {
3710       // Check for InnerClasses tag
3711       if (parsed_innerclasses_attribute) {
3712         classfile_parse_error("Multiple InnerClasses attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3713       } else {
3714         parsed_innerclasses_attribute = true;
3715       }
3716       inner_classes_attribute_start = cfs->current();
3717       inner_classes_attribute_length = attribute_length;
3718       cfs->skip_u1(inner_classes_attribute_length, CHECK);
3719     } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_synthetic()) {
3720       // Check for Synthetic tag
3721       // Shouldn't we check that the synthetic flags wasn't already set? - not required in spec
3722       if (attribute_length != 0) {
3723         classfile_parse_error(
3724           "Invalid Synthetic classfile attribute length %u in class file %s",
3725           attribute_length, CHECK);
3726       }
3727       parse_classfile_synthetic_attribute(CHECK);
3728     } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_deprecated()) {
3729       // Check for Deprecatd tag - 4276120
3730       if (attribute_length != 0) {
3731         classfile_parse_error(
3732           "Invalid Deprecated classfile attribute length %u in class file %s",
3733           attribute_length, CHECK);
3734       }
3735     } else if (_major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
3736       if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_signature()) {
3737         if (_generic_signature_index != 0) {
3738           classfile_parse_error(
3739             "Multiple Signature attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3740         }
3741         if (attribute_length != 2) {
3742           classfile_parse_error(
3743             "Wrong Signature attribute length %u in class file %s",
3744             attribute_length, CHECK);
3745         }
3746         parse_classfile_signature_attribute(cfs, CHECK);
3747       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_annotations()) {
3748         if (runtime_visible_annotations != NULL) {
3749           classfile_parse_error(
3750             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleAnnotations attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3751         }
3752         runtime_visible_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3753         runtime_visible_annotations = cfs->current();
3754         assert(runtime_visible_annotations != NULL, "null visible annotations");
3755         cfs->guarantee_more(runtime_visible_annotations_length, CHECK);
3756         parse_annotations(cp,
3757                           runtime_visible_annotations,
3758                           runtime_visible_annotations_length,
3759                           parsed_annotations,
3760                           _loader_data,
3761                           CHECK);
3762         cfs->skip_u1_fast(runtime_visible_annotations_length);
3763       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_annotations()) {
3764         if (runtime_invisible_annotations_exists) {
3765           classfile_parse_error(
3766             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleAnnotations attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3767         }
3768         runtime_invisible_annotations_exists = true;
3769         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
3770           runtime_invisible_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3771           runtime_invisible_annotations = cfs->current();
3772           assert(runtime_invisible_annotations != NULL, "null invisible annotations");
3773         }
3774         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3775       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_enclosing_method()) {
3776         if (parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute) {
3777           classfile_parse_error("Multiple EnclosingMethod attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3778         } else {
3779           parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute = true;
3780         }
3781         guarantee_property(attribute_length == 4,
3782           "Wrong EnclosingMethod attribute length %u in class file %s",
3783           attribute_length, CHECK);
3784         cfs->guarantee_more(4, CHECK);  // class_index, method_index
3785         enclosing_method_class_index  = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3786         enclosing_method_method_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3787         if (enclosing_method_class_index == 0) {
3788           classfile_parse_error("Invalid class index in EnclosingMethod attribute in class file %s", CHECK);
3789         }
3790         // Validate the constant pool indices and types
3791         check_property(valid_klass_reference_at(enclosing_method_class_index),
3792           "Invalid or out-of-bounds class index in EnclosingMethod attribute in class file %s", CHECK);
3793         if (enclosing_method_method_index != 0 &&
3794             (!cp->is_within_bounds(enclosing_method_method_index) ||
3795              !cp->tag_at(enclosing_method_method_index).is_name_and_type())) {
3796           classfile_parse_error("Invalid or out-of-bounds method index in EnclosingMethod attribute in class file %s", CHECK);
3797         }
3798       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_bootstrap_methods() &&
3799                  _major_version >= Verifier::INVOKEDYNAMIC_MAJOR_VERSION) {
3800         if (parsed_bootstrap_methods_attribute) {
3801           classfile_parse_error("Multiple BootstrapMethods attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3802         }
3803         parsed_bootstrap_methods_attribute = true;
3804         parse_classfile_bootstrap_methods_attribute(cfs, cp, attribute_length, CHECK);
3805       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_type_annotations()) {
3806         if (runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL) {
3807           classfile_parse_error(
3808             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleTypeAnnotations attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3809         }
3810         runtime_visible_type_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3811         runtime_visible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
3812         assert(runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL, "null visible type annotations");
3813         // No need for the VM to parse Type annotations
3814         cfs->skip_u1(runtime_visible_type_annotations_length, CHECK);
3815       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_type_annotations()) {
3816         if (runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists) {
3817           classfile_parse_error(
3818             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleTypeAnnotations attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3819         } else {
3820           runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists = true;
3821         }
3822         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
3823           runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3824           runtime_invisible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
3825           assert(runtime_invisible_type_annotations != NULL, "null invisible type annotations");
3826         }
3827         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3828       } else if (_major_version >= JAVA_11_VERSION) {
3829         if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_nest_members()) {
3830           // Check for NestMembers tag
3831           if (parsed_nest_members_attribute) {
3832             classfile_parse_error("Multiple NestMembers attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3833           } else {
3834             parsed_nest_members_attribute = true;
3835           }
3836           if (parsed_nest_host_attribute) {
3837             classfile_parse_error("Conflicting NestHost and NestMembers attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3838           }
3839           nest_members_attribute_start = cfs->current();
3840           nest_members_attribute_length = attribute_length;
3841           cfs->skip_u1(nest_members_attribute_length, CHECK);
3842         } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_nest_host()) {
3843           if (parsed_nest_host_attribute) {
3844             classfile_parse_error("Multiple NestHost attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3845           } else {
3846             parsed_nest_host_attribute = true;
3847           }
3848           if (parsed_nest_members_attribute) {
3849             classfile_parse_error("Conflicting NestMembers and NestHost attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3850           }
3851           if (_need_verify) {
3852             guarantee_property(attribute_length == 2, "Wrong NestHost attribute length in class file %s", CHECK);
3853           }
3854           cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK);
3855           u2 class_info_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3856           check_property(
3857                          valid_klass_reference_at(class_info_index),
3858                          "Nest-host class_info_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3859                          class_info_index, CHECK);
3860           _nest_host = class_info_index;
3861         } else if (_major_version >= JAVA_14_VERSION) {
3862           if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_record()) {
3863             // Skip over Record attribute if not supported or if super class is
3864             // not java.lang.Record.
3865             if (supports_records() &&
3866                 cp->klass_name_at(_super_class_index) == vmSymbols::java_lang_Record()) {
3867               if (parsed_record_attribute) {
3868                 classfile_parse_error("Multiple Record attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3869               }
3870               // Check that class is final and not abstract.
3871               if (!_access_flags.is_final() || _access_flags.is_abstract()) {
3872                 classfile_parse_error("Record attribute in non-final or abstract class file %s", CHECK);
3873               }
3874               parsed_record_attribute = true;
3875               record_attribute_start = cfs->current();
3876               record_attribute_length = attribute_length;
3877             } else if (log_is_enabled(Info, class, record)) {
3878               // Log why the Record attribute was ignored.  Note that if the
3879               // class file version is JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION.65535 and
3880               // --enable-preview wasn't specified then a java.lang.UnsupportedClassVersionError
3881               // exception would have been thrown.
3882               ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
3883               if (supports_records()) {
3884                 log_info(class, record)(
3885                   "Ignoring Record attribute in class %s because super type is not java.lang.Record",
3886                   _class_name->as_C_string());
3887               } else {
3888                 log_info(class, record)(
3889                   "Ignoring Record attribute in class %s because class file version is not %d.65535",
3890                    _class_name->as_C_string(), JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION);
3891               }
3892             }
3893             cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3894           } else {
3895             // Unknown attribute
3896             cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3897           }
3898         } else {
3899           // Unknown attribute
3900           cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3901         }
3902       } else {
3903         // Unknown attribute
3904         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3905       }
3906     } else {
3907       // Unknown attribute
3908       cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3909     }
3910   }
3911   _class_annotations = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_annotations,
3912                                             runtime_visible_annotations_length,
3913                                             runtime_invisible_annotations,
3914                                             runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
3915                                             CHECK);
3916   _class_type_annotations = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_type_annotations,
3917                                                  runtime_visible_type_annotations_length,
3918                                                  runtime_invisible_type_annotations,
3919                                                  runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length,
3920                                                  CHECK);
3921 
3922   if (parsed_innerclasses_attribute || parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute) {
3923     const u2 num_of_classes = parse_classfile_inner_classes_attribute(
3924                             cfs,
3925                             inner_classes_attribute_start,
3926                             parsed_innerclasses_attribute,
3927                             enclosing_method_class_index,
3928                             enclosing_method_method_index,
3929                             CHECK);
3930     if (parsed_innerclasses_attribute && _need_verify && _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
3931       guarantee_property(
3932         inner_classes_attribute_length == sizeof(num_of_classes) + 4 * sizeof(u2) * num_of_classes,
3933         "Wrong InnerClasses attribute length in class file %s", CHECK);
3934     }
3935   }
3936 
3937   if (parsed_nest_members_attribute) {
3938     const u2 num_of_classes = parse_classfile_nest_members_attribute(
3939                             cfs,
3940                             nest_members_attribute_start,
3941                             CHECK);
3942     if (_need_verify) {
3943       guarantee_property(
3944         nest_members_attribute_length == sizeof(num_of_classes) + sizeof(u2) * num_of_classes,
3945         "Wrong NestMembers attribute length in class file %s", CHECK);
3946     }
3947   }
3948 
3949   if (parsed_record_attribute) {
3950     const unsigned int calculated_attr_length = parse_classfile_record_attribute(
3951                             cfs,
3952                             cp,
3953                             record_attribute_start,
3954                             CHECK);
3955     if (_need_verify) {
3956       guarantee_property(record_attribute_length == calculated_attr_length,
3957                          "Record attribute has wrong length in class file %s",
3958                          CHECK);
3959     }
3960   }
3961 
3962   if (_max_bootstrap_specifier_index >= 0) {
3963     guarantee_property(parsed_bootstrap_methods_attribute,
3964                        "Missing BootstrapMethods attribute in class file %s", CHECK);
3965   }
3966 }
3967 
3968 void ClassFileParser::apply_parsed_class_attributes(InstanceKlass* k) {
3969   assert(k != NULL, "invariant");
3970 
3971   if (_synthetic_flag)
3972     k->set_is_synthetic();
3973   if (_sourcefile_index != 0) {
3974     k->set_source_file_name_index(_sourcefile_index);
3975   }
3976   if (_generic_signature_index != 0) {
3977     k->set_generic_signature_index(_generic_signature_index);
3978   }
3979   if (_sde_buffer != NULL) {
3980     k->set_source_debug_extension(_sde_buffer, _sde_length);
3981   }
3982 }
3983 
3984 // Create the Annotations object that will
3985 // hold the annotations array for the Klass.
3986 void ClassFileParser::create_combined_annotations(TRAPS) {
3987     if (_class_annotations == NULL &&
3988         _class_type_annotations == NULL &&
3989         _fields_annotations == NULL &&
3990         _fields_type_annotations == NULL) {
3991       // Don't create the Annotations object unnecessarily.
3992       return;
3993     }
3994 
3995     Annotations* const annotations = Annotations::allocate(_loader_data, CHECK);
3996     annotations->set_class_annotations(_class_annotations);
3997     annotations->set_class_type_annotations(_class_type_annotations);
3998     annotations->set_fields_annotations(_fields_annotations);
3999     annotations->set_fields_type_annotations(_fields_type_annotations);
4000 
4001     // This is the Annotations object that will be
4002     // assigned to InstanceKlass being constructed.
4003     _combined_annotations = annotations;
4004 
4005     // The annotations arrays below has been transfered the
4006     // _combined_annotations so these fields can now be cleared.
4007     _class_annotations       = NULL;
4008     _class_type_annotations  = NULL;
4009     _fields_annotations      = NULL;
4010     _fields_type_annotations = NULL;
4011 }
4012 
4013 // Transfer ownership of metadata allocated to the InstanceKlass.
4014 void ClassFileParser::apply_parsed_class_metadata(
4015                                             InstanceKlass* this_klass,
4016                                             int java_fields_count,
4017                                             TRAPS) {
4018   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
4019 
4020   _cp->set_pool_holder(this_klass);
4021   this_klass->set_constants(_cp);
4022   this_klass->set_fields(_fields, java_fields_count);
4023   this_klass->set_methods(_methods);
4024   this_klass->set_inner_classes(_inner_classes);
4025   this_klass->set_nest_members(_nest_members);
4026   this_klass->set_nest_host_index(_nest_host);
4027   this_klass->set_local_interfaces(_local_interfaces);
4028   this_klass->set_annotations(_combined_annotations);
4029   this_klass->set_record_components(_record_components);
4030   // Delay the setting of _transitive_interfaces until after initialize_supers() in
4031   // fill_instance_klass(). It is because the _transitive_interfaces may be shared with
4032   // its _super. If an OOM occurs while loading the current klass, its _super field
4033   // may not have been set. When GC tries to free the klass, the _transitive_interfaces
4034   // may be deallocated mistakenly in InstanceKlass::deallocate_interfaces(). Subsequent
4035   // dereferences to the deallocated _transitive_interfaces will result in a crash.
4036 
4037   // Clear out these fields so they don't get deallocated by the destructor
4038   clear_class_metadata();
4039 }
4040 
4041 AnnotationArray* ClassFileParser::assemble_annotations(const u1* const runtime_visible_annotations,
4042                                                        int runtime_visible_annotations_length,
4043                                                        const u1* const runtime_invisible_annotations,
4044                                                        int runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
4045                                                        TRAPS) {
4046   AnnotationArray* annotations = NULL;
4047   if (runtime_visible_annotations != NULL ||
4048       runtime_invisible_annotations != NULL) {
4049     annotations = MetadataFactory::new_array<u1>(_loader_data,
4050                                           runtime_visible_annotations_length +
4051                                           runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
4052                                           CHECK_(annotations));
4053     if (runtime_visible_annotations != NULL) {
4054       for (int i = 0; i < runtime_visible_annotations_length; i++) {
4055         annotations->at_put(i, runtime_visible_annotations[i]);
4056       }
4057     }
4058     if (runtime_invisible_annotations != NULL) {
4059       for (int i = 0; i < runtime_invisible_annotations_length; i++) {
4060         int append = runtime_visible_annotations_length+i;
4061         annotations->at_put(append, runtime_invisible_annotations[i]);
4062       }
4063     }
4064   }
4065   return annotations;
4066 }
4067 
4068 const InstanceKlass* ClassFileParser::parse_super_class(ConstantPool* const cp,
4069                                                         const int super_class_index,
4070                                                         const bool need_verify,
4071                                                         TRAPS) {
4072   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
4073   const InstanceKlass* super_klass = NULL;
4074 
4075   if (super_class_index == 0) {
4076     check_property(_class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Object()
4077                    || (_access_flags.get_flags() & JVM_ACC_VALUE),
4078                    "Invalid superclass index %u in class file %s",
4079                    super_class_index,
4080                    CHECK_NULL);
4081   } else {
4082     check_property(valid_klass_reference_at(super_class_index),
4083                    "Invalid superclass index %u in class file %s",
4084                    super_class_index,
4085                    CHECK_NULL);
4086     // The class name should be legal because it is checked when parsing constant pool.
4087     // However, make sure it is not an array type.
4088     bool is_array = false;
4089     if (cp->tag_at(super_class_index).is_klass()) {
4090       super_klass = InstanceKlass::cast(cp->resolved_klass_at(super_class_index));
4091       if (need_verify)
4092         is_array = super_klass->is_array_klass();
4093     } else if (need_verify) {
4094       is_array = (cp->klass_name_at(super_class_index)->char_at(0) == JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY);
4095     }
4096     if (need_verify) {
4097       guarantee_property(!is_array,
4098                         "Bad superclass name in class file %s", CHECK_NULL);
4099     }
4100   }
4101   return super_klass;
4102 }
4103 
4104 #ifndef PRODUCT
4105 static void print_field_layout(const Symbol* name,
4106                                Array<u2>* fields,
4107                                ConstantPool* cp,
4108                                int instance_size,
4109                                int instance_fields_start,
4110                                int instance_fields_end,
4111                                int static_fields_end) {
4112 
4113   assert(name != NULL, "invariant");
4114 
4115   tty->print("%s: field layout\n", name->as_klass_external_name());
4116   tty->print("  @%3d %s\n", instance_fields_start, "--- instance fields start ---");
4117   for (AllFieldStream fs(fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4118     if (!fs.access_flags().is_static()) {
4119       tty->print("  @%3d \"%s\" %s\n",
4120         fs.offset(),
4121         fs.name()->as_klass_external_name(),
4122         fs.signature()->as_klass_external_name());
4123     }
4124   }
4125   tty->print("  @%3d %s\n", instance_fields_end, "--- instance fields end ---");
4126   tty->print("  @%3d %s\n", instance_size * wordSize, "--- instance ends ---");
4127   tty->print("  @%3d %s\n", InstanceMirrorKlass::offset_of_static_fields(), "--- static fields start ---");
4128   for (AllFieldStream fs(fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4129     if (fs.access_flags().is_static()) {
4130       tty->print("  @%3d \"%s\" %s\n",
4131         fs.offset(),
4132         fs.name()->as_klass_external_name(),
4133         fs.signature()->as_klass_external_name());
4134     }
4135   }
4136   tty->print("  @%3d %s\n", static_fields_end, "--- static fields end ---");
4137   tty->print("\n");
4138 }
4139 #endif
4140 
4141 OopMapBlocksBuilder::OopMapBlocksBuilder(unsigned int max_blocks) {
4142   _max_nonstatic_oop_maps = max_blocks;
4143   _nonstatic_oop_map_count = 0;
4144   if (max_blocks == 0) {
4145     _nonstatic_oop_maps = NULL;
4146   } else {
4147     _nonstatic_oop_maps =
4148         NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY(OopMapBlock, _max_nonstatic_oop_maps);
4149     memset(_nonstatic_oop_maps, 0, sizeof(OopMapBlock) * max_blocks);
4150   }
4151 }
4152 
4153 OopMapBlock* OopMapBlocksBuilder::last_oop_map() const {
4154   assert(_nonstatic_oop_map_count > 0, "Has no oop maps");
4155   return _nonstatic_oop_maps + (_nonstatic_oop_map_count - 1);
4156 }
4157 
4158 // addition of super oop maps
4159 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::initialize_inherited_blocks(OopMapBlock* blocks, unsigned int nof_blocks) {
4160   assert(nof_blocks && _nonstatic_oop_map_count == 0 &&
4161          nof_blocks <= _max_nonstatic_oop_maps, "invariant");
4162 
4163   memcpy(_nonstatic_oop_maps, blocks, sizeof(OopMapBlock) * nof_blocks);
4164   _nonstatic_oop_map_count += nof_blocks;
4165 }
4166 
4167 // collection of oops
4168 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::add(int offset, int count) {
4169   if (_nonstatic_oop_map_count == 0) {
4170     _nonstatic_oop_map_count++;
4171   }
4172   OopMapBlock* nonstatic_oop_map = last_oop_map();
4173   if (nonstatic_oop_map->count() == 0) {  // Unused map, set it up
4174     nonstatic_oop_map->set_offset(offset);
4175     nonstatic_oop_map->set_count(count);
4176   } else if (nonstatic_oop_map->is_contiguous(offset)) { // contiguous, add
4177     nonstatic_oop_map->increment_count(count);
4178   } else { // Need a new one...
4179     _nonstatic_oop_map_count++;
4180     assert(_nonstatic_oop_map_count <= _max_nonstatic_oop_maps, "range check");
4181     nonstatic_oop_map = last_oop_map();
4182     nonstatic_oop_map->set_offset(offset);
4183     nonstatic_oop_map->set_count(count);
4184   }
4185 }
4186 
4187 // general purpose copy, e.g. into allocated instanceKlass
4188 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::copy(OopMapBlock* dst) {
4189   if (_nonstatic_oop_map_count != 0) {
4190     memcpy(dst, _nonstatic_oop_maps, sizeof(OopMapBlock) * _nonstatic_oop_map_count);
4191   }
4192 }
4193 
4194 // Sort and compact adjacent blocks
4195 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::compact() {
4196   if (_nonstatic_oop_map_count <= 1) {
4197     return;
4198   }
4199   /*
4200    * Since field layout sneeks in oops before values, we will be able to condense
4201    * blocks. There is potential to compact between super, own refs and values
4202    * containing refs.
4203    *
4204    * Currently compaction is slightly limited due to values being 8 byte aligned.
4205    * This may well change: FixMe if it doesn't, the code below is fairly general purpose
4206    * and maybe it doesn't need to be.
4207    */
4208   qsort(_nonstatic_oop_maps, _nonstatic_oop_map_count, sizeof(OopMapBlock),
4209         (_sort_Fn)OopMapBlock::compare_offset);
4210   if (_nonstatic_oop_map_count < 2) {
4211     return;
4212   }
4213 
4214   // Make a temp copy, and iterate through and copy back into the original
4215   ResourceMark rm;
4216   OopMapBlock* oop_maps_copy =
4217       NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY(OopMapBlock, _nonstatic_oop_map_count);
4218   OopMapBlock* oop_maps_copy_end = oop_maps_copy + _nonstatic_oop_map_count;
4219   copy(oop_maps_copy);
4220   OopMapBlock* nonstatic_oop_map = _nonstatic_oop_maps;
4221   unsigned int new_count = 1;
4222   oop_maps_copy++;
4223   while(oop_maps_copy < oop_maps_copy_end) {
4224     assert(nonstatic_oop_map->offset() < oop_maps_copy->offset(), "invariant");
4225     if (nonstatic_oop_map->is_contiguous(oop_maps_copy->offset())) {
4226       nonstatic_oop_map->increment_count(oop_maps_copy->count());
4227     } else {
4228       nonstatic_oop_map++;
4229       new_count++;
4230       nonstatic_oop_map->set_offset(oop_maps_copy->offset());
4231       nonstatic_oop_map->set_count(oop_maps_copy->count());
4232     }
4233     oop_maps_copy++;
4234   }
4235   assert(new_count <= _nonstatic_oop_map_count, "end up with more maps after compact() ?");
4236   _nonstatic_oop_map_count = new_count;
4237 }
4238 
4239 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::print_on(outputStream* st) const {
4240   st->print_cr("  OopMapBlocks: %3d  /%3d", _nonstatic_oop_map_count, _max_nonstatic_oop_maps);
4241   if (_nonstatic_oop_map_count > 0) {
4242     OopMapBlock* map = _nonstatic_oop_maps;
4243     OopMapBlock* last_map = last_oop_map();
4244     assert(map <= last_map, "Last less than first");
4245     while (map <= last_map) {
4246       st->print_cr("    Offset: %3d  -%3d Count: %3d", map->offset(),
4247                    map->offset() + map->offset_span() - heapOopSize, map->count());
4248       map++;
4249     }
4250   }
4251 }
4252 
4253 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::print_value_on(outputStream* st) const {
4254   print_on(st);
4255 }
4256 
4257 void ClassFileParser::throwValueTypeLimitation(THREAD_AND_LOCATION_DECL,
4258                                                const char* msg,
4259                                                const Symbol* name,
4260                                                const Symbol* sig) const {
4261 
4262   ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
4263   if (name == NULL || sig == NULL) {
4264     Exceptions::fthrow(THREAD_AND_LOCATION_ARGS,
4265         vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
4266         "class: %s - %s", _class_name->as_C_string(), msg);
4267   }
4268   else {
4269     Exceptions::fthrow(THREAD_AND_LOCATION_ARGS,
4270         vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
4271         "\"%s\" sig: \"%s\" class: %s - %s", name->as_C_string(), sig->as_C_string(),
4272         _class_name->as_C_string(), msg);
4273   }
4274 }
4275 
4276 // Layout fields and fill in FieldLayoutInfo.  Could use more refactoring!
4277 void ClassFileParser::layout_fields(ConstantPool* cp,
4278                                     const FieldAllocationCount* fac,
4279                                     const ClassAnnotationCollector* parsed_annotations,
4280                                     FieldLayoutInfo* info,
4281                                     TRAPS) {
4282 
4283   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
4284 
4285   // Field size and offset computation
4286   int nonstatic_field_size = _super_klass == NULL ? 0 :
4287                                _super_klass->nonstatic_field_size();
4288   int next_nonstatic_valuetype_offset = 0;
4289   int first_nonstatic_valuetype_offset = 0;
4290 
4291   // Fields that are value types are handled differently depending if they are static or not:
4292   // - static fields are oops
4293   // - non-static fields are embedded
4294 
4295   // Count the contended fields by type.
4296   //
4297   // We ignore static fields, because @Contended is not supported for them.
4298   // The layout code below will also ignore the static fields.
4299   int nonstatic_contended_count = 0;
4300   FieldAllocationCount fac_contended;
4301   for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4302     FieldAllocationType atype = (FieldAllocationType) fs.allocation_type();
4303     if (fs.is_contended()) {
4304       fac_contended.count[atype]++;
4305       if (!fs.access_flags().is_static()) {
4306         nonstatic_contended_count++;
4307       }
4308     }
4309   }
4310 
4311 
4312   // Calculate the starting byte offsets
4313   int next_static_oop_offset    = InstanceMirrorKlass::offset_of_static_fields();
4314   // Value types in static fields are not embedded, they are handled with oops
4315   int next_static_double_offset = next_static_oop_offset +
4316                                   ((fac->count[STATIC_OOP] + fac->count[STATIC_FLATTENABLE]) * heapOopSize);
4317   if (fac->count[STATIC_DOUBLE]) {
4318     next_static_double_offset = align_up(next_static_double_offset, BytesPerLong);
4319   }
4320 
4321   int next_static_word_offset   = next_static_double_offset +
4322                                     ((fac->count[STATIC_DOUBLE]) * BytesPerLong);
4323   int next_static_short_offset  = next_static_word_offset +
4324                                     ((fac->count[STATIC_WORD]) * BytesPerInt);
4325   int next_static_byte_offset   = next_static_short_offset +
4326                                   ((fac->count[STATIC_SHORT]) * BytesPerShort);
4327 
4328   int nonstatic_fields_start  = instanceOopDesc::base_offset_in_bytes() +
4329                                 nonstatic_field_size * heapOopSize;
4330 
4331   // First field of value types is aligned on a long boundary in order to ease
4332   // in-lining of value types (with header removal) in packed arrays and
4333   // flatten value types
4334   int initial_value_type_padding = 0;
4335   if (is_value_type()) {
4336     int old = nonstatic_fields_start;
4337     nonstatic_fields_start = align_up(nonstatic_fields_start, BytesPerLong);
4338     initial_value_type_padding = nonstatic_fields_start - old;
4339   }
4340 
4341   int next_nonstatic_field_offset = nonstatic_fields_start;
4342 
4343   const bool is_contended_class     = parsed_annotations->is_contended();
4344 
4345   // Class is contended, pad before all the fields
4346   if (is_contended_class) {
4347     next_nonstatic_field_offset += ContendedPaddingWidth;
4348   }
4349 
4350   // Temporary value types restrictions
4351   if (is_value_type()) {
4352     if (is_contended_class) {
4353       throwValueTypeLimitation(THREAD_AND_LOCATION, "Inline Types do not support @Contended annotation yet");
4354       return;
4355     }
4356   }
4357 
4358   // Compute the non-contended fields count.
4359   // The packing code below relies on these counts to determine if some field
4360   // can be squeezed into the alignment gap. Contended fields are obviously
4361   // exempt from that.
4362   unsigned int nonstatic_double_count = fac->count[NONSTATIC_DOUBLE] - fac_contended.count[NONSTATIC_DOUBLE];
4363   unsigned int nonstatic_word_count   = fac->count[NONSTATIC_WORD]   - fac_contended.count[NONSTATIC_WORD];
4364   unsigned int nonstatic_short_count  = fac->count[NONSTATIC_SHORT]  - fac_contended.count[NONSTATIC_SHORT];
4365   unsigned int nonstatic_byte_count   = fac->count[NONSTATIC_BYTE]   - fac_contended.count[NONSTATIC_BYTE];
4366   unsigned int nonstatic_oop_count    = fac->count[NONSTATIC_OOP]    - fac_contended.count[NONSTATIC_OOP];
4367 
4368   int static_value_type_count = 0;
4369   int nonstatic_value_type_count = 0;
4370   int* nonstatic_value_type_indexes = NULL;
4371   Klass** nonstatic_value_type_klasses = NULL;
4372   unsigned int value_type_oop_map_count = 0;
4373   int not_flattened_value_types = 0;
4374   int not_atomic_value_types = 0;
4375 
4376   int max_nonstatic_value_type = fac->count[NONSTATIC_FLATTENABLE] + 1;
4377 
4378   nonstatic_value_type_indexes = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(THREAD, int,
4379                                                               max_nonstatic_value_type);
4380   for (int i = 0; i < max_nonstatic_value_type; i++) {
4381     nonstatic_value_type_indexes[i] = -1;
4382   }
4383   nonstatic_value_type_klasses = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(THREAD, Klass*,
4384                                                               max_nonstatic_value_type);
4385 
4386   for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, _cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4387     if (fs.allocation_type() == STATIC_FLATTENABLE) {
4388       ResourceMark rm;
4389       if (!fs.signature()->is_Q_signature()) {
4390         THROW(vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError());
4391       }
4392       static_value_type_count++;
4393     } else if (fs.allocation_type() == NONSTATIC_FLATTENABLE) {
4394       // Pre-resolve the flattenable field and check for value type circularity issues.
4395       ResourceMark rm;
4396       if (!fs.signature()->is_Q_signature()) {
4397         THROW(vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError());
4398       }
4399       Klass* klass =
4400         SystemDictionary::resolve_flattenable_field_or_fail(&fs,
4401                                                             Handle(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader()),
4402                                                             _protection_domain, true, CHECK);
4403       assert(klass != NULL, "Sanity check");
4404       if (!klass->access_flags().is_value_type()) {
4405         THROW(vmSymbols::java_lang_IncompatibleClassChangeError());
4406       }
4407       ValueKlass* vk = ValueKlass::cast(klass);
4408       // Conditions to apply flattening or not should be defined in a single place
4409       bool too_big_to_flatten = (ValueFieldMaxFlatSize >= 0 &&
4410                                  (vk->size_helper() * HeapWordSize) > ValueFieldMaxFlatSize);
4411       bool too_atomic_to_flatten = vk->is_declared_atomic();
4412       bool too_volatile_to_flatten = fs.access_flags().is_volatile();
4413       if (vk->is_naturally_atomic()) {
4414         too_atomic_to_flatten = false;
4415         //too_volatile_to_flatten = false; //FIXME
4416         // volatile fields are currently never flattened, this could change in the future
4417       }
4418       if (!(too_big_to_flatten | too_atomic_to_flatten | too_volatile_to_flatten)) {
4419         nonstatic_value_type_indexes[nonstatic_value_type_count] = fs.index();
4420         nonstatic_value_type_klasses[nonstatic_value_type_count] = klass;
4421         nonstatic_value_type_count++;
4422 
4423         ValueKlass* vklass = ValueKlass::cast(klass);
4424         if (vklass->contains_oops()) {
4425           value_type_oop_map_count += vklass->nonstatic_oop_map_count();
4426         }
4427         fs.set_flattened(true);
4428         if (!vk->is_atomic()) {  // flat and non-atomic: take note
4429           not_atomic_value_types++;
4430         }
4431       } else {
4432         not_flattened_value_types++;
4433         fs.set_flattened(false);
4434       }
4435     }
4436   }
4437 
4438   // Adjusting non_static_oop_count to take into account not flattened value types;
4439   nonstatic_oop_count += not_flattened_value_types;
4440 
4441   // Total non-static fields count, including every contended field
4442   unsigned int nonstatic_fields_count = fac->count[NONSTATIC_DOUBLE] + fac->count[NONSTATIC_WORD] +
4443                                         fac->count[NONSTATIC_SHORT] + fac->count[NONSTATIC_BYTE] +
4444                                         fac->count[NONSTATIC_OOP] + fac->count[NONSTATIC_FLATTENABLE];
4445 
4446   const bool super_has_nonstatic_fields =
4447           (_super_klass != NULL && _super_klass->has_nonstatic_fields());
4448   const bool has_nonstatic_fields =
4449     super_has_nonstatic_fields || (nonstatic_fields_count != 0);
4450   const bool has_nonstatic_value_fields = nonstatic_value_type_count > 0;
4451 
4452   if (is_value_type() && (!has_nonstatic_fields)) {
4453     // There are a number of fixes required throughout the type system and JIT
4454     throwValueTypeLimitation(THREAD_AND_LOCATION, "Inline Types do not support zero instance size yet");
4455     return;
4456   }
4457 
4458   // Prepare list of oops for oop map generation.
4459   //
4460   // "offset" and "count" lists are describing the set of contiguous oop
4461   // regions. offset[i] is the start of the i-th region, which then has
4462   // count[i] oops following. Before we know how many regions are required,
4463   // we pessimistically allocate the maps to fit all the oops into the
4464   // distinct regions.
4465   //
4466   int super_oop_map_count = (_super_klass == NULL) ? 0 :_super_klass->nonstatic_oop_map_count();
4467   int max_oop_map_count =
4468       super_oop_map_count +
4469       fac->count[NONSTATIC_OOP] +
4470       value_type_oop_map_count +
4471       not_flattened_value_types;
4472 
4473   OopMapBlocksBuilder* nonstatic_oop_maps = new OopMapBlocksBuilder(max_oop_map_count);
4474   if (super_oop_map_count > 0) {
4475     nonstatic_oop_maps->initialize_inherited_blocks(_super_klass->start_of_nonstatic_oop_maps(),
4476                                                     _super_klass->nonstatic_oop_map_count());
4477   }
4478 
4479   int first_nonstatic_oop_offset = 0; // will be set for first oop field
4480 
4481   bool compact_fields  = true;
4482   bool allocate_oops_first = false;
4483 
4484   // The next classes have predefined hard-coded fields offsets
4485   // (see in JavaClasses::compute_hard_coded_offsets()).
4486   // Use default fields allocation order for them.
4487   if (_loader_data->class_loader() == NULL &&
4488       (_class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_ref_Reference() ||
4489        _class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Boolean() ||
4490        _class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Character() ||
4491        _class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Float() ||
4492        _class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Double() ||
4493        _class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Byte() ||
4494        _class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Short() ||
4495        _class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Integer() ||
4496        _class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Long())) {
4497     allocate_oops_first = true;     // Allocate oops first
4498     compact_fields   = false; // Don't compact fields
4499   }
4500 
4501   int next_nonstatic_oop_offset = 0;
4502   int next_nonstatic_double_offset = 0;
4503 
4504   // Rearrange fields for a given allocation style
4505   if (allocate_oops_first) {
4506     // Fields order: oops, longs/doubles, ints, shorts/chars, bytes, padded fields
4507     next_nonstatic_oop_offset    = next_nonstatic_field_offset;
4508     next_nonstatic_double_offset = next_nonstatic_oop_offset +
4509                                     (nonstatic_oop_count * heapOopSize);
4510   } else {
4511     // Fields order: longs/doubles, ints, shorts/chars, bytes, oops, padded fields
4512     next_nonstatic_double_offset = next_nonstatic_field_offset;
4513   }
4514 
4515   int nonstatic_oop_space_count   = 0;
4516   int nonstatic_word_space_count  = 0;
4517   int nonstatic_short_space_count = 0;
4518   int nonstatic_byte_space_count  = 0;
4519   int nonstatic_oop_space_offset = 0;
4520   int nonstatic_word_space_offset = 0;
4521   int nonstatic_short_space_offset = 0;
4522   int nonstatic_byte_space_offset = 0;
4523 
4524   // Try to squeeze some of the fields into the gaps due to
4525   // long/double alignment.
4526   if (nonstatic_double_count > 0) {
4527     int offset = next_nonstatic_double_offset;
4528     next_nonstatic_double_offset = align_up(offset, BytesPerLong);
4529     if (compact_fields && offset != next_nonstatic_double_offset) {
4530       // Allocate available fields into the gap before double field.
4531       int length = next_nonstatic_double_offset - offset;
4532       assert(length == BytesPerInt, "");
4533       nonstatic_word_space_offset = offset;
4534       if (nonstatic_word_count > 0) {
4535         nonstatic_word_count      -= 1;
4536         nonstatic_word_space_count = 1; // Only one will fit
4537         length -= BytesPerInt;
4538         offset += BytesPerInt;
4539       }
4540       nonstatic_short_space_offset = offset;
4541       while (length >= BytesPerShort && nonstatic_short_count > 0) {
4542         nonstatic_short_count       -= 1;
4543         nonstatic_short_space_count += 1;
4544         length -= BytesPerShort;
4545         offset += BytesPerShort;
4546       }
4547       nonstatic_byte_space_offset = offset;
4548       while (length > 0 && nonstatic_byte_count > 0) {
4549         nonstatic_byte_count       -= 1;
4550         nonstatic_byte_space_count += 1;
4551         length -= 1;
4552       }
4553       // Allocate oop field in the gap if there are no other fields for that.
4554       nonstatic_oop_space_offset = offset;
4555       if (length >= heapOopSize && nonstatic_oop_count > 0 &&
4556           !allocate_oops_first) { // when oop fields not first
4557         nonstatic_oop_count      -= 1;
4558         nonstatic_oop_space_count = 1; // Only one will fit
4559         length -= heapOopSize;
4560         offset += heapOopSize;
4561       }
4562     }
4563   }
4564 
4565   int next_nonstatic_word_offset = next_nonstatic_double_offset +
4566                                      (nonstatic_double_count * BytesPerLong);
4567   int next_nonstatic_short_offset = next_nonstatic_word_offset +
4568                                       (nonstatic_word_count * BytesPerInt);
4569   int next_nonstatic_byte_offset = next_nonstatic_short_offset +
4570                                      (nonstatic_short_count * BytesPerShort);
4571   int next_nonstatic_padded_offset = next_nonstatic_byte_offset +
4572                                        nonstatic_byte_count;
4573 
4574   // let oops jump before padding with this allocation style
4575   if (!allocate_oops_first) {
4576     next_nonstatic_oop_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4577     if( nonstatic_oop_count > 0 ) {
4578       next_nonstatic_oop_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_oop_offset, heapOopSize);
4579     }
4580     next_nonstatic_padded_offset = next_nonstatic_oop_offset + (nonstatic_oop_count * heapOopSize);
4581   }
4582 
4583   // Aligning embedded value types
4584   // bug below, the current algorithm to layout embedded value types always put them at the
4585   // end of the layout, which doesn't match the different allocation policies the VM is
4586   // supposed to provide => FixMe
4587   // Note also that the current alignment policy is to make each value type starting on a
4588   // 64 bits boundary. This could be optimized later. For instance, it could be nice to
4589   // align value types according to their most constrained internal type.
4590   next_nonstatic_valuetype_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, BytesPerLong);
4591   int next_value_type_index = 0;
4592 
4593   // Iterate over fields again and compute correct offsets.
4594   // The field allocation type was temporarily stored in the offset slot.
4595   // oop fields are located before non-oop fields (static and non-static).
4596   for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4597 
4598     // skip already laid out fields
4599     if (fs.is_offset_set()) continue;
4600 
4601     // contended instance fields are handled below
4602     if (fs.is_contended() && !fs.access_flags().is_static()) continue;
4603 
4604     int real_offset = 0;
4605     const FieldAllocationType atype = (const FieldAllocationType) fs.allocation_type();
4606 
4607     // pack the rest of the fields
4608     switch (atype) {
4609       // Value types in static fields are handled with oops
4610       case STATIC_FLATTENABLE:   // Fallthrough
4611       case STATIC_OOP:
4612         real_offset = next_static_oop_offset;
4613         next_static_oop_offset += heapOopSize;
4614         break;
4615       case STATIC_BYTE:
4616         real_offset = next_static_byte_offset;
4617         next_static_byte_offset += 1;
4618         break;
4619       case STATIC_SHORT:
4620         real_offset = next_static_short_offset;
4621         next_static_short_offset += BytesPerShort;
4622         break;
4623       case STATIC_WORD:
4624         real_offset = next_static_word_offset;
4625         next_static_word_offset += BytesPerInt;
4626         break;
4627       case STATIC_DOUBLE:
4628         real_offset = next_static_double_offset;
4629         next_static_double_offset += BytesPerLong;
4630         break;
4631       case NONSTATIC_FLATTENABLE:
4632         if (fs.is_flattened()) {
4633           Klass* klass = nonstatic_value_type_klasses[next_value_type_index];
4634           assert(klass != NULL, "Klass should have been loaded and resolved earlier");
4635           assert(klass->access_flags().is_value_type(),"Must be a value type");
4636           ValueKlass* vklass = ValueKlass::cast(klass);
4637           real_offset = next_nonstatic_valuetype_offset;
4638           next_nonstatic_valuetype_offset += (vklass->size_helper()) * wordSize - vklass->first_field_offset();
4639           // aligning next value type on a 64 bits boundary
4640           next_nonstatic_valuetype_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_valuetype_offset, BytesPerLong);
4641           next_value_type_index += 1;
4642 
4643           if (vklass->contains_oops()) { // add flatten oop maps
4644             int diff = real_offset - vklass->first_field_offset();
4645             const OopMapBlock* map = vklass->start_of_nonstatic_oop_maps();
4646             const OopMapBlock* const last_map = map + vklass->nonstatic_oop_map_count();
4647             while (map < last_map) {
4648               nonstatic_oop_maps->add(map->offset() + diff, map->count());
4649               map++;
4650             }
4651           }
4652           break;
4653         } else {
4654           // Fall through
4655         }
4656       case NONSTATIC_OOP:
4657         if( nonstatic_oop_space_count > 0 ) {
4658           real_offset = nonstatic_oop_space_offset;
4659           nonstatic_oop_space_offset += heapOopSize;
4660           nonstatic_oop_space_count  -= 1;
4661         } else {
4662           real_offset = next_nonstatic_oop_offset;
4663           next_nonstatic_oop_offset += heapOopSize;
4664         }
4665         nonstatic_oop_maps->add(real_offset, 1);
4666         break;
4667       case NONSTATIC_BYTE:
4668         if( nonstatic_byte_space_count > 0 ) {
4669           real_offset = nonstatic_byte_space_offset;
4670           nonstatic_byte_space_offset += 1;
4671           nonstatic_byte_space_count  -= 1;
4672         } else {
4673           real_offset = next_nonstatic_byte_offset;
4674           next_nonstatic_byte_offset += 1;
4675         }
4676         break;
4677       case NONSTATIC_SHORT:
4678         if( nonstatic_short_space_count > 0 ) {
4679           real_offset = nonstatic_short_space_offset;
4680           nonstatic_short_space_offset += BytesPerShort;
4681           nonstatic_short_space_count  -= 1;
4682         } else {
4683           real_offset = next_nonstatic_short_offset;
4684           next_nonstatic_short_offset += BytesPerShort;
4685         }
4686         break;
4687       case NONSTATIC_WORD:
4688         if( nonstatic_word_space_count > 0 ) {
4689           real_offset = nonstatic_word_space_offset;
4690           nonstatic_word_space_offset += BytesPerInt;
4691           nonstatic_word_space_count  -= 1;
4692         } else {
4693           real_offset = next_nonstatic_word_offset;
4694           next_nonstatic_word_offset += BytesPerInt;
4695         }
4696         break;
4697       case NONSTATIC_DOUBLE:
4698         real_offset = next_nonstatic_double_offset;
4699         next_nonstatic_double_offset += BytesPerLong;
4700         break;
4701       default:
4702         ShouldNotReachHere();
4703     }
4704     fs.set_offset(real_offset);
4705   }
4706 
4707 
4708   // Handle the contended cases.
4709   //
4710   // Each contended field should not intersect the cache line with another contended field.
4711   // In the absence of alignment information, we end up with pessimistically separating
4712   // the fields with full-width padding.
4713   //
4714   // Additionally, this should not break alignment for the fields, so we round the alignment up
4715   // for each field.
4716   if (nonstatic_contended_count > 0) {
4717 
4718     // if there is at least one contended field, we need to have pre-padding for them
4719     next_nonstatic_padded_offset += ContendedPaddingWidth;
4720 
4721     // collect all contended groups
4722     ResourceBitMap bm(cp->size());
4723     for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4724       // skip already laid out fields
4725       if (fs.is_offset_set()) continue;
4726 
4727       if (fs.is_contended()) {
4728         bm.set_bit(fs.contended_group());
4729       }
4730     }
4731 
4732     int current_group = -1;
4733     while ((current_group = (int)bm.get_next_one_offset(current_group + 1)) != (int)bm.size()) {
4734 
4735       for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4736 
4737         // skip already laid out fields
4738         if (fs.is_offset_set()) continue;
4739 
4740         // skip non-contended fields and fields from different group
4741         if (!fs.is_contended() || (fs.contended_group() != current_group)) continue;
4742 
4743         // handle statics below
4744         if (fs.access_flags().is_static()) continue;
4745 
4746         int real_offset = 0;
4747         FieldAllocationType atype = (FieldAllocationType) fs.allocation_type();
4748 
4749         switch (atype) {
4750           case NONSTATIC_BYTE:
4751             next_nonstatic_padded_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, 1);
4752             real_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4753             next_nonstatic_padded_offset += 1;
4754             break;
4755 
4756           case NONSTATIC_SHORT:
4757             next_nonstatic_padded_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, BytesPerShort);
4758             real_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4759             next_nonstatic_padded_offset += BytesPerShort;
4760             break;
4761 
4762           case NONSTATIC_WORD:
4763             next_nonstatic_padded_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, BytesPerInt);
4764             real_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4765             next_nonstatic_padded_offset += BytesPerInt;
4766             break;
4767 
4768           case NONSTATIC_DOUBLE:
4769             next_nonstatic_padded_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, BytesPerLong);
4770             real_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4771             next_nonstatic_padded_offset += BytesPerLong;
4772             break;
4773 
4774             // Value types in static fields are handled with oops
4775           case NONSTATIC_FLATTENABLE:
4776             throwValueTypeLimitation(THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
4777                                      "@Contended annotation not supported for inline types yet", fs.name(), fs.signature());
4778             return;
4779 
4780           case NONSTATIC_OOP:
4781             next_nonstatic_padded_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, heapOopSize);
4782             real_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4783             next_nonstatic_padded_offset += heapOopSize;
4784             nonstatic_oop_maps->add(real_offset, 1);
4785             break;
4786 
4787           default:
4788             ShouldNotReachHere();
4789         }
4790 
4791         if (fs.contended_group() == 0) {
4792           // Contended group defines the equivalence class over the fields:
4793           // the fields within the same contended group are not inter-padded.
4794           // The only exception is default group, which does not incur the
4795           // equivalence, and so requires intra-padding.
4796           next_nonstatic_padded_offset += ContendedPaddingWidth;
4797         }
4798 
4799         fs.set_offset(real_offset);
4800       } // for
4801 
4802       // Start laying out the next group.
4803       // Note that this will effectively pad the last group in the back;
4804       // this is expected to alleviate memory contention effects for
4805       // subclass fields and/or adjacent object.
4806       // If this was the default group, the padding is already in place.
4807       if (current_group != 0) {
4808         next_nonstatic_padded_offset += ContendedPaddingWidth;
4809       }
4810     }
4811 
4812     // handle static fields
4813   }
4814 
4815   // Entire class is contended, pad in the back.
4816   // This helps to alleviate memory contention effects for subclass fields
4817   // and/or adjacent object.
4818   if (is_contended_class) {
4819     assert(!is_value_type(), "@Contended not supported for value types yet");
4820     next_nonstatic_padded_offset += ContendedPaddingWidth;
4821   }
4822 
4823   int notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end;
4824   if (nonstatic_value_type_count != 0) {
4825     notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end = next_nonstatic_valuetype_offset;
4826   } else {
4827     notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4828   }
4829 
4830   int nonstatic_field_sz_align = heapOopSize;
4831   if (is_value_type()) {
4832     if ((notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end - nonstatic_fields_start) > heapOopSize) {
4833       nonstatic_field_sz_align = BytesPerLong; // value copy of fields only uses jlong copy
4834     }
4835   }
4836   int nonstatic_fields_end      = align_up(notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end, nonstatic_field_sz_align);
4837   int instance_end              = align_up(notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end, wordSize);
4838   int static_fields_end         = align_up(next_static_byte_offset, wordSize);
4839 
4840   int static_field_size         = (static_fields_end -
4841                                    InstanceMirrorKlass::offset_of_static_fields()) / wordSize;
4842   nonstatic_field_size          = nonstatic_field_size +
4843                                   (nonstatic_fields_end - nonstatic_fields_start) / heapOopSize;
4844 
4845   int instance_size             = align_object_size(instance_end / wordSize);
4846 
4847   assert(instance_size == align_object_size(align_up(
4848          (instanceOopDesc::base_offset_in_bytes() + nonstatic_field_size*heapOopSize)
4849          + initial_value_type_padding, wordSize) / wordSize), "consistent layout helper value");
4850 
4851 
4852   // Invariant: nonstatic_field end/start should only change if there are
4853   // nonstatic fields in the class, or if the class is contended. We compare
4854   // against the non-aligned value, so that end alignment will not fail the
4855   // assert without actually having the fields.
4856   assert((notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end == nonstatic_fields_start) ||
4857          is_contended_class ||
4858          (nonstatic_fields_count > 0), "double-check nonstatic start/end");
4859 
4860   // Number of non-static oop map blocks allocated at end of klass.
4861   nonstatic_oop_maps->compact();
4862 
4863 #ifndef PRODUCT
4864   if ((PrintFieldLayout && !is_value_type()) ||
4865       (PrintValueLayout && (is_value_type() || has_nonstatic_value_fields))) {
4866     print_field_layout(_class_name,
4867           _fields,
4868           cp,
4869           instance_size,
4870           nonstatic_fields_start,
4871           nonstatic_fields_end,
4872           static_fields_end);
4873     nonstatic_oop_maps->print_on(tty);
4874     tty->print("\n");
4875     tty->print_cr("Instance size = %d", instance_size);
4876     tty->print_cr("Nonstatic_field_size = %d", nonstatic_field_size);
4877     tty->print_cr("Static_field_size = %d", static_field_size);
4878     tty->print_cr("Has nonstatic fields = %d", has_nonstatic_fields);
4879     tty->print_cr("---");
4880   }
4881 
4882 #endif
4883   // Pass back information needed for InstanceKlass creation
4884   info->oop_map_blocks = nonstatic_oop_maps;
4885   info->_instance_size = instance_size;
4886   info->_static_field_size = static_field_size;
4887   info->_nonstatic_field_size = nonstatic_field_size;
4888   info->_has_nonstatic_fields = has_nonstatic_fields;
4889 
4890   // A value type is naturally atomic if it has just one field, and
4891   // that field is simple enough.
4892   info->_is_naturally_atomic = (is_value_type() &&
4893                                 !super_has_nonstatic_fields &&
4894                                 (nonstatic_fields_count <= 1) &&
4895                                 (not_atomic_value_types == 0) &&
4896                                 (nonstatic_contended_count == 0));
4897   // This may be too restrictive, since if all the fields fit in 64
4898   // bits we could make the decision to align instances of this class
4899   // to 64-bit boundaries, and load and store them as single words.
4900   // And on machines which supported larger atomics we could similarly
4901   // allow larger values to be atomic, if properly aligned.
4902 }
4903 
4904 void ClassFileParser::set_precomputed_flags(InstanceKlass* ik) {
4905   assert(ik != NULL, "invariant");
4906 
4907   const Klass* const super = ik->super();
4908 
4909   // Check if this klass has an empty finalize method (i.e. one with return bytecode only),
4910   // in which case we don't have to register objects as finalizable
4911   if (!_has_empty_finalizer) {
4912     if (_has_finalizer ||
4913         (super != NULL && super->has_finalizer())) {
4914       ik->set_has_finalizer();
4915     }
4916   }
4917 
4918 #ifdef ASSERT
4919   bool f = false;
4920   const Method* const m = ik->lookup_method(vmSymbols::finalize_method_name(),
4921                                            vmSymbols::void_method_signature());
4922   if (m != NULL && !m->is_empty_method()) {
4923       f = true;
4924   }
4925 
4926   // Spec doesn't prevent agent from redefinition of empty finalizer.
4927   // Despite the fact that it's generally bad idea and redefined finalizer
4928   // will not work as expected we shouldn't abort vm in this case
4929   if (!ik->has_redefined_this_or_super()) {
4930     assert(ik->has_finalizer() == f, "inconsistent has_finalizer");
4931   }
4932 #endif
4933 
4934   // Check if this klass supports the java.lang.Cloneable interface
4935   if (SystemDictionary::Cloneable_klass_loaded()) {
4936     if (ik->is_subtype_of(SystemDictionary::Cloneable_klass())) {
4937       if (ik->is_value()) {
4938         Thread *THREAD = Thread::current();
4939         throwValueTypeLimitation(THREAD_AND_LOCATION, "Inline Types do not support Cloneable");
4940         return;
4941       }
4942       ik->set_is_cloneable();
4943     }
4944   }
4945 
4946   // Check if this klass has a vanilla default constructor
4947   if (super == NULL) {
4948     // java.lang.Object has empty default constructor
4949     ik->set_has_vanilla_constructor();
4950   } else {
4951     if (super->has_vanilla_constructor() &&
4952         _has_vanilla_constructor) {
4953       ik->set_has_vanilla_constructor();
4954     }
4955 #ifdef ASSERT
4956     bool v = false;
4957     if (super->has_vanilla_constructor()) {
4958       const Method* const constructor =
4959         ik->find_method(vmSymbols::object_initializer_name(),
4960                        vmSymbols::void_method_signature());
4961       if (constructor != NULL && constructor->is_vanilla_constructor()) {
4962         v = true;
4963       }
4964     }
4965     assert(v == ik->has_vanilla_constructor(), "inconsistent has_vanilla_constructor");
4966 #endif
4967   }
4968 
4969   // If it cannot be fast-path allocated, set a bit in the layout helper.
4970   // See documentation of InstanceKlass::can_be_fastpath_allocated().
4971   assert(ik->size_helper() > 0, "layout_helper is initialized");
4972   if ((!RegisterFinalizersAtInit && ik->has_finalizer())
4973       || ik->is_abstract() || ik->is_interface()
4974       || (ik->name() == vmSymbols::java_lang_Class() && ik->class_loader() == NULL)
4975       || ik->size_helper() >= FastAllocateSizeLimit) {
4976     // Forbid fast-path allocation.
4977     const jint lh = Klass::instance_layout_helper(ik->size_helper(), true);
4978     ik->set_layout_helper(lh);
4979   }
4980 }
4981 
4982 bool ClassFileParser::supports_value_types() const {
4983   // Value types are only supported by class file version 55 and later
4984   return _major_version >= JAVA_11_VERSION;
4985 }
4986 
4987 // utility methods for appending an array with check for duplicates
4988 
4989 static void append_interfaces(GrowableArray<InstanceKlass*>* result,
4990                               const Array<InstanceKlass*>* const ifs) {
4991   // iterate over new interfaces
4992   for (int i = 0; i < ifs->length(); i++) {
4993     InstanceKlass* const e = ifs->at(i);
4994     assert(e->is_klass() && e->is_interface(), "just checking");
4995     // add new interface
4996     result->append_if_missing(e);
4997   }
4998 }
4999 
5000 static Array<InstanceKlass*>* compute_transitive_interfaces(const InstanceKlass* super,
5001                                                             Array<InstanceKlass*>* local_ifs,
5002                                                             ClassLoaderData* loader_data,
5003                                                             TRAPS) {
5004   assert(local_ifs != NULL, "invariant");
5005   assert(loader_data != NULL, "invariant");
5006 
5007   // Compute maximum size for transitive interfaces
5008   int max_transitive_size = 0;
5009   int super_size = 0;
5010   // Add superclass transitive interfaces size
5011   if (super != NULL) {
5012     super_size = super->transitive_interfaces()->length();
5013     max_transitive_size += super_size;
5014   }
5015   // Add local interfaces' super interfaces
5016   const int local_size = local_ifs->length();
5017   for (int i = 0; i < local_size; i++) {
5018     InstanceKlass* const l = local_ifs->at(i);
5019     max_transitive_size += l->transitive_interfaces()->length();
5020   }
5021   // Finally add local interfaces
5022   max_transitive_size += local_size;
5023   // Construct array
5024   if (max_transitive_size == 0) {
5025     // no interfaces, use canonicalized array
5026     return Universe::the_empty_instance_klass_array();
5027   } else if (max_transitive_size == super_size) {
5028     // no new local interfaces added, share superklass' transitive interface array
5029     return super->transitive_interfaces();
5030   } else if (max_transitive_size == local_size) {
5031     // only local interfaces added, share local interface array
5032     return local_ifs;
5033   } else {
5034     ResourceMark rm;
5035     GrowableArray<InstanceKlass*>* const result = new GrowableArray<InstanceKlass*>(max_transitive_size);
5036 
5037     // Copy down from superclass
5038     if (super != NULL) {
5039       append_interfaces(result, super->transitive_interfaces());
5040     }
5041 
5042     // Copy down from local interfaces' superinterfaces
5043     for (int i = 0; i < local_size; i++) {
5044       InstanceKlass* const l = local_ifs->at(i);
5045       append_interfaces(result, l->transitive_interfaces());
5046     }
5047     // Finally add local interfaces
5048     append_interfaces(result, local_ifs);
5049 
5050     // length will be less than the max_transitive_size if duplicates were removed
5051     const int length = result->length();
5052     assert(length <= max_transitive_size, "just checking");
5053     Array<InstanceKlass*>* const new_result =
5054       MetadataFactory::new_array<InstanceKlass*>(loader_data, length, CHECK_NULL);
5055     for (int i = 0; i < length; i++) {
5056       InstanceKlass* const e = result->at(i);
5057       assert(e != NULL, "just checking");
5058       new_result->at_put(i, e);
5059     }
5060     return new_result;
5061   }
5062 }
5063 
5064 static void check_super_class_access(const InstanceKlass* this_klass, TRAPS) {
5065   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
5066   const Klass* const super = this_klass->super();
5067 
5068   if (super != NULL) {
5069 
5070     // If the loader is not the boot loader then throw an exception if its
5071     // superclass is in package jdk.internal.reflect and its loader is not a
5072     // special reflection class loader
5073     if (!this_klass->class_loader_data()->is_the_null_class_loader_data()) {
5074       assert(super->is_instance_klass(), "super is not instance klass");
5075       PackageEntry* super_package = super->package();
5076       if (super_package != NULL &&
5077           super_package->name()->fast_compare(vmSymbols::jdk_internal_reflect()) == 0 &&
5078           !java_lang_ClassLoader::is_reflection_class_loader(this_klass->class_loader())) {
5079         ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5080         Exceptions::fthrow(
5081           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5082           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5083           "class %s loaded by %s cannot access jdk/internal/reflect superclass %s",
5084           this_klass->external_name(),
5085           this_klass->class_loader_data()->loader_name_and_id(),
5086           super->external_name());
5087         return;
5088       }
5089     }
5090 
5091     Reflection::VerifyClassAccessResults vca_result =
5092       Reflection::verify_class_access(this_klass, InstanceKlass::cast(super), false);
5093     if (vca_result != Reflection::ACCESS_OK) {
5094       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5095       char* msg = Reflection::verify_class_access_msg(this_klass,
5096                                                       InstanceKlass::cast(super),
5097                                                       vca_result);
5098       if (msg == NULL) {
5099         bool same_module = (this_klass->module() == super->module());
5100         Exceptions::fthrow(
5101           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5102           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5103           "class %s cannot access its %ssuperclass %s (%s%s%s)",
5104           this_klass->external_name(),
5105           super->is_abstract() ? "abstract " : "",
5106           super->external_name(),
5107           (same_module) ? this_klass->joint_in_module_of_loader(super) : this_klass->class_in_module_of_loader(),
5108           (same_module) ? "" : "; ",
5109           (same_module) ? "" : super->class_in_module_of_loader());
5110       } else {
5111         // Add additional message content.
5112         Exceptions::fthrow(
5113           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5114           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5115           "superclass access check failed: %s",
5116           msg);
5117       }
5118     }
5119   }
5120 }
5121 
5122
