5123 static void check_super_interface_access(const InstanceKlass* this_klass, TRAPS) {
5124   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
5125   const Array<InstanceKlass*>* const local_interfaces = this_klass->local_interfaces();
5126   const int lng = local_interfaces->length();
5127   for (int i = lng - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
5128     InstanceKlass* const k = local_interfaces->at(i);
5129     assert (k != NULL && k->is_interface(), "invalid interface");
5130     Reflection::VerifyClassAccessResults vca_result =
5131       Reflection::verify_class_access(this_klass, k, false);
5132     if (vca_result != Reflection::ACCESS_OK) {
5133       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5134       char* msg = Reflection::verify_class_access_msg(this_klass,
5135                                                       k,
5136                                                       vca_result);
5137       if (msg == NULL) {
5138         bool same_module = (this_klass->module() == k->module());
5139         Exceptions::fthrow(
5140           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5141           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5142           "class %s cannot access its superinterface %s (%s%s%s)",
5143           this_klass->external_name(),
5144           k->external_name(),
5145           (same_module) ? this_klass->joint_in_module_of_loader(k) : this_klass->class_in_module_of_loader(),
5146           (same_module) ? "" : "; ",
5147           (same_module) ? "" : k->class_in_module_of_loader());
5148       } else {
5149         // Add additional message content.
5150         Exceptions::fthrow(
5151           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5152           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5153           "superinterface check failed: %s",
5154           msg);
5155       }
5156     }
5157   }
5158 }
5159 
5160 
5161 static void check_final_method_override(const InstanceKlass* this_klass, TRAPS) {
5162   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
5163   const Array<Method*>* const methods = this_klass->methods();
5164   const int num_methods = methods->length();
5165 
5166   // go thru each method and check if it overrides a final method
5167   for (int index = 0; index < num_methods; index++) {
5168     const Method* const m = methods->at(index);
5169 
5170     // skip private, static, and <init> methods
5171     if ((!m->is_private() && !m->is_static()) &&
5172         (m->name() != vmSymbols::object_initializer_name())) {
5173 
5174       const Symbol* const name = m->name();
5175       const Symbol* const signature = m->signature();
5176       const Klass* k = this_klass->super();
5177       const Method* super_m = NULL;
5178       while (k != NULL) {
5179         // skip supers that don't have final methods.
5180         if (k->has_final_method()) {
5181           // lookup a matching method in the super class hierarchy
5182           super_m = InstanceKlass::cast(k)->lookup_method(name, signature);
5183           if (super_m == NULL) {
5184             break; // didn't find any match; get out
5185           }
5186 
5187           if (super_m->is_final() && !super_m->is_static() &&
5188               !super_m->access_flags().is_private()) {
5189             // matching method in super is final, and not static or private
5190             bool can_access = Reflection::verify_member_access(this_klass,
5191                                                                super_m->method_holder(),
5192                                                                super_m->method_holder(),
5193                                                                super_m->access_flags(),
5194                                                               false, false, CHECK);
5195             if (can_access) {
5196               // this class can access super final method and therefore override
5197               ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5198               Exceptions::fthrow(THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5199                                  vmSymbols::java_lang_VerifyError(),
5200                                  "class %s overrides final method %s.%s%s",
5201                                  this_klass->external_name(),
5202                                  super_m->method_holder()->external_name(),
5203                                  name->as_C_string(),
5204                                  signature->as_C_string()
5205                                  );
5206               return;
5207             }
5208           }
5209 
5210           // continue to look from super_m's holder's super.
5211           k = super_m->method_holder()->super();
5212           continue;
5213         }
5214 
5215         k = k->super();
5216       }
5217     }
5218   }
5219 }
5220 
5221 
5222 // assumes that this_klass is an interface
5223 static void check_illegal_static_method(const InstanceKlass* this_klass, TRAPS) {
5224   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
5225   assert(this_klass->is_interface(), "not an interface");
5226   const Array<Method*>* methods = this_klass->methods();
5227   const int num_methods = methods->length();
5228 
5229   for (int index = 0; index < num_methods; index++) {
5230     const Method* const m = methods->at(index);
5231     // if m is static and not the init method, throw a verify error
5232     if ((m->is_static()) && (m->name() != vmSymbols::class_initializer_name())) {
5233       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5234       Exceptions::fthrow(
5235         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5236         vmSymbols::java_lang_VerifyError(),
5237         "Illegal static method %s in interface %s",
5238         m->name()->as_C_string(),
5239         this_klass->external_name()
5240       );
5241       return;
5242     }
5243   }
5244 }
5245 
5246 // utility methods for format checking
5247 
5248 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_class_modifiers(jint flags, TRAPS) const {
5249   const bool is_module = (flags & JVM_ACC_MODULE) != 0;
5250   const bool is_value_type = (flags & JVM_ACC_VALUE) != 0;
5251   assert(_major_version >= JAVA_9_VERSION || !is_module, "JVM_ACC_MODULE should not be set");
5252   assert(supports_value_types() || !is_value_type, "JVM_ACC_VALUE should not be set");
5253   if (is_module) {
5254     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5255     Exceptions::fthrow(
5256       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5257       vmSymbols::java_lang_NoClassDefFoundError(),
5258       "%s is not a class because access_flag ACC_MODULE is set",
5259       _class_name->as_C_string());
5260     return;
5261   }
5262 
5263   if (is_value_type && !EnableValhalla) {
5264     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5265     Exceptions::fthrow(
5266       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5267       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5268       "Class modifier ACC_VALUE in class %s requires option -XX:+EnableValhalla",
5269       _class_name->as_C_string()
5270     );
5271   }
5272 
5273   if (!_need_verify) { return; }
5274 
5275   const bool is_interface  = (flags & JVM_ACC_INTERFACE)  != 0;
5276   const bool is_abstract   = (flags & JVM_ACC_ABSTRACT)   != 0;
5277   const bool is_final      = (flags & JVM_ACC_FINAL)      != 0;
5278   const bool is_super      = (flags & JVM_ACC_SUPER)      != 0;
5279   const bool is_enum       = (flags & JVM_ACC_ENUM)       != 0;
5280   const bool is_annotation = (flags & JVM_ACC_ANNOTATION) != 0;
5281   const bool major_gte_1_5 = _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION;
5282   const bool major_gte_14  = _major_version >= JAVA_14_VERSION;
5283 
5284   if ((is_abstract && is_final) ||
5285       (is_interface && !is_abstract) ||
5286       (is_interface && major_gte_1_5 && (is_super || is_enum)) ||
5287       (!is_interface && major_gte_1_5 && is_annotation) ||
5288       (is_value_type && (is_interface || is_abstract || is_enum || !is_final))) {
5289     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5290     const char* class_note = "";
5291     if (is_value_type)  class_note = " (an inline class)";
5292     Exceptions::fthrow(
5293       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5294       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5295       "Illegal class modifiers in class %s%s: 0x%X",
5296       _class_name->as_C_string(), class_note, flags
5297     );
5298     return;
5299   }
5300 }
5301 
5302 static bool has_illegal_visibility(jint flags) {
5303   const bool is_public    = (flags & JVM_ACC_PUBLIC)    != 0;
5304   const bool is_protected = (flags & JVM_ACC_PROTECTED) != 0;
5305   const bool is_private   = (flags & JVM_ACC_PRIVATE)   != 0;
5306 
5307   return ((is_public && is_protected) ||
5308           (is_public && is_private) ||
5309           (is_protected && is_private));
5310 }
5311 
5312 // A legal major_version.minor_version must be one of the following:
5313 //
5314 //  Major_version >= 45 and major_version < 56, any minor_version.
5315 //  Major_version >= 56 and major_version <= JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION and minor_version = 0.
5316 //  Major_version = JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION and minor_version = 65535 and --enable-preview is present.
5317 //
5318 static void verify_class_version(u2 major, u2 minor, Symbol* class_name, TRAPS){
5319   ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5320   const u2 max_version = JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION;
5321   if (major < JAVA_MIN_SUPPORTED_VERSION) {
5322     Exceptions::fthrow(
5323       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5324       vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
5325       "%s (class file version %u.%u) was compiled with an invalid major version",
5326       class_name->as_C_string(), major, minor);
5327     return;
5328   }
5329 
5330   if (major > max_version) {
5331     Exceptions::fthrow(
5332       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5333       vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
5334       "%s has been compiled by a more recent version of the Java Runtime (class file version %u.%u), "
5335       "this version of the Java Runtime only recognizes class file versions up to %u.0",
5336       class_name->as_C_string(), major, minor, JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION);
5337     return;
5338   }
5339 
5340   if (major < JAVA_12_VERSION || minor == 0) {
5341     return;
5342   }
5343 
5344   if (minor == JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION) {
5345     if (major != max_version) {
5346       Exceptions::fthrow(
5347         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5348         vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
5349         "%s (class file version %u.%u) was compiled with preview features that are unsupported. "
5350         "This version of the Java Runtime only recognizes preview features for class file version %u.%u",
5351         class_name->as_C_string(), major, minor, JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION, JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION);
5352       return;
5353     }
5354 
5355     if (!Arguments::enable_preview()) {
5356       Exceptions::fthrow(
5357         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5358         vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
5359         "Preview features are not enabled for %s (class file version %u.%u). Try running with '--enable-preview'",
5360         class_name->as_C_string(), major, minor);
5361       return;
5362     }
5363 
5364   } else { // minor != JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION
5365     Exceptions::fthrow(
5366         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5367         vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
5368         "%s (class file version %u.%u) was compiled with an invalid non-zero minor version",
5369         class_name->as_C_string(), major, minor);
5370   }
5371 }
5372 
5373 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_field_modifiers(jint flags,
5374                                                    bool is_interface,
5375                                                    bool is_value_type,
5376                                                    TRAPS) const {
5377   if (!_need_verify) { return; }
5378 
5379   const bool is_public    = (flags & JVM_ACC_PUBLIC)    != 0;
5380   const bool is_protected = (flags & JVM_ACC_PROTECTED) != 0;
5381   const bool is_private   = (flags & JVM_ACC_PRIVATE)   != 0;
5382   const bool is_static    = (flags & JVM_ACC_STATIC)    != 0;
5383   const bool is_final     = (flags & JVM_ACC_FINAL)     != 0;
5384   const bool is_volatile  = (flags & JVM_ACC_VOLATILE)  != 0;
5385   const bool is_transient = (flags & JVM_ACC_TRANSIENT) != 0;
5386   const bool is_enum      = (flags & JVM_ACC_ENUM)      != 0;
5387   const bool major_gte_1_5 = _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION;
5388 
5389   bool is_illegal = false;
5390 
5391   if (is_interface) {
5392     if (!is_public || !is_static || !is_final || is_private ||
5393         is_protected || is_volatile || is_transient ||
5394         (major_gte_1_5 && is_enum)) {
5395       is_illegal = true;
5396     }
5397   } else { // not interface
5398     if (has_illegal_visibility(flags) || (is_final && is_volatile)) {
5399       is_illegal = true;
5400     } else {
5401       if (is_value_type && !is_static && !is_final) {
5402         is_illegal = true;
5403       }
5404     }
5405   }
5406 
5407   if (is_illegal) {
5408     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5409     Exceptions::fthrow(
5410       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5411       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5412       "Illegal field modifiers in class %s: 0x%X",
5413       _class_name->as_C_string(), flags);
5414     return;
5415   }
5416 }
5417 
5418 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_method_modifiers(jint flags,
5419                                                     bool is_interface,
5420                                                     bool is_value_type,
5421                                                     const Symbol* name,
5422                                                     TRAPS) const {
5423   if (!_need_verify) { return; }
5424 
5425   const bool is_public       = (flags & JVM_ACC_PUBLIC)       != 0;
5426   const bool is_private      = (flags & JVM_ACC_PRIVATE)      != 0;
5427   const bool is_static       = (flags & JVM_ACC_STATIC)       != 0;
5428   const bool is_final        = (flags & JVM_ACC_FINAL)        != 0;
5429   const bool is_native       = (flags & JVM_ACC_NATIVE)       != 0;
5430   const bool is_abstract     = (flags & JVM_ACC_ABSTRACT)     != 0;
5431   const bool is_bridge       = (flags & JVM_ACC_BRIDGE)       != 0;
5432   const bool is_strict       = (flags & JVM_ACC_STRICT)       != 0;
5433   const bool is_synchronized = (flags & JVM_ACC_SYNCHRONIZED) != 0;
5434   const bool is_protected    = (flags & JVM_ACC_PROTECTED)    != 0;
5435   const bool major_gte_1_5   = _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION;
5436   const bool major_gte_8     = _major_version >= JAVA_8_VERSION;
5437   const bool is_initializer  = (name == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name());
5438 
5439   bool is_illegal = false;
5440 
5441   const char* class_note = "";
5442 
5443   if (is_interface) {
5444     if (major_gte_8) {
5445       // Class file version is JAVA_8_VERSION or later Methods of
5446       // interfaces may set any of the flags except ACC_PROTECTED,
5447       // ACC_FINAL, ACC_NATIVE, and ACC_SYNCHRONIZED; they must
5448       // have exactly one of the ACC_PUBLIC or ACC_PRIVATE flags set.
5449       if ((is_public == is_private) || /* Only one of private and public should be true - XNOR */
5450           (is_native || is_protected || is_final || is_synchronized) ||
5451           // If a specific method of a class or interface has its
5452           // ACC_ABSTRACT flag set, it must not have any of its
5453           // ACC_FINAL, ACC_NATIVE, ACC_PRIVATE, ACC_STATIC,
5454           // ACC_STRICT, or ACC_SYNCHRONIZED flags set.  No need to
5455           // check for ACC_FINAL, ACC_NATIVE or ACC_SYNCHRONIZED as
5456           // those flags are illegal irrespective of ACC_ABSTRACT being set or not.
5457           (is_abstract && (is_private || is_static || is_strict))) {
5458         is_illegal = true;
5459       }
5460     } else if (major_gte_1_5) {
5461       // Class file version in the interval [JAVA_1_5_VERSION, JAVA_8_VERSION)
5462       if (!is_public || is_private || is_protected || is_static || is_final ||
5463           is_synchronized || is_native || !is_abstract || is_strict) {
5464         is_illegal = true;
5465       }
5466     } else {
5467       // Class file version is pre-JAVA_1_5_VERSION
5468       if (!is_public || is_static || is_final || is_native || !is_abstract) {
5469         is_illegal = true;
5470       }
5471     }
5472   } else { // not interface
5473     if (has_illegal_visibility(flags)) {
5474       is_illegal = true;
5475     } else {
5476       if (is_initializer) {
5477         if (is_final || is_synchronized || is_native ||
5478             is_abstract || (major_gte_1_5 && is_bridge)) {
5479           is_illegal = true;
5480         }
5481         if (!is_static && !is_value_type) {
5482           // OK, an object constructor in a regular class
5483         } else if (is_static && is_value_type) {
5484           // OK, a static init factory in an inline class
5485         } else {
5486           // but no other combinations are allowed
5487           is_illegal = true;
5488           class_note = (is_value_type ? " (an inline class)" : " (not an inline class)");
5489         }
5490       } else { // not initializer
5491         if (is_value_type && is_synchronized && !is_static) {
5492           is_illegal = true;
5493           class_note = " (an inline class)";
5494         } else {
5495           if (is_abstract) {
5496             if ((is_final || is_native || is_private || is_static ||
5497                 (major_gte_1_5 && (is_synchronized || is_strict)))) {
5498               is_illegal = true;
5499             }
5500           }
5501         }
5502       }
5503     }
5504   }
5505 
5506   if (is_illegal) {
5507     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5508     Exceptions::fthrow(
5509       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5510       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5511       "Method %s in class %s%s has illegal modifiers: 0x%X",
5512       name->as_C_string(), _class_name->as_C_string(), class_note, flags);
5513     return;
5514   }
5515 }
5516 
5517 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_utf8(const unsigned char* buffer,
5518                                         int length,
5519                                         TRAPS) const {
5520   assert(_need_verify, "only called when _need_verify is true");
5521   if (!UTF8::is_legal_utf8(buffer, length, _major_version <= 47)) {
5522     classfile_parse_error("Illegal UTF8 string in constant pool in class file %s", CHECK);
5523   }
5524 }
5525 
5526 // Unqualified names may not contain the characters '.', ';', '[', or '/'.
5527 // In class names, '/' separates unqualified names.  This is verified in this function also.
5528 // Method names also may not contain the characters '<' or '>', unless <init>
5529 // or <clinit>.  Note that method names may not be <init> or <clinit> in this
5530 // method.  Because these names have been checked as special cases before
5531 // calling this method in verify_legal_method_name.
5532 //
5533 // This method is also called from the modular system APIs in modules.cpp
5534 // to verify the validity of module and package names.
5535 bool ClassFileParser::verify_unqualified_name(const char* name,
5536                                               unsigned int length,
5537                                               int type) {
5538   if (length == 0) return false;  // Must have at least one char.
5539   for (const char* p = name; p != name + length; p++) {
5540     switch(*p) {
5541       case JVM_SIGNATURE_DOT:
5542       case JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDCLASS:
5543       case JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY:
5544         // do not permit '.', ';', or '['
5545         return false;
5546       case JVM_SIGNATURE_SLASH:
5547         // check for '//' or leading or trailing '/' which are not legal
5548         // unqualified name must not be empty
5549         if (type == ClassFileParser::LegalClass) {
5550           if (p == name || p+1 >= name+length ||
5551               *(p+1) == JVM_SIGNATURE_SLASH) {
5552             return false;
5553           }
5554         } else {
5555           return false;   // do not permit '/' unless it's class name
5556         }
5557         break;
5558       case JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL:
5559       case JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDSPECIAL:
5560         // do not permit '<' or '>' in method names
5561         if (type == ClassFileParser::LegalMethod) {
5562           return false;
5563         }
5564     }
5565   }
5566   return true;
5567 }
5568 
5569 // Take pointer to a UTF8 byte string (not NUL-terminated).
5570 // Skip over the longest part of the string that could
5571 // be taken as a fieldname. Allow '/' if slash_ok is true.
5572 // Return a pointer to just past the fieldname.
5573 // Return NULL if no fieldname at all was found, or in the case of slash_ok
5574 // being true, we saw consecutive slashes (meaning we were looking for a
5575 // qualified path but found something that was badly-formed).
5576 static const char* skip_over_field_name(const char* const name,
5577                                         bool slash_ok,
5578                                         unsigned int length) {
5579   const char* p;
5580   jboolean last_is_slash = false;
5581   jboolean not_first_ch = false;
5582 
5583   for (p = name; p != name + length; not_first_ch = true) {
5584     const char* old_p = p;
5585     jchar ch = *p;
5586     if (ch < 128) {
5587       p++;
5588       // quick check for ascii
5589       if ((ch >= 'a' && ch <= 'z') ||
5590         (ch >= 'A' && ch <= 'Z') ||
5591         (ch == '_' || ch == '$') ||
5592         (not_first_ch && ch >= '0' && ch <= '9')) {
5593         last_is_slash = false;
5594         continue;
5595       }
5596       if (slash_ok && ch == JVM_SIGNATURE_SLASH) {
5597         if (last_is_slash) {
5598           return NULL;  // Don't permit consecutive slashes
5599         }
5600         last_is_slash = true;
5601         continue;
5602       }
5603     }
5604     else {
5605       jint unicode_ch;
5606       char* tmp_p = UTF8::next_character(p, &unicode_ch);
5607       p = tmp_p;
5608       last_is_slash = false;
5609       // Check if ch is Java identifier start or is Java identifier part
5610       // 4672820: call java.lang.Character methods directly without generating separate tables.
5611       EXCEPTION_MARK;
5612       // return value
5613       JavaValue result(T_BOOLEAN);
5614       // Set up the arguments to isJavaIdentifierStart or isJavaIdentifierPart
5615       JavaCallArguments args;
5616       args.push_int(unicode_ch);
5617 
5618       if (not_first_ch) {
5619         // public static boolean isJavaIdentifierPart(char ch);
5620         JavaCalls::call_static(&result,
5621           SystemDictionary::Character_klass(),
5622           vmSymbols::isJavaIdentifierPart_name(),
5623           vmSymbols::int_bool_signature(),
5624           &args,
5625           THREAD);
5626       } else {
5627         // public static boolean isJavaIdentifierStart(char ch);
5628         JavaCalls::call_static(&result,
5629           SystemDictionary::Character_klass(),
5630           vmSymbols::isJavaIdentifierStart_name(),
5631           vmSymbols::int_bool_signature(),
5632           &args,
5633           THREAD);
5634       }
5635       if (HAS_PENDING_EXCEPTION) {
5636         CLEAR_PENDING_EXCEPTION;
5637         return NULL;
5638       }
5639       if(result.get_jboolean()) {
5640         continue;
5641       }
5642     }
5643     return (not_first_ch) ? old_p : NULL;
5644   }
5645   return (not_first_ch) ? p : NULL;
5646 }
5647 
5648 // Take pointer to a UTF8 byte string (not NUL-terminated).
5649 // Skip over the longest part of the string that could
5650 // be taken as a field signature. Allow "void" if void_ok.
5651 // Return a pointer to just past the signature.
5652 // Return NULL if no legal signature is found.
5653 const char* ClassFileParser::skip_over_field_signature(const char* signature,
5654                                                        bool void_ok,
5655                                                        unsigned int length,
5656                                                        TRAPS) const {
5657   unsigned int array_dim = 0;
5658   while (length > 0) {
5659     switch (signature[0]) {
5660     case JVM_SIGNATURE_VOID: if (!void_ok) { return NULL; }
5661     case JVM_SIGNATURE_BOOLEAN:
5662     case JVM_SIGNATURE_BYTE:
5663     case JVM_SIGNATURE_CHAR:
5664     case JVM_SIGNATURE_SHORT:
5665     case JVM_SIGNATURE_INT:
5666     case JVM_SIGNATURE_FLOAT:
5667     case JVM_SIGNATURE_LONG:
5668     case JVM_SIGNATURE_DOUBLE:
5669       return signature + 1;
5670     case JVM_SIGNATURE_VALUETYPE:
5671       // Can't enable this check until JDK upgrades the bytecode generators
5672       // if (_major_version < CONSTANT_CLASS_DESCRIPTORS ) {
5673       //   classfile_parse_error("Class name contains illegal Q-signature "
5674       //                                    "in descriptor in class file %s",
5675       //                                    CHECK_0);
5676       // }
5677       // fall through
5678     case JVM_SIGNATURE_CLASS:
5679     {
5680       if (_major_version < JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
5681         // Skip over the class name if one is there
5682         const char* const p = skip_over_field_name(signature + 1, true, --length);
5683 
5684         // The next character better be a semicolon
5685         if (p && (p - signature) > 1 && p[0] == JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDCLASS) {
5686           return p + 1;
5687         }
5688       }
5689       else {
5690         // Skip leading 'L' or 'Q' and ignore first appearance of ';'
5691         signature++;
5692         const char* c = (const char*) memchr(signature, JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDCLASS, length - 1);
5693         // Format check signature
5694         if (c != NULL) {
5695           int newlen = c - (char*) signature;
5696           bool legal = verify_unqualified_name(signature, newlen, LegalClass);
5697           if (!legal) {
5698             classfile_parse_error("Class name is empty or contains illegal character "
5699                                   "in descriptor in class file %s",
5700                                   CHECK_NULL);
5701             return NULL;
5702           }
5703           return signature + newlen + 1;
5704         }
5705       }
5706       return NULL;
5707     }
5708     case JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY:
5709       array_dim++;
5710       if (array_dim > 255) {
5711         // 4277370: array descriptor is valid only if it represents 255 or fewer dimensions.
5712         classfile_parse_error("Array type descriptor has more than 255 dimensions in class file %s", CHECK_NULL);
5713       }
5714       // The rest of what's there better be a legal signature
5715       signature++;
5716       length--;
5717       void_ok = false;
5718       break;
5719     default:
5720       return NULL;
5721     }
5722   }
5723   return NULL;
5724 }
5725 
5726 // Checks if name is a legal class name.
5727 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_class_name(const Symbol* name, TRAPS) const {
5728   if (!_need_verify || _relax_verify) { return; }
5729 
5730   assert(name->refcount() > 0, "symbol must be kept alive");
5731   char* bytes = (char*)name->bytes();
5732   unsigned int length = name->utf8_length();
5733   bool legal = false;
5734 
5735   if (length > 0) {
5736     const char* p;
5737     if (bytes[0] == JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY) {
5738       p = skip_over_field_signature(bytes, false, length, CHECK);
5739       legal = (p != NULL) && ((p - bytes) == (int)length);
5740     } else if (_major_version < JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
5741       if (bytes[0] != JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL) {
5742         p = skip_over_field_name(bytes, true, length);
5743         legal = (p != NULL) && ((p - bytes) == (int)length);
5744       }
5745     } else if (_major_version >= CONSTANT_CLASS_DESCRIPTORS && bytes[length - 1] == ';' ) {
5746       // Support for L...; and Q...; descriptors
5747       legal = verify_unqualified_name(bytes + 1, length - 2, LegalClass);
5748     } else {
5749       // 4900761: relax the constraints based on JSR202 spec
5750       // Class names may be drawn from the entire Unicode character set.
5751       // Identifiers between '/' must be unqualified names.
5752       // The utf8 string has been verified when parsing cpool entries.
5753       legal = verify_unqualified_name(bytes, length, LegalClass);
5754     }
5755   }
5756   if (!legal) {
5757     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5758     assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
5759     Exceptions::fthrow(
5760       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5761       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5762       "Illegal class name \"%.*s\" in class file %s", length, bytes,
5763       _class_name->as_C_string()
5764     );
5765     return;
5766   }
5767 }
5768 
5769 // Checks if name is a legal field name.
5770 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_field_name(const Symbol* name, TRAPS) const {
5771   if (!_need_verify || _relax_verify) { return; }
5772 
5773   char* bytes = (char*)name->bytes();
5774   unsigned int length = name->utf8_length();
5775   bool legal = false;
5776 
5777   if (length > 0) {
5778     if (_major_version < JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
5779       if (bytes[0] != JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL) {
5780         const char* p = skip_over_field_name(bytes, false, length);
5781         legal = (p != NULL) && ((p - bytes) == (int)length);
5782       }
5783     } else {
5784       // 4881221: relax the constraints based on JSR202 spec
5785       legal = verify_unqualified_name(bytes, length, LegalField);
5786     }
5787   }
5788 
5789   if (!legal) {
5790     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5791     assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
5792     Exceptions::fthrow(
5793       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5794       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5795       "Illegal field name \"%.*s\" in class %s", length, bytes,
5796       _class_name->as_C_string()
5797     );
5798     return;
5799   }
5800 }
5801 
5802 // Checks if name is a legal method name.
5803 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_method_name(const Symbol* name, TRAPS) const {
5804   if (!_need_verify || _relax_verify) { return; }
5805 
5806   assert(name != NULL, "method name is null");
5807   char* bytes = (char*)name->bytes();
5808   unsigned int length = name->utf8_length();
5809   bool legal = false;
5810 
5811   if (length > 0) {
5812     if (bytes[0] == JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL) {
5813       if (name == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name() || name == vmSymbols::class_initializer_name()) {
5814         legal = true;
5815       }
5816     } else if (_major_version < JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
5817       const char* p;
5818       p = skip_over_field_name(bytes, false, length);
5819       legal = (p != NULL) && ((p - bytes) == (int)length);
5820     } else {
5821       // 4881221: relax the constraints based on JSR202 spec
5822       legal = verify_unqualified_name(bytes, length, LegalMethod);
5823     }
5824   }
5825 
5826   if (!legal) {
5827     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5828     assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
5829     Exceptions::fthrow(
5830       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5831       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5832       "Illegal method name \"%.*s\" in class %s", length, bytes,
5833       _class_name->as_C_string()
5834     );
5835     return;
5836   }
5837 }
5838 
5839 
5840 // Checks if signature is a legal field signature.
5841 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_field_signature(const Symbol* name,
5842                                                    const Symbol* signature,
5843                                                    TRAPS) const {
5844   if (!_need_verify) { return; }
5845 
5846   const char* const bytes = (const char* const)signature->bytes();
5847   const unsigned int length = signature->utf8_length();
5848   const char* const p = skip_over_field_signature(bytes, false, length, CHECK);
5849 
5850   if (p == NULL || (p - bytes) != (int)length) {
5851     throwIllegalSignature("Field", name, signature, CHECK);
5852   }
5853 }
5854 
5855 // Checks if signature is a legal method signature.
5856 // Returns number of parameters
5857 int ClassFileParser::verify_legal_method_signature(const Symbol* name,
5858                                                    const Symbol* signature,
5859                                                    TRAPS) const {
5860   if (!_need_verify) {
5861     // make sure caller's args_size will be less than 0 even for non-static
5862     // method so it will be recomputed in compute_size_of_parameters().
5863     return -2;
5864   }
5865 
5866   // Class initializers cannot have args for class format version >= 51.
5867   if (name == vmSymbols::class_initializer_name() &&
5868       signature != vmSymbols::void_method_signature() &&
5869       _major_version >= JAVA_7_VERSION) {
5870     throwIllegalSignature("Method", name, signature, CHECK_0);
5871     return 0;
5872   }
5873 
5874   unsigned int args_size = 0;
5875   const char* p = (const char*)signature->bytes();
5876   unsigned int length = signature->utf8_length();
5877   const char* nextp;
5878 
5879   // The first character must be a '('
5880   if ((length > 0) && (*p++ == JVM_SIGNATURE_FUNC)) {
5881     length--;
5882     // Skip over legal field signatures
5883     nextp = skip_over_field_signature(p, false, length, CHECK_0);
5884     while ((length > 0) && (nextp != NULL)) {
5885       args_size++;
5886       if (p[0] == 'J' || p[0] == 'D') {
5887         args_size++;
5888       }
5889       length -= nextp - p;
5890       p = nextp;
5891       nextp = skip_over_field_signature(p, false, length, CHECK_0);
5892     }
5893     // The first non-signature thing better be a ')'
5894     if ((length > 0) && (*p++ == JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDFUNC)) {
5895       length--;
5896       if (name->utf8_length() > 0 && name->char_at(0) == JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL) {
5897         // All constructor methods must return void
5898         if ((length == 1) && (p[0] == JVM_SIGNATURE_VOID)) {
5899           return args_size;
5900         }
5901         // All static init methods must return the current class
5902         if ((length >= 3) && (p[length-1] == JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDCLASS)
5903             && name == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name()) {
5904           nextp = skip_over_field_signature(p, true, length, CHECK_0);
5905           if (nextp && ((int)length == (nextp - p))) {
5906             // The actual class will be checked against current class
5907             // when the method is defined (see parse_method).
5908             // A reference to a static init with a bad return type
5909             // will load and verify OK, but will fail to link.
5910             return args_size;
5911           }
5912         }
5913         // The distinction between static factory methods and
5914         // constructors depends on the JVM_ACC_STATIC modifier.
5915         // This distinction must be reflected in a void or non-void
5916         // return. For declared methods, the check is in parse_method.
5917       } else {
5918         // Now we better just have a return value
5919         nextp = skip_over_field_signature(p, true, length, CHECK_0);
5920         if (nextp && ((int)length == (nextp - p))) {
5921           return args_size;
5922         }
5923       }
5924     }
5925   }
5926   // Report error
5927   throwIllegalSignature("Method", name, signature, CHECK_0);
5928   return 0;
5929 }
5930 
5931 int ClassFileParser::static_field_size() const {
5932   assert(_field_info != NULL, "invariant");
5933   return _field_info->_static_field_size;
5934 }
5935 
5936 int ClassFileParser::total_oop_map_count() const {
5937   assert(_field_info != NULL, "invariant");
5938   return _field_info->oop_map_blocks->_nonstatic_oop_map_count;
5939 }
5940 
5941 jint ClassFileParser::layout_size() const {
5942   assert(_field_info != NULL, "invariant");
5943   return _field_info->_instance_size;
5944 }
5945 
5946 static void check_methods_for_intrinsics(const InstanceKlass* ik,
5947                                          const Array<Method*>* methods) {
5948   assert(ik != NULL, "invariant");
5949   assert(methods != NULL, "invariant");
5950 
5951   // Set up Method*::intrinsic_id as soon as we know the names of methods.
5952   // (We used to do this lazily, but now we query it in Rewriter,
5953   // which is eagerly done for every method, so we might as well do it now,
5954   // when everything is fresh in memory.)
5955   const vmSymbols::SID klass_id = Method::klass_id_for_intrinsics(ik);
5956 
5957   if (klass_id != vmSymbols::NO_SID) {
5958     for (int j = 0; j < methods->length(); ++j) {
5959       Method* method = methods->at(j);
5960       method->init_intrinsic_id();
5961 
5962       if (CheckIntrinsics) {
5963         // Check if an intrinsic is defined for method 'method',
5964         // but the method is not annotated with @HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate.
5965         if (method->intrinsic_id() != vmIntrinsics::_none &&
5966             !method->intrinsic_candidate()) {
5967               tty->print("Compiler intrinsic is defined for method [%s], "
5968               "but the method is not annotated with @HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate.%s",
5969               method->name_and_sig_as_C_string(),
5970               NOT_DEBUG(" Method will not be inlined.") DEBUG_ONLY(" Exiting.")
5971             );
5972           tty->cr();
5973           DEBUG_ONLY(vm_exit(1));
5974         }
5975         // Check is the method 'method' is annotated with @HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate,
5976         // but there is no intrinsic available for it.
5977         if (method->intrinsic_candidate() &&
5978           method->intrinsic_id() == vmIntrinsics::_none) {
5979             tty->print("Method [%s] is annotated with @HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate, "
5980               "but no compiler intrinsic is defined for the method.%s",
5981               method->name_and_sig_as_C_string(),
5982               NOT_DEBUG("") DEBUG_ONLY(" Exiting.")
5983             );
5984           tty->cr();
5985           DEBUG_ONLY(vm_exit(1));
5986         }
5987       }
5988     } // end for
5989 
5990 #ifdef ASSERT
5991     if (CheckIntrinsics) {
5992       // Check for orphan methods in the current class. A method m
5993       // of a class C is orphan if an intrinsic is defined for method m,
5994       // but class C does not declare m.
5995       // The check is potentially expensive, therefore it is available
5996       // only in debug builds.
5997 
5998       for (int id = vmIntrinsics::FIRST_ID; id < (int)vmIntrinsics::ID_LIMIT; ++id) {
5999         if (vmIntrinsics::_compiledLambdaForm == id) {
6000           // The _compiledLamdbdaForm intrinsic is a special marker for bytecode
6001           // generated for the JVM from a LambdaForm and therefore no method
6002           // is defined for it.
6003           continue;
6004         }
6005 
6006         if (vmIntrinsics::class_for(vmIntrinsics::ID_from(id)) == klass_id) {
6007           // Check if the current class contains a method with the same
6008           // name, flags, signature.
6009           bool match = false;
6010           for (int j = 0; j < methods->length(); ++j) {
6011             const Method* method = methods->at(j);
6012             if (method->intrinsic_id() == id) {
6013               match = true;
6014               break;
6015             }
6016           }
6017 
6018           if (!match) {
6019             char buf[1000];
6020             tty->print("Compiler intrinsic is defined for method [%s], "
6021                        "but the method is not available in class [%s].%s",
6022                         vmIntrinsics::short_name_as_C_string(vmIntrinsics::ID_from(id),
6023                                                              buf, sizeof(buf)),
6024                         ik->name()->as_C_string(),
6025                         NOT_DEBUG("") DEBUG_ONLY(" Exiting.")
6026             );
6027             tty->cr();
6028             DEBUG_ONLY(vm_exit(1));
6029           }
6030         }
6031       } // end for
6032     } // CheckIntrinsics
6033 #endif // ASSERT
6034   }
6035 }
6036 
6037 // Called from a factory method in KlassFactory, not from this file.
6038 InstanceKlass* ClassFileParser::create_instance_klass(bool changed_by_loadhook, TRAPS) {
6039   if (_klass != NULL) {
6040     return _klass;
6041   }
6042 
6043   InstanceKlass* const ik =
6044     InstanceKlass::allocate_instance_klass(*this, CHECK_NULL);
6045 
6046   fill_instance_klass(ik, changed_by_loadhook, CHECK_NULL);
6047   assert(_klass == ik, "invariant");
6048 
6049 
6050   if (ik->should_store_fingerprint()) {
6051     ik->store_fingerprint(_stream->compute_fingerprint());
6052   }
6053 
6054   ik->set_has_passed_fingerprint_check(false);
6055   if (UseAOT && ik->supers_have_passed_fingerprint_checks()) {
6056     uint64_t aot_fp = AOTLoader::get_saved_fingerprint(ik);
6057     uint64_t fp = ik->has_stored_fingerprint() ? ik->get_stored_fingerprint() : _stream->compute_fingerprint();
6058     if (aot_fp != 0 && aot_fp == fp) {
6059       // This class matches with a class saved in an AOT library
6060       ik->set_has_passed_fingerprint_check(true);
6061     } else {
6062       ResourceMark rm;
6063       log_info(class, fingerprint)("%s :  expected = " PTR64_FORMAT " actual = " PTR64_FORMAT,
6064                                  ik->external_name(), aot_fp, _stream->compute_fingerprint());
6065     }
6066   }
6067 
6068   if (ik->is_value()) {
6069     ValueKlass* vk = ValueKlass::cast(ik);
6070     oop val = ik->allocate_instance(CHECK_NULL);
6071     vk->set_default_value(val);
6072   }
6073 
6074   return ik;
6075 }
6076 
6077 // Return true if the specified class is not a valid super class for an inline type.
6078 // A valid super class for an inline type is abstract, has no instance fields,
6079 // does not implement interface java.lang.IdentityObject (checked elsewhere), has
6080 // an empty body-less no-arg constructor, and no synchronized instance methods.
6081 // This function doesn't check if the class's super types are invalid.  Those checks
6082 // are done elsewhere.  The final determination of whether or not a class is an
6083 // invalid super type for an inline class is done in fill_instance_klass().
6084 static bool is_invalid_super_for_inline_type(const InstanceKlass* ik) {
6085   if (ik->name() == vmSymbols::java_lang_IdentityObject()) {
6086     return true;
6087   }
6088   if (ik->is_interface() || ik->name() == vmSymbols::java_lang_Object()) {
6089     return false;
6090   }
6091   if (!ik->is_abstract() || ik->has_nonstatic_fields()) {
6092     return true;
6093   } else {
6094     Array<Method*>* methods = ik->methods();
6095     // Look at each method.
6096     for (int x = 0; x < methods->length(); x++) {
6097       const Method* const method = methods->at(x);
6098       if (method->is_synchronized() && !method->is_static()) {
6099         return true;
6100 
6101       } else if (method->name() == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name()) {
6102         if (method->signature() != vmSymbols::void_method_signature() ||
6103             !method->is_vanilla_constructor()) {
6104           return true;
6105         }
6106       }
6107     }
6108   }
6109   return false;
6110 }
6111 
6112 void ClassFileParser::fill_instance_klass(InstanceKlass* ik, bool changed_by_loadhook, TRAPS) {
6113   assert(ik != NULL, "invariant");
6114 
6115   // Set name and CLD before adding to CLD
6116   ik->set_class_loader_data(_loader_data);
6117   ik->set_name(_class_name);
6118 
6119   // Add all classes to our internal class loader list here,
6120   // including classes in the bootstrap (NULL) class loader.
6121   const bool publicize = !is_internal();
6122 
6123   _loader_data->add_class(ik, publicize);
6124 
6125   set_klass_to_deallocate(ik);
6126 
6127   assert(_field_info != NULL, "invariant");
6128   assert(ik->static_field_size() == _field_info->_static_field_size, "sanity");
6129   assert(ik->nonstatic_oop_map_count() == _field_info->oop_map_blocks->_nonstatic_oop_map_count,
6130          "sanity");
6131 
6132   assert(ik->is_instance_klass(), "sanity");
6133   assert(ik->size_helper() == _field_info->_instance_size, "sanity");
6134 
6135   // Fill in information already parsed
6136   ik->set_should_verify_class(_need_verify);
6137 
6138   // Not yet: supers are done below to support the new subtype-checking fields
6139   ik->set_nonstatic_field_size(_field_info->_nonstatic_field_size);
6140   ik->set_has_nonstatic_fields(_field_info->_has_nonstatic_fields);
6141   if (_field_info->_is_naturally_atomic && ik->is_value()) {
6142     ik->set_is_naturally_atomic();
6143   }
6144   if (_is_empty_value) {
6145     ik->set_is_empty_value();
6146   }
6147   assert(_fac != NULL, "invariant");
6148   ik->set_static_oop_field_count(_fac->count[STATIC_OOP] + _fac->count[STATIC_FLATTENABLE]);
6149 
6150   // this transfers ownership of a lot of arrays from
6151   // the parser onto the InstanceKlass*
6152   apply_parsed_class_metadata(ik, _java_fields_count, CHECK);
6153 
6154   // note that is not safe to use the fields in the parser from this point on
6155   assert(NULL == _cp, "invariant");
6156   assert(NULL == _fields, "invariant");
6157   assert(NULL == _methods, "invariant");
6158   assert(NULL == _inner_classes, "invariant");
6159   assert(NULL == _nest_members, "invariant");
6160   assert(NULL == _local_interfaces, "invariant");
6161   assert(NULL == _combined_annotations, "invariant");
6162   assert(NULL == _record_components, "invariant");
6163 
6164   if (_has_final_method) {
6165     ik->set_has_final_method();
6166   }
6167 
6168   ik->copy_method_ordering(_method_ordering, CHECK);
6169   // The InstanceKlass::_methods_jmethod_ids cache
6170   // is managed on the assumption that the initial cache
6171   // size is equal to the number of methods in the class. If
6172   // that changes, then InstanceKlass::idnum_can_increment()
6173   // has to be changed accordingly.
6174   ik->set_initial_method_idnum(ik->methods()->length());
6175 
6176   ik->set_this_class_index(_this_class_index);
6177 
6178   if (is_unsafe_anonymous()) {
6179     // _this_class_index is a CONSTANT_Class entry that refers to this
6180     // anonymous class itself. If this class needs to refer to its own methods or
6181     // fields, it would use a CONSTANT_MethodRef, etc, which would reference
6182     // _this_class_index. However, because this class is anonymous (it's
6183     // not stored in SystemDictionary), _this_class_index cannot be resolved
6184     // with ConstantPool::klass_at_impl, which does a SystemDictionary lookup.
6185     // Therefore, we must eagerly resolve _this_class_index now.
6186     ik->constants()->klass_at_put(_this_class_index, ik);
6187   }
6188 
6189   ik->set_minor_version(_minor_version);
6190   ik->set_major_version(_major_version);
6191   ik->set_has_nonstatic_concrete_methods(_has_nonstatic_concrete_methods);
6192   ik->set_declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods(_declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods);
6193   if (_is_declared_atomic) {
6194     ik->set_is_declared_atomic();
6195   }
6196 
6197   if (_unsafe_anonymous_host != NULL) {
6198     assert (ik->is_unsafe_anonymous(), "should be the same");
6199     ik->set_unsafe_anonymous_host(_unsafe_anonymous_host);
6200   }
6201 
6202   // Set PackageEntry for this_klass
6203   oop cl = ik->class_loader();
6204   Handle clh = Handle(THREAD, java_lang_ClassLoader::non_reflection_class_loader(cl));
6205   ClassLoaderData* cld = ClassLoaderData::class_loader_data_or_null(clh());
6206   ik->set_package(cld, NULL, CHECK);
6207 
6208   const Array<Method*>* const methods = ik->methods();
6209   assert(methods != NULL, "invariant");
6210   const int methods_len = methods->length();
6211 
6212   check_methods_for_intrinsics(ik, methods);
6213 
6214   // Fill in field values obtained by parse_classfile_attributes
6215   if (_parsed_annotations->has_any_annotations()) {
6216     _parsed_annotations->apply_to(ik);
6217   }
6218 
6219   apply_parsed_class_attributes(ik);
6220 
6221   // Miranda methods
6222   if ((_num_miranda_methods > 0) ||
6223       // if this class introduced new miranda methods or
6224       (_super_klass != NULL && _super_klass->has_miranda_methods())
6225         // super class exists and this class inherited miranda methods
6226      ) {
6227        ik->set_has_miranda_methods(); // then set a flag
6228   }
6229 
6230   // Fill in information needed to compute superclasses.
6231   ik->initialize_supers(const_cast<InstanceKlass*>(_super_klass), _transitive_interfaces, CHECK);
6232   ik->set_transitive_interfaces(_transitive_interfaces);
6233   _transitive_interfaces = NULL;
6234 
6235   // Initialize itable offset tables
6236   klassItable::setup_itable_offset_table(ik);
6237 
6238   // Compute transitive closure of interfaces this class implements
6239   // Do final class setup
6240   OopMapBlocksBuilder* oop_map_blocks = _field_info->oop_map_blocks;
6241   if (oop_map_blocks->_nonstatic_oop_map_count > 0) {
6242     oop_map_blocks->copy(ik->start_of_nonstatic_oop_maps());
6243   }
6244 
6245   if (_has_contended_fields || _parsed_annotations->is_contended() ||
6246       ( _super_klass != NULL && _super_klass->has_contended_annotations())) {
6247     ik->set_has_contended_annotations(true);
6248   }
6249 
6250   // Fill in has_finalizer, has_vanilla_constructor, and layout_helper
6251   set_precomputed_flags(ik);
6252 
6253   // check if this class can access its super class
6254   check_super_class_access(ik, CHECK);
6255 
6256   // check if this class can access its superinterfaces
6257   check_super_interface_access(ik, CHECK);
6258 
6259   // check if this class overrides any final method
6260   check_final_method_override(ik, CHECK);
6261 
6262   // reject static interface methods prior to Java 8
6263   if (ik->is_interface() && _major_version < JAVA_8_VERSION) {
6264     check_illegal_static_method(ik, CHECK);
6265   }
6266 
6267   // Obtain this_klass' module entry
6268   ModuleEntry* module_entry = ik->module();
6269   assert(module_entry != NULL, "module_entry should always be set");
6270 
6271   // Obtain java.lang.Module
6272   Handle module_handle(THREAD, module_entry->module());
6273 
6274   // Allocate mirror and initialize static fields
6275   // The create_mirror() call will also call compute_modifiers()
6276   java_lang_Class::create_mirror(ik,
6277                                  Handle(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader()),
6278                                  module_handle,
6279                                  _protection_domain,
6280                                  CHECK);
6281 
6282   assert(_all_mirandas != NULL, "invariant");
6283 
6284   // Generate any default methods - default methods are public interface methods
6285   // that have a default implementation.  This is new with Java 8.
6286   if (_has_nonstatic_concrete_methods) {
6287     DefaultMethods::generate_default_methods(ik,
6288                                              _all_mirandas,
6289                                              CHECK);
6290   }
6291 
6292   // Add read edges to the unnamed modules of the bootstrap and app class loaders.
6293   if (changed_by_loadhook && !module_handle.is_null() && module_entry->is_named() &&
6294       !module_entry->has_default_read_edges()) {
6295     if (!module_entry->set_has_default_read_edges()) {
6296       // We won a potential race
6297       JvmtiExport::add_default_read_edges(module_handle, THREAD);
6298     }
6299   }
6300 
6301   int nfields = ik->java_fields_count();
6302   if (ik->is_value()) nfields++;
6303   for (int i = 0; i < nfields; i++) {
6304     if (ik->field_is_flattenable(i)) {
6305       Symbol* klass_name = ik->field_signature(i)->fundamental_name(CHECK);
6306       // Inline classes for instance fields must have been pre-loaded
6307       // Inline classes for static fields might not have been loaded yet
6308       Klass* klass = SystemDictionary::find(klass_name,
6309           Handle(THREAD, ik->class_loader()),
6310           Handle(THREAD, ik->protection_domain()), CHECK);
6311       if (klass != NULL) {
6312         assert(klass->access_flags().is_value_type(), "Value type expected");
6313         ik->set_value_field_klass(i, klass);
6314       }
6315       klass_name->decrement_refcount();
6316     } else
6317       if (is_value_type() && ((ik->field_access_flags(i) & JVM_ACC_FIELD_INTERNAL) != 0)
6318         && ((ik->field_access_flags(i) & JVM_ACC_STATIC) != 0)) {
6319       ValueKlass::cast(ik)->set_default_value_offset(ik->field_offset(i));
6320     }
6321   }
6322 
6323   if (is_value_type()) {
6324     ValueKlass* vk = ValueKlass::cast(ik);
6325     if (UseNewFieldLayout) {
6326       vk->set_alignment(_alignment);
6327       vk->set_first_field_offset(_first_field_offset);
6328       vk->set_exact_size_in_bytes(_exact_size_in_bytes);
6329     } else {
6330       vk->set_first_field_offset(vk->first_field_offset_old());
6331     }
6332     ValueKlass::cast(ik)->initialize_calling_convention(CHECK);
6333   }
6334 
6335   ClassLoadingService::notify_class_loaded(ik, false /* not shared class */);
6336 
6337   if (!is_internal()) {
6338     if (log_is_enabled(Info, class, load)) {
6339       ResourceMark rm;
6340       const char* module_name = (module_entry->name() == NULL) ? UNNAMED_MODULE : module_entry->name()->as_C_string();
6341       ik->print_class_load_logging(_loader_data, module_name, _stream);
6342     }
6343 
6344     if (ik->minor_version() == JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION &&
6345         ik->major_version() == JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION &&
6346         log_is_enabled(Info, class, preview)) {
6347       ResourceMark rm;
6348       log_info(class, preview)("Loading class %s that depends on preview features (class file version %d.65535)",
6349                                ik->external_name(), JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION);
6350     }
6351 
6352     if (log_is_enabled(Debug, class, resolve))  {
6353       ResourceMark rm;
6354       // print out the superclass.
6355       const char * from = ik->external_name();
6356       if (ik->java_super() != NULL) {
6357         log_debug(class, resolve)("%s %s (super)",
6358                    from,
6359                    ik->java_super()->external_name());
6360       }
6361       // print out each of the interface classes referred to by this class.
6362       const Array<InstanceKlass*>* const local_interfaces = ik->local_interfaces();
6363       if (local_interfaces != NULL) {
6364         const int length = local_interfaces->length();
6365         for (int i = 0; i < length; i++) {
6366           const InstanceKlass* const k = local_interfaces->at(i);
6367           const char * to = k->external_name();
6368           log_debug(class, resolve)("%s %s (interface)", from, to);
6369         }
6370       }
6371     }
6372   }
6373 
6374   // Set ik->invalid_inline_super field to TRUE if already marked as invalid,
6375   // if super is marked invalid, or if is_invalid_super_for_inline_type()
6376   // returns true
6377   if (invalid_inline_super() ||
6378       (_super_klass != NULL && _super_klass->invalid_inline_super()) ||
6379       is_invalid_super_for_inline_type(ik)) {
6380     ik->set_invalid_inline_super();
6381   }
6382 
6383   JFR_ONLY(INIT_ID(ik);)
6384 
6385   // If we reach here, all is well.
6386   // Now remove the InstanceKlass* from the _klass_to_deallocate field
6387   // in order for it to not be destroyed in the ClassFileParser destructor.
6388   set_klass_to_deallocate(NULL);
6389 
6390   // it's official
6391   set_klass(ik);
6392 
6393   debug_only(ik->verify();)
6394 }
6395 
6396 void ClassFileParser::update_class_name(Symbol* new_class_name) {
6397   // Decrement the refcount in the old name, since we're clobbering it.
6398   _class_name->decrement_refcount();
6399 
6400   _class_name = new_class_name;
6401   // Increment the refcount of the new name.
6402   // Now the ClassFileParser owns this name and will decrement in
6403   // the destructor.
6404   _class_name->increment_refcount();
6405 }
6406 
6407 
6408 // For an unsafe anonymous class that is in the unnamed package, move it to its host class's
6409 // package by prepending its host class's package name to its class name and setting
6410 // its _class_name field.
6411 void ClassFileParser::prepend_host_package_name(const InstanceKlass* unsafe_anonymous_host, TRAPS) {
6412   ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6413   assert(strrchr(_class_name->as_C_string(), JVM_SIGNATURE_SLASH) == NULL,
6414          "Unsafe anonymous class should not be in a package");
6415   TempNewSymbol host_pkg_name =
6416     ClassLoader::package_from_class_name(unsafe_anonymous_host->name());
6417 
6418   if (host_pkg_name != NULL) {
6419     int host_pkg_len = host_pkg_name->utf8_length();
6420     int class_name_len = _class_name->utf8_length();
6421     int symbol_len = host_pkg_len + 1 + class_name_len;
6422     char* new_anon_name = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY(char, symbol_len + 1);
6423     int n = os::snprintf(new_anon_name, symbol_len + 1, "%.*s/%.*s",
6424                          host_pkg_len, host_pkg_name->base(), class_name_len, _class_name->base());
6425     assert(n == symbol_len, "Unexpected number of characters in string");
6426 
6427     // Decrement old _class_name to avoid leaking.
6428     _class_name->decrement_refcount();
6429 
6430     // Create a symbol and update the anonymous class name.
6431     // The new class name is created with a refcount of one. When installed into the InstanceKlass,
6432     // it'll be two and when the ClassFileParser destructor runs, it'll go back to one and get deleted
6433     // when the class is unloaded.
6434     _class_name = SymbolTable::new_symbol(new_anon_name, symbol_len);
6435   }
6436 }
6437 
6438 // If the host class and the anonymous class are in the same package then do
6439 // nothing.  If the anonymous class is in the unnamed package then move it to its
6440 // host's package.  If the classes are in different packages then throw an IAE
6441 // exception.
6442 void ClassFileParser::fix_unsafe_anonymous_class_name(TRAPS) {
6443   assert(_unsafe_anonymous_host != NULL, "Expected an unsafe anonymous class");
6444 
6445   const jbyte* anon_last_slash = UTF8::strrchr((const jbyte*)_class_name->base(),
6446                                                _class_name->utf8_length(), JVM_SIGNATURE_SLASH);
6447   if (anon_last_slash == NULL) {  // Unnamed package
6448     prepend_host_package_name(_unsafe_anonymous_host, CHECK);
6449   } else {
6450     if (!_unsafe_anonymous_host->is_same_class_package(_unsafe_anonymous_host->class_loader(), _class_name)) {
6451       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6452       THROW_MSG(vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalArgumentException(),
6453         err_msg("Host class %s and anonymous class %s are in different packages",
6454         _unsafe_anonymous_host->name()->as_C_string(), _class_name->as_C_string()));
6455     }
6456   }
6457 }
6458 
6459 static bool relax_format_check_for(ClassLoaderData* loader_data) {
6460   bool trusted = (loader_data->is_the_null_class_loader_data() ||
6461                   SystemDictionary::is_platform_class_loader(loader_data->class_loader()));
6462   bool need_verify =
6463     // verifyAll
6464     (BytecodeVerificationLocal && BytecodeVerificationRemote) ||
6465     // verifyRemote
6466     (!BytecodeVerificationLocal && BytecodeVerificationRemote && !trusted);
6467   return !need_verify;
6468 }
