6470 ClassFileParser::ClassFileParser(ClassFileStream* stream,
6471                                  Symbol* name,
6472                                  ClassLoaderData* loader_data,
6473                                  Handle protection_domain,
6474                                  const InstanceKlass* unsafe_anonymous_host,
6475                                  GrowableArray<Handle>* cp_patches,
6476                                  Publicity pub_level,
6477                                  TRAPS) :
6478   _stream(stream),
6479   _requested_name(name),
6480   _class_name(NULL),
6481   _loader_data(loader_data),
6482   _unsafe_anonymous_host(unsafe_anonymous_host),
6483   _cp_patches(cp_patches),
6484   _num_patched_klasses(0),
6485   _max_num_patched_klasses(0),
6486   _orig_cp_size(0),
6487   _first_patched_klass_resolved_index(0),
6488   _super_klass(),
6489   _cp(NULL),
6490   _fields(NULL),
6491   _methods(NULL),
6492   _inner_classes(NULL),
6493   _nest_members(NULL),
6494   _nest_host(0),
6495   _record_components(NULL),
6496   _local_interfaces(NULL),
6497   _transitive_interfaces(NULL),
6498   _combined_annotations(NULL),
6499   _class_annotations(NULL),
6500   _class_type_annotations(NULL),
6501   _fields_annotations(NULL),
6502   _fields_type_annotations(NULL),
6503   _klass(NULL),
6504   _klass_to_deallocate(NULL),
6505   _parsed_annotations(NULL),
6506   _fac(NULL),
6507   _field_info(NULL),
6508   _method_ordering(NULL),
6509   _all_mirandas(NULL),
6510   _vtable_size(0),
6511   _itable_size(0),
6512   _num_miranda_methods(0),
6513   _rt(REF_NONE),
6514   _protection_domain(protection_domain),
6515   _access_flags(),
6516   _pub_level(pub_level),
6517   _bad_constant_seen(0),
6518   _synthetic_flag(false),
6519   _sde_length(false),
6520   _sde_buffer(NULL),
6521   _sourcefile_index(0),
6522   _generic_signature_index(0),
6523   _major_version(0),
6524   _minor_version(0),
6525   _this_class_index(0),
6526   _super_class_index(0),
6527   _itfs_len(0),
6528   _java_fields_count(0),
6529   _need_verify(false),
6530   _relax_verify(false),
6531   _has_nonstatic_concrete_methods(false),
6532   _declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods(false),
6533   _has_final_method(false),
6534   _has_contended_fields(false),
6535   _has_flattenable_fields(false),
6536   _is_empty_value(false),
6537   _is_naturally_atomic(false),
6538   _is_declared_atomic(false),
6539   _invalid_inline_super(false),
6540   _invalid_identity_super(false),
6541   _has_finalizer(false),
6542   _has_empty_finalizer(false),
6543   _has_vanilla_constructor(false),
6544   _max_bootstrap_specifier_index(-1) {
6545 
6546   _class_name = name != NULL ? name : vmSymbols::unknown_class_name();
6547   _class_name->increment_refcount();
6548 
6549   assert(THREAD->is_Java_thread(), "invariant");
6550   assert(_loader_data != NULL, "invariant");
6551   assert(stream != NULL, "invariant");
6552   assert(_stream != NULL, "invariant");
6553   assert(_stream->buffer() == _stream->current(), "invariant");
6554   assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
6555   assert(0 == _access_flags.as_int(), "invariant");
6556 
6557   // Figure out whether we can skip format checking (matching classic VM behavior)
6558   if (DumpSharedSpaces) {
6559     // verify == true means it's a 'remote' class (i.e., non-boot class)
6560     // Verification decision is based on BytecodeVerificationRemote flag
6561     // for those classes.
6562     _need_verify = (stream->need_verify()) ? BytecodeVerificationRemote :
6563                                               BytecodeVerificationLocal;
6564   }
6565   else {
6566     _need_verify = Verifier::should_verify_for(_loader_data->class_loader(),
6567                                                stream->need_verify());
6568   }
6569   if (_cp_patches != NULL) {
6570     int len = _cp_patches->length();
6571     for (int i=0; i<len; i++) {
6572       if (has_cp_patch_at(i)) {
6573         Handle patch = cp_patch_at(i);
6574         if (java_lang_String::is_instance(patch()) || java_lang_Class::is_instance(patch())) {
6575           // We need to append the names of the patched classes to the end of the constant pool,
6576           // because a patched class may have a Utf8 name that's not already included in the
6577           // original constant pool. These class names are used when patch_constant_pool()
6578           // calls patch_class().
6579           //
6580           // Note that a String in cp_patch_at(i) may be used to patch a Utf8, a String, or a Class.
6581           // At this point, we don't know the tag for index i yet, because we haven't parsed the
6582           // constant pool. So we can only assume the worst -- every String is used to patch a Class.
6583           _max_num_patched_klasses++;
6584         }
6585       }
6586     }
6587   }
6588 
6589   // synch back verification state to stream
6590   stream->set_verify(_need_verify);
6591 
6592   // Check if verification needs to be relaxed for this class file
6593   // Do not restrict it to jdk1.0 or jdk1.1 to maintain backward compatibility (4982376)
6594   _relax_verify = relax_format_check_for(_loader_data);
6595 
6596   parse_stream(stream, CHECK);
6597 
6598   post_process_parsed_stream(stream, _cp, CHECK);
6599 }
6600 
6601 void ClassFileParser::clear_class_metadata() {
6602   // metadata created before the instance klass is created.  Must be
6603   // deallocated if classfile parsing returns an error.
6604   _cp = NULL;
6605   _fields = NULL;
6606   _methods = NULL;
6607   _inner_classes = NULL;
6608   _nest_members = NULL;
6609   _local_interfaces = NULL;
6610   _combined_annotations = NULL;
6611   _class_annotations = _class_type_annotations = NULL;
6612   _fields_annotations = _fields_type_annotations = NULL;
6613   _record_components = NULL;
6614 }
6615 
6616 // Destructor to clean up
6617 ClassFileParser::~ClassFileParser() {
6618   _class_name->decrement_refcount();
6619 
6620   if (_cp != NULL) {
6621     MetadataFactory::free_metadata(_loader_data, _cp);
6622   }
6623   if (_fields != NULL) {
6624     MetadataFactory::free_array<u2>(_loader_data, _fields);
6625   }
6626 
6627   if (_methods != NULL) {
6628     // Free methods
6629     InstanceKlass::deallocate_methods(_loader_data, _methods);
6630   }
6631 
6632   // beware of the Universe::empty_blah_array!!
6633   if (_inner_classes != NULL && _inner_classes != Universe::the_empty_short_array()) {
6634     MetadataFactory::free_array<u2>(_loader_data, _inner_classes);
6635   }
6636 
6637   if (_nest_members != NULL && _nest_members != Universe::the_empty_short_array()) {
6638     MetadataFactory::free_array<u2>(_loader_data, _nest_members);
6639   }
6640 
6641   if (_record_components != NULL) {
6642     InstanceKlass::deallocate_record_components(_loader_data, _record_components);
6643   }
6644 
6645   // Free interfaces
6646   InstanceKlass::deallocate_interfaces(_loader_data, _super_klass,
6647                                        _local_interfaces, _transitive_interfaces);
6648 
6649   if (_combined_annotations != NULL) {
6650     // After all annotations arrays have been created, they are installed into the
6651     // Annotations object that will be assigned to the InstanceKlass being created.
6652 
6653     // Deallocate the Annotations object and the installed annotations arrays.
6654     _combined_annotations->deallocate_contents(_loader_data);
6655 
6656     // If the _combined_annotations pointer is non-NULL,
6657     // then the other annotations fields should have been cleared.
6658     assert(_class_annotations       == NULL, "Should have been cleared");
6659     assert(_class_type_annotations  == NULL, "Should have been cleared");
6660     assert(_fields_annotations      == NULL, "Should have been cleared");
6661     assert(_fields_type_annotations == NULL, "Should have been cleared");
6662   } else {
6663     // If the annotations arrays were not installed into the Annotations object,
6664     // then they have to be deallocated explicitly.
6665     MetadataFactory::free_array<u1>(_loader_data, _class_annotations);
6666     MetadataFactory::free_array<u1>(_loader_data, _class_type_annotations);
6667     Annotations::free_contents(_loader_data, _fields_annotations);
6668     Annotations::free_contents(_loader_data, _fields_type_annotations);
6669   }
6670 
6671   clear_class_metadata();
6672   _transitive_interfaces = NULL;
6673 
6674   // deallocate the klass if already created.  Don't directly deallocate, but add
6675   // to the deallocate list so that the klass is removed from the CLD::_klasses list
6676   // at a safepoint.
6677   if (_klass_to_deallocate != NULL) {
6678     _loader_data->add_to_deallocate_list(_klass_to_deallocate);
6679   }
6680 }
6681 
6682 void ClassFileParser::parse_stream(const ClassFileStream* const stream,
6683                                    TRAPS) {
6684 
6685   assert(stream != NULL, "invariant");
6686   assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
6687 
6688   // BEGIN STREAM PARSING
6689   stream->guarantee_more(8, CHECK);  // magic, major, minor
6690   // Magic value
6691   const u4 magic = stream->get_u4_fast();
6692   guarantee_property(magic == JAVA_CLASSFILE_MAGIC,
6693                      "Incompatible magic value %u in class file %s",
6694                      magic, CHECK);
6695 
6696   // Version numbers
6697   _minor_version = stream->get_u2_fast();
6698   _major_version = stream->get_u2_fast();
6699 
6700   if (DumpSharedSpaces && _major_version < JAVA_6_VERSION) {
6701     ResourceMark rm;
6702     warning("Pre JDK 6 class not supported by CDS: %u.%u %s",
6703             _major_version,  _minor_version, _class_name->as_C_string());
6704     Exceptions::fthrow(
6705       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
6706       vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
6707       "Unsupported major.minor version for dump time %u.%u",
6708       _major_version,
6709       _minor_version);
6710   }
6711 
6712   // Check version numbers - we check this even with verifier off
6713   verify_class_version(_major_version, _minor_version, _class_name, CHECK);
6714 
6715   stream->guarantee_more(3, CHECK); // length, first cp tag
6716   u2 cp_size = stream->get_u2_fast();
6717 
6718   guarantee_property(
6719     cp_size >= 1, "Illegal constant pool size %u in class file %s",
6720     cp_size, CHECK);
6721 
6722   _orig_cp_size = cp_size;
6723   if (int(cp_size) + _max_num_patched_klasses > 0xffff) {
6724     THROW_MSG(vmSymbols::java_lang_InternalError(), "not enough space for patched classes");
6725   }
6726   cp_size += _max_num_patched_klasses;
6727 
6728   _cp = ConstantPool::allocate(_loader_data,
6729                                cp_size,
6730                                CHECK);
6731 
6732   ConstantPool* const cp = _cp;
6733 
6734   parse_constant_pool(stream, cp, _orig_cp_size, CHECK);
6735 
6736   assert(cp_size == (const u2)cp->length(), "invariant");
6737 
6738   // ACCESS FLAGS
6739   stream->guarantee_more(8, CHECK);  // flags, this_class, super_class, infs_len
6740 
6741   jint recognized_modifiers = JVM_RECOGNIZED_CLASS_MODIFIERS;
6742   // JVM_ACC_MODULE is defined in JDK-9 and later.
6743   if (_major_version >= JAVA_9_VERSION) {
6744     recognized_modifiers |= JVM_ACC_MODULE;
6745   }
6746   // JVM_ACC_VALUE is defined for class file version 55 and later
6747   if (supports_value_types()) {
6748     recognized_modifiers |= JVM_ACC_VALUE;
6749   }
6750 
6751   // Access flags
6752   jint flags = stream->get_u2_fast() & recognized_modifiers;
6753 
6754   if ((flags & JVM_ACC_INTERFACE) && _major_version < JAVA_6_VERSION) {
6755     // Set abstract bit for old class files for backward compatibility
6756     flags |= JVM_ACC_ABSTRACT;
6757   }
6758 
6759   verify_legal_class_modifiers(flags, CHECK);
6760 
6761   short bad_constant = class_bad_constant_seen();
6762   if (bad_constant != 0) {
6763     // Do not throw CFE until after the access_flags are checked because if
6764     // ACC_MODULE is set in the access flags, then NCDFE must be thrown, not CFE.
6765     classfile_parse_error("Unknown constant tag %u in class file %s", bad_constant, CHECK);
6766   }
6767 
6768   _access_flags.set_flags(flags);
6769 
6770   // This class and superclass
6771   _this_class_index = stream->get_u2_fast();
6772   check_property(
6773     valid_cp_range(_this_class_index, cp_size) &&
6774       cp->tag_at(_this_class_index).is_unresolved_klass(),
6775     "Invalid this class index %u in constant pool in class file %s",
6776     _this_class_index, CHECK);
6777 
6778   Symbol* const class_name_in_cp = cp->klass_name_at(_this_class_index);
6779   assert(class_name_in_cp != NULL, "class_name can't be null");
6780 
6781   // Update _class_name to reflect the name in the constant pool
6782   update_class_name(class_name_in_cp);
6783 
6784   // Don't need to check whether this class name is legal or not.
6785   // It has been checked when constant pool is parsed.
6786   // However, make sure it is not an array type.
6787   if (_need_verify) {
6788     guarantee_property(_class_name->char_at(0) != JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY,
6789                        "Bad class name in class file %s",
6790                        CHECK);
6791   }
6792 
6793   // Checks if name in class file matches requested name
6794   if (_requested_name != NULL && _requested_name != _class_name) {
6795     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6796     Exceptions::fthrow(
6797       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
6798       vmSymbols::java_lang_NoClassDefFoundError(),
6799       "%s (wrong name: %s)",
6800       _class_name->as_C_string(),
6801       _requested_name != NULL ? _requested_name->as_C_string() : "NoName"
6802     );
6803     return;
6804   }
6805 
6806   // if this is an anonymous class fix up its name if it's in the unnamed
6807   // package.  Otherwise, throw IAE if it is in a different package than
6808   // its host class.
6809   if (_unsafe_anonymous_host != NULL) {
6810     fix_unsafe_anonymous_class_name(CHECK);
6811   }
6812 
6813   // Verification prevents us from creating names with dots in them, this
6814   // asserts that that's the case.
6815   assert(is_internal_format(_class_name), "external class name format used internally");
6816 
6817   if (!is_internal()) {
6818     LogTarget(Debug, class, preorder) lt;
6819     if (lt.is_enabled()){
6820       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6821       LogStream ls(lt);
6822       ls.print("%s", _class_name->as_klass_external_name());
6823       if (stream->source() != NULL) {
6824         ls.print(" source: %s", stream->source());
6825       }
6826       ls.cr();
6827     }
6828 
6829 #if INCLUDE_CDS
6830     if (DumpLoadedClassList != NULL && stream->source() != NULL && classlist_file->is_open()) {
6831       if (!ClassLoader::has_jrt_entry()) {
6832         warning("DumpLoadedClassList and CDS are not supported in exploded build");
6833         DumpLoadedClassList = NULL;
6834       } else if (SystemDictionaryShared::is_sharing_possible(_loader_data) &&
6835                  _unsafe_anonymous_host == NULL) {
6836         // Only dump the classes that can be stored into CDS archive.
6837         // Unsafe anonymous classes such as generated LambdaForm classes are also not included.
6838         oop class_loader = _loader_data->class_loader();
6839         ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6840         bool skip = false;
6841         if (class_loader == NULL || SystemDictionary::is_platform_class_loader(class_loader)) {
6842           // For the boot and platform class loaders, skip classes that are not found in the
6843           // java runtime image, such as those found in the --patch-module entries.
6844           // These classes can't be loaded from the archive during runtime.
6845           if (!stream->from_boot_loader_modules_image() && strncmp(stream->source(), "jrt:", 4) != 0) {
6846             skip = true;
6847           }
6848 
6849           if (class_loader == NULL && ClassLoader::contains_append_entry(stream->source())) {
6850             // .. but don't skip the boot classes that are loaded from -Xbootclasspath/a
6851             // as they can be loaded from the archive during runtime.
6852             skip = false;
6853           }
6854         }
6855         if (skip) {
6856           tty->print_cr("skip writing class %s from source %s to classlist file",
6857             _class_name->as_C_string(), stream->source());
6858         } else {
6859           classlist_file->print_cr("%s", _class_name->as_C_string());
6860           classlist_file->flush();
6861         }
6862       }
6863     }
6864 #endif
6865   }
6866 
6867   // SUPERKLASS
6868   _super_class_index = stream->get_u2_fast();
6869   _super_klass = parse_super_class(cp,
6870                                    _super_class_index,
6871                                    _need_verify,
6872                                    CHECK);
6873 
6874   // Interfaces
6875   _itfs_len = stream->get_u2_fast();
6876   parse_interfaces(stream,
6877                    _itfs_len,
6878                    cp,
6879                    is_value_type(),
6880                    &_has_nonstatic_concrete_methods,
6881                    &_is_declared_atomic,
6882                    CHECK);
6883 
6884   assert(_local_interfaces != NULL, "invariant");
6885 
6886   // Fields (offsets are filled in later)
6887   _fac = new FieldAllocationCount();
6888   parse_fields(stream,
6889                is_interface(),
6890                is_value_type(),
6891                _fac,
6892                cp,
6893                cp_size,
6894                &_java_fields_count,
6895                CHECK);
6896 
6897   assert(_fields != NULL, "invariant");
6898 
6899   // Methods
6900   AccessFlags promoted_flags;
6901   parse_methods(stream,
6902                 is_interface(),
6903                 is_value_type(),
6904                 &promoted_flags,
6905                 &_has_final_method,
6906                 &_declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods,
6907                 CHECK);
6908 
6909   assert(_methods != NULL, "invariant");
6910 
6911   // promote flags from parse_methods() to the klass' flags
6912   _access_flags.add_promoted_flags(promoted_flags.as_int());
6913 
6914   if (_declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods) {
6915     _has_nonstatic_concrete_methods = true;
6916   }
6917 
6918   // Additional attributes/annotations
6919   _parsed_annotations = new ClassAnnotationCollector();
6920   parse_classfile_attributes(stream, cp, _parsed_annotations, CHECK);
6921 
6922   assert(_inner_classes != NULL, "invariant");
6923 
6924   // Finalize the Annotations metadata object,
6925   // now that all annotation arrays have been created.
6926   create_combined_annotations(CHECK);
6927 
6928   // Make sure this is the end of class file stream
6929   guarantee_property(stream->at_eos(),
6930                      "Extra bytes at the end of class file %s",
6931                      CHECK);
6932 
6933   // all bytes in stream read and parsed
6934 }
6935 
6936 void ClassFileParser::post_process_parsed_stream(const ClassFileStream* const stream,
6937                                                  ConstantPool* cp,
6938                                                  TRAPS) {
6939   assert(stream != NULL, "invariant");
6940   assert(stream->at_eos(), "invariant");
6941   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
6942   assert(_loader_data != NULL, "invariant");
6943 
6944   if (_class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Object()) {
6945     check_property(_local_interfaces == Universe::the_empty_instance_klass_array(),
6946                    "java.lang.Object cannot implement an interface in class file %s",
6947                    CHECK);
6948   }
6949   // We check super class after class file is parsed and format is checked
6950   if (_super_class_index > 0 && NULL ==_super_klass) {
6951     Symbol* const super_class_name = cp->klass_name_at(_super_class_index);
6952     if (is_interface()) {
6953       // Before attempting to resolve the superclass, check for class format
6954       // errors not checked yet.
6955       guarantee_property(super_class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Object(),
6956         "Interfaces must have java.lang.Object as superclass in class file %s",
6957         CHECK);
6958     }
6959     Handle loader(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader());
6960     _super_klass = (const InstanceKlass*)
6961                        SystemDictionary::resolve_super_or_fail(_class_name,
6962                                                                super_class_name,
6963                                                                loader,
6964                                                                _protection_domain,
6965                                                                true,
6966                                                                CHECK);
6967   }
6968 
6969   if (_super_klass != NULL) {
6970     if (_super_klass->has_nonstatic_concrete_methods()) {
6971       _has_nonstatic_concrete_methods = true;
6972     }
6973     if (_super_klass->is_declared_atomic()) {
6974       _is_declared_atomic = true;
6975     }
6976 
6977     if (_super_klass->is_interface()) {
6978       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6979       Exceptions::fthrow(
6980         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
6981         vmSymbols::java_lang_IncompatibleClassChangeError(),
6982         "class %s has interface %s as super class",
6983         _class_name->as_klass_external_name(),
6984         _super_klass->external_name()
6985       );
6986       return;
6987     }
6988 
6989     // Make sure super class is not final
6990     if (_super_klass->is_final()) {
6991       THROW_MSG(vmSymbols::java_lang_VerifyError(), "Cannot inherit from final class");
6992     }
6993 
6994     // For an inline class, only java/lang/Object or special abstract classes
6995     // are acceptable super classes.
6996     if (is_value_type()) {
6997       const InstanceKlass* super_ik = _super_klass;
6998       if (super_ik->invalid_inline_super()) {
6999         ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
7000         Exceptions::fthrow(
7001           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
7002           vmSymbols::java_lang_IncompatibleClassChangeError(),
7003           "inline class %s has an invalid super class %s",
7004           _class_name->as_klass_external_name(),
7005           _super_klass->external_name());
7006         return;
7007       }
7008     }
7009   }
7010 
7011   if (_class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_NonTearable() && _loader_data->class_loader() == NULL) {
7012     // This is the original source of this condition.
7013     // It propagates by inheritance, as if testing "instanceof NonTearable".
7014     _is_declared_atomic = true;
7015   } else if (*ForceNonTearable != '\0') {
7016     // Allow a command line switch to force the same atomicity property:
7017     const char* class_name_str = _class_name->as_C_string();
7018     if (StringUtils::class_list_match(ForceNonTearable, class_name_str)) {
7019       _is_declared_atomic = true;
7020     }
7021   }
7022 
7023   // Compute the transitive list of all unique interfaces implemented by this class
7024   _transitive_interfaces =
7025     compute_transitive_interfaces(_super_klass,
7026                                   _local_interfaces,
7027                                   _loader_data,
7028                                   CHECK);
7029 
7030   assert(_transitive_interfaces != NULL, "invariant");
7031 
7032   // sort methods
7033   _method_ordering = sort_methods(_methods);
7034 
7035   _all_mirandas = new GrowableArray<Method*>(20);
7036 
7037   Handle loader(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader());
7038   klassVtable::compute_vtable_size_and_num_mirandas(&_vtable_size,
7039                                                     &_num_miranda_methods,
7040                                                     _all_mirandas,
7041                                                     _super_klass,
7042                                                     _methods,
7043                                                     _access_flags,
7044                                                     _major_version,
7045                                                     loader,
7046                                                     _class_name,
7047                                                     _local_interfaces,
7048                                                     CHECK);
7049 
7050   // Size of Java itable (in words)
7051   _itable_size = is_interface() ? 0 :
7052     klassItable::compute_itable_size(_transitive_interfaces);
7053 
7054   assert(_fac != NULL, "invariant");
7055   assert(_parsed_annotations != NULL, "invariant");
7056 
7057 
7058   for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
7059     if (fs.is_flattenable() && !fs.access_flags().is_static()) {
7060       // Pre-load value class
7061       Klass* klass = SystemDictionary::resolve_flattenable_field_or_fail(&fs,
7062           Handle(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader()),
7063           _protection_domain, true, CHECK);
7064       assert(klass != NULL, "Sanity check");
7065       assert(klass->access_flags().is_value_type(), "Value type expected");
7066       _has_flattenable_fields = true;
7067     }
7068   }
7069 
7070   _field_info = new FieldLayoutInfo();
7071   if (UseNewFieldLayout) {
7072     FieldLayoutBuilder lb(class_name(), super_klass(), _cp, _fields,
7073         _parsed_annotations->is_contended(), is_value_type(),
7074         loader_data(), _protection_domain, _field_info);
7075     lb.build_layout(CHECK);
7076     if (is_value_type()) {
7077       _alignment = lb.get_alignment();
7078       _first_field_offset = lb.get_first_field_offset();
7079       _exact_size_in_bytes = lb.get_exact_size_in_byte();
7080     }
7081   } else {
7082     layout_fields(cp, _fac, _parsed_annotations, _field_info, CHECK);
7083   }
7084 
7085   // Compute reference type
7086   _rt = (NULL ==_super_klass) ? REF_NONE : _super_klass->reference_type();
7087 }
7088 
7089 void ClassFileParser::set_klass(InstanceKlass* klass) {
7090 
7091 #ifdef ASSERT
7092   if (klass != NULL) {
7093     assert(NULL == _klass, "leaking?");
7094   }
7095 #endif
7096 
7097   _klass = klass;
7098 }
7099 
7100 void ClassFileParser::set_klass_to_deallocate(InstanceKlass* klass) {
7101 
7102 #ifdef ASSERT
7103   if (klass != NULL) {
7104     assert(NULL == _klass_to_deallocate, "leaking?");
7105   }
7106 #endif
7107 
7108   _klass_to_deallocate = klass;
7109 }
7110 
7111 // Caller responsible for ResourceMark
7112 // clone stream with rewound position
7113 const ClassFileStream* ClassFileParser::clone_stream() const {
7114   assert(_stream != NULL, "invariant");
7115 
7116   return _stream->clone();
7117 }
7118 
7119 // ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
7120 // debugging
7121 
7122 #ifdef ASSERT
7123 
7124 // return true if class_name contains no '.' (internal format is '/')
7125 bool ClassFileParser::is_internal_format(Symbol* class_name) {
7126   if (class_name != NULL) {
7127     ResourceMark rm;
7128     char* name = class_name->as_C_string();
7129     return strchr(name, JVM_SIGNATURE_DOT) == NULL;
7130   } else {
7131     return true;
7132   }
7133 }
7134 
7135 #endif
